module DASHI.Geometry.NoLeakageOrthogonality where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Inner-product data supplied as assumptions (no metas/stubs).
----------------------------------------------------------------

record InnerProductData : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    V : Set
    _+_ _-_ _*_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    0v : V
    two : V
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    ‚à•_‚à•¬≤ : V ‚Üí V
    add-norm¬≤ :
      ‚àÄ a b ‚Üí ‚à• a + b ‚à•¬≤ ‚â° (‚à• a ‚à•¬≤ + ‚à• b ‚à•¬≤) + (two * ‚ü™ a , b ‚ü´)
    cancel-add-left : ‚àÄ {a c} ‚Üí a ‚â° a + c ‚Üí c ‚â° 0v
    div2-zero : ‚àÄ {z} ‚Üí two * z ‚â° 0v ‚Üí z ‚â° 0v

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projections and ‚Äúno leakage ‚áí orthogonality‚Äù
----------------------------------------------------------------

record Projection (D : InnerProductData) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open InnerProductData D
  field
    P : V ‚Üí V
    idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x
    split : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P x + (x - P x) ‚â° x

coarse : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D
coarse Pr x = Projection.P Pr x

detail : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D
detail {D} Pr x =
  let open InnerProductData D in x - Projection.P Pr x

NoLeakage : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí Set
NoLeakage {D} Pr =
  ‚àÄ x ‚Üí ‚à• x ‚à•¬≤ ‚â° ‚à• coarse Pr x ‚à•¬≤ + ‚à• detail Pr x ‚à•¬≤
  where open InnerProductData D

Orthogonal : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí Set
Orthogonal {D} Pr =
  ‚àÄ x ‚Üí ‚ü™ coarse Pr x , detail Pr x ‚ü´ ‚â° 0v
  where open InnerProductData D

NoLeakage‚áíOrthogonal :
  ‚àÄ {D} (Pr : Projection D) ‚Üí
  NoLeakage Pr ‚Üí
  Orthogonal Pr
NoLeakage‚áíOrthogonal {D} Pr NL x =
  let open Projection Pr
      open InnerProductData D
      c = coarse Pr x
      d = detail Pr x
      eq1 = NL x
      eq2 = add-norm¬≤ c d
      eqSplit = sym (cong (Œª z ‚Üí ‚à• z ‚à•¬≤) (split x))
      eq2' = trans eqSplit eq2
      eq3 = trans (sym eq1) eq2'
  in
  div2-zero (cancel-add-left eq3)
module DASHI.Geometry.Polarization where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ñö; _+‚Ñö_; _-‚Ñö_; _*‚Ñö_; four‚Ñö)

record Polarization (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    V : Set ‚Ñì
    _+_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    _-_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    Q : V ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    polarization :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí four‚Ñö *‚Ñö ‚ü™ x , y ‚ü´ ‚â° Q (x + y) -‚Ñö Q (x - y)

open Polarization public

module DASHI.Geometry.ParallelogramToInnerProduct where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Geometry.Parallelogram
open import DASHI.Core.Q as Q using (‚Ñö; _+‚Ñö_; _-‚Ñö_; _*‚Ñö_; four‚Ñö)
open import Data.Integer using (+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

record InnerProduct (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    V : Set ‚Ñì
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ñö

-- Polarization formula (no further properties required here).
polarization :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} (N : NormedSpace ‚Ñì) ‚Üí
  NormedSpace.V N ‚Üí NormedSpace.V N ‚Üí ‚Ñö
polarization N x y =
  let open NormedSpace N in
  let inv4 : ‚Ñö
      inv4 = Q._/_ (+ 1) 4
      num : ‚Ñö
      num = ((‚Äñ (x + y) ‚Äñ *‚Ñö ‚Äñ (x + y) ‚Äñ) -‚Ñö (‚Äñ (x - y) ‚Äñ *‚Ñö ‚Äñ (x - y) ‚Äñ))
  in inv4 *‚Ñö num

Parallelogram‚áíInnerProduct :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} (N : NormedSpace ‚Ñì) ‚Üí
  Parallelogram N ‚Üí
  InnerProduct ‚Ñì
Parallelogram‚áíInnerProduct N _ =
  record
    { V = NormedSpace.V N
    ; ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ = polarization N
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.FixedPointExistence_Projection where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (trans; sym)

open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15; Kernel; projectTo)
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 using (UMask15)
open import Ultrametric

Fixed : (Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) ‚Üí Mask15 ‚Üí Set
Fixed K m = K m ‚â° m

iterate : (Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15
iterate K zero    m = m
iterate K (suc n) m = iterate K n (K m)

-- For projection K = Œª _ ‚Üí target:
-- (1) target is a fixed point
fixed-target : ‚àÄ target ‚Üí Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) target
fixed-target target = refl

-- (2) unique fixed point
unique-fixed :
  ‚àÄ target x y ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y ‚Üí
  x ‚â° y
unique-fixed target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy

-- (3) convergence in 1 step
converges-1 :
  ‚àÄ target m ‚Üí iterate (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) 1 m ‚â° target
converges-1 target m = refl
module DASHI.Geometry.EnergyAdditivityProof where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong; cong‚ÇÇ; sym; trans)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record Additive {‚Ñì} : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Carrier : Set ‚Ñì
    _+_     : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier

open Additive public

record ScalarField {‚Ñì} : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Scalar : Set ‚Ñì
    _+s_ _*s_ : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar ‚Üí Scalar
    0s 1s : Scalar
    -s_ : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar

open ScalarField public

record ScalarLaws {‚Ñì} (F : ScalarField {‚Ñì}) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  open ScalarField F
  field
    +s-assoc :
      ‚àÄ (a b c : ScalarField.Scalar F) ‚Üí
      ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField._+s_ F a b) c
        ‚â°
      ScalarField._+s_ F a (ScalarField._+s_ F b c)
    +s-comm  :
      ‚àÄ (a b : ScalarField.Scalar F) ‚Üí
      ScalarField._+s_ F a b ‚â° ScalarField._+s_ F b a
    +s-idL   :
      ‚àÄ (a : ScalarField.Scalar F) ‚Üí
      ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField.0s F) a ‚â° a

open ScalarLaws public

record InnerProductSpace {‚Ñì} (A : Additive {‚Ñì}) (F : ScalarField {‚Ñì}) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  field
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´   : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.Scalar F
    ip-sym  : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü™ x , y ‚ü´ ‚â° ‚ü™ y , x ‚ü´
    ip-addL : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí
      ‚ü™ Additive._+_ A x y , z ‚ü´ ‚â°
      ScalarField._+s_ F (‚ü™ x , z ‚ü´) (‚ü™ y , z ‚ü´)
    ip-addR : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí
      ‚ü™ x , Additive._+_ A y z ‚ü´ ‚â°
      ScalarField._+s_ F (‚ü™ x , y ‚ü´) (‚ü™ x , z ‚ü´)
    ip-negL : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      ‚ü™ Additive.-_ A x , y ‚ü´ ‚â° ScalarField.-s_ F (‚ü™ x , y ‚ü´)
    E       : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.Scalar F
    E-def   : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí E x ‚â° ‚ü™ x , x ‚ü´

open InnerProductSpace public

Orth : ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {A : Additive {‚Ñì}} {F : ScalarField {‚Ñì}}
       (V : InnerProductSpace A F) ‚Üí
       Carrier A ‚Üí Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì
Orth {A = A} {F = F} V x y = ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ V x y ‚â° 0s F

record Two {‚Ñì} (F : ScalarField {‚Ñì}) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  open ScalarField F
  field
    two : ScalarField.Scalar F
    two-def : two ‚â° ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField.1s F) (ScalarField.1s F)

open Two public

EnergyAdditivityProof :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì}
  {A : Additive {‚Ñì}} {F : ScalarField {‚Ñì}}
  (V : InnerProductSpace A F) (T : Two F) (L : ScalarLaws F) ‚Üí
  (‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Orth V x y ‚Üí ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ V x y ‚â° 0s F) ‚Üí
  ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Orth V x y ‚Üí E V ( _+_ A x y ) ‚â° ( _+s_ F (E V x) (E V y) )
EnergyAdditivityProof {A = A} {F = F} V T L killCross x y orth =
  let open Additive A
      open ScalarField F
      open InnerProductSpace V
      open ScalarLaws L
      infixl 6 _‚äï_
      _‚äï_ : ScalarField.Scalar F ‚Üí ScalarField.Scalar F ‚Üí ScalarField.Scalar F
      _‚äï_ = ScalarField._+s_ F
      ip : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.Scalar F
      ip = InnerProductSpace.‚ü™_,_‚ü´ V
      cross0 : ip x y ‚â° ScalarField.0s F
      cross0 = killCross x y orth
      cross0' : ip y x ‚â° ScalarField.0s F
      cross0' = trans (InnerProductSpace.ip-sym V y x) cross0
  in
  trans (InnerProductSpace.E-def V (Additive._+_ A x y))
        (trans
           (InnerProductSpace.ip-addL V x y (Additive._+_ A x y))
           (trans
              (cong‚ÇÇ (ScalarField._+s_ F) (InnerProductSpace.ip-addR V x x y) (InnerProductSpace.ip-addR V y x y))
              (let
                  step1 : (ip x x ‚äï ip x y) ‚äï (ip y x ‚äï ip y y)
                          ‚â° (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚äï (ScalarField.0s F ‚äï ip y y)
                  step1 = cong‚ÇÇ _‚äï_ (cong (Œª t ‚Üí ip x x ‚äï t) cross0)
                                    (cong (Œª t ‚Üí t ‚äï ip y y) cross0')
                  step2 : (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚äï (ScalarField.0s F ‚äï ip y y)
                          ‚â° (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚äï ip y y
                  step2 = cong (Œª t ‚Üí (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚äï t) (ScalarLaws.+s-idL L (ip y y))
                  step3 : (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚äï ip y y
                          ‚â° ip x x ‚äï ip y y
                  step3 =
                    let leftId : (ip x x ‚äï ScalarField.0s F) ‚â° ip x x
                        leftId = trans (ScalarLaws.+s-comm L (ip x x) (ScalarField.0s F))
                                      (ScalarLaws.+s-idL L (ip x x))
                    in
                    cong (Œª t ‚Üí t ‚äï ip y y) leftId
                  step4 : ip x x ‚äï ip y y ‚â° InnerProductSpace.E V x ‚äï InnerProductSpace.E V y
                  step4 = cong‚ÇÇ _‚äï_ (sym (InnerProductSpace.E-def V x))
                                       (sym (InnerProductSpace.E-def V y))
               in
               trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4)))))

module DASHI.Geometry.FiniteSpeed where

module DASHI.Geometry.ContractiveDemo where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (¬¨_; Dec; yes; no)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong)
-- Removed Reasoning imports as they are missing in stdlib.
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s; _‚âü_; _‚â§_; _‚äî_)
open import Data.Nat.Base         using (z<s)
open import Data.Empty            using (‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric
open import Contraction

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Discrete ultrametric on Nat: d x y = 0 if x=y else 1
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
dNat x y with x ‚âü y
... | yes _ = 0
... | no  _ = 1

dNat-refl0 : ‚àÄ t ‚Üí dNat t t ‚â° 0
dNat-refl0 t with t ‚âü t
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = ‚ä•-elim (n refl)

id-zeroNat : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí dNat x x ‚â° 0
id-zeroNat x with x ‚âü x
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = ‚ä•-elim (n refl)

symNat : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚â° dNat y x
symNat x y with x ‚âü y | y ‚âü x
... | yes xy | yes yx = refl
... | no  xy | no  yx = refl
... | yes xy | no  yx = ‚ä•-elim (yx (sym xy))
... | no  xy | yes yx = ‚ä•-elim (xy (sym yx))

-- ultratriangle: d x z ‚â§ max (d x y) (d y z)
-- for discrete metric this holds by case split
ultraNat : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí dNat x z ‚â§ (dNat x y ‚äî dNat y z)
ultraNat x y z with x ‚âü z
... | yes _ = z‚â§n
... | no x‚â¢z with x ‚âü y | y ‚âü z
...   | yes xy | yes yz = ‚ä•-elim (x‚â¢z (trans xy yz))
...   | no  _  | yes yz = s‚â§s z‚â§n
...   | yes xy | no  _  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
...   | no  _  | no  _  = s‚â§s z‚â§n

UNat : Ultrametric Nat
UNat = record
  { d             = dNat
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroNat
  ; symmetric     = symNat
  ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A projection operator: K projects everything to a fixed target t
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Kproj : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
Kproj t _ = t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness helper
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat-x‚â¢y=1 : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚â° 1
dNat-x‚â¢y=1 {x} {y} x‚â¢y with x ‚âü y
... | yes eq = ‚ä•-elim (x‚â¢y eq)
... | no _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Strict contraction on distinct points (Contractive‚â¢ style)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

contractive‚â¢-proj : ‚àÄ t ‚Üí (‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí dNat (Kproj t x) (Kproj t y) < dNat x y)
contractive‚â¢-proj t {x} {y} x‚â¢y
  rewrite dNat-refl0 t
        | dNat-x‚â¢y=1 {x} {y} x‚â¢y
  = z<s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point uniqueness for projection
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fixed : (Nat ‚Üí Nat) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
Fixed K a = K a ‚â° a

uniqueFixedProj :
  ‚àÄ t x y ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kproj t) x ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kproj t) y ‚Üí
  x ‚â° y
uniqueFixedProj t x y fx fy =
  trans (sym fx) fy
module DASHI.Geometry.Signature.HyperbolicFormZ where

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _*_; _+_; _-_; _‚â§_; _<_; +_)
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

record CausalCountsZ (k : ‚Ñï) : Set where
  field
    tau   : ‚Ñ§
    sigma : Vec ‚Ñ§ k

open CausalCountsZ public

-- Sum of squares for a vector of ‚Ñ§.
sumSq : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ k ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sumSq [] = + 0
sumSq (x ‚à∑ xs) = (x * x) + sumSq xs

-- Hyperbolic quadratic form: a * tau^2 - b * |sigma|^2
F : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí CausalCountsZ k ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
F {k} a b c =
  (a * ((tau c) * (tau c))) - (b * sumSq (sigma c))

-- Finite-speed cone: |sigma|^2 ‚â§ c^2 * tau^2
ConeBound : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí CausalCountsZ k ‚Üí Set
ConeBound {k} c q =
  sumSq (sigma q) ‚â§ (c * c) * ((tau q) * (tau q))

-- Exact cone boundary (lightlike).
ConeBoundary : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí CausalCountsZ k ‚Üí Set
ConeBoundary {k} c q =
  sumSq (sigma q) ‚â° (c * c) * ((tau q) * (tau q))
module DASHI.Geometry.Signature.Signature31Instance where

open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; replicate)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (refl)

open import DASHI.Geometry.ConeTimeIsotropy as CTI
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect using (Additive)
open import DASHI.Geometry.Signature.HyperbolicForm as HF
open import DASHI.Geometry.Signature.ConeArrowInstances as CAI
open import DASHI.Geometry.Signature31FromConeArrowIsotropy as S31

-- Minimal additive + scalar structures for the carrier V.
AdditiveV : Additive _
AdditiveV =
  record
    { Carrier = CAI.V
    ; _+_ = Œª x y ‚Üí
        record
          { tau = HF.tau x + HF.tau y
          ; sigma = HF.sigma x
          }
    ; 0# = record { tau = 0 ; sigma = replicate 3 0 }
    ; -_ = Œª x ‚Üí x
    }

ScalarNat : ScalarField _
ScalarNat =
  record
    { S = ‚Ñï
    ; _+s_ = _+_
    ; _*s_ = _*_
    ; 0s = 0
    ; 1s = 1
    ; -s_ = Œª n ‚Üí n
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.Signature.ConeArrowInstances where

open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

-- Concrete carrier: causal counts with 3 spatial components.
V : Set
V = HF.CausalCounts 3

-- Cone: hyperbolic bound at fixed speed c (parametric).
coneStructure : ‚Ñï ‚Üí ConeStructure V
coneStructure c =
  record
    { Cone = HF.ConeBound c
    ; ConeNontrivial = tt
    }

-- Arrow: time increases (tau strictly increases).
timeArrow : TimeArrow V
timeArrow =
  record
    { _‚â∫_ = Œª x y ‚Üí HF.tau x < HF.tau y
    ; Irreflexive = Œª _ ‚Üí tt
    ; Transitive = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí tt
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.Signature.HyperbolicForm where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _*_; _+_; _‚à∏_; _^_; _‚â§_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

record CausalCounts (k : ‚Ñï) : Set where
  field
    tau   : ‚Ñï
    sigma : Vec ‚Ñï k

open CausalCounts public

-- Sum of squares for a vector of Nat.
sumSq : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñï k ‚Üí ‚Ñï
sumSq [] = zero
sumSq (x ‚à∑ xs) = (x * x) + sumSq xs

-- Hyperbolic quadratic form: a * tau^2 - b * |sigma|^2
F : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí CausalCounts k ‚Üí ‚Ñï
F {k} a b c =
  (a * ((tau c) ^ 2)) ‚à∏ (b * sumSq (sigma c))

-- Finite-speed cone: |sigma|^2 ‚â§ c^2 * tau^2
ConeBound : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí CausalCounts k ‚Üí Set
ConeBound {k} c q =
  sumSq (sigma q) ‚â§ (c * c) * ((tau q) ^ 2)

-- Exact cone boundary (lightlike).
ConeBoundary : ‚àÄ {k} ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí CausalCounts k ‚Üí Set
ConeBoundary {k} c q =
  sumSq (sigma q) ‚â° (c * c) * ((tau q) ^ 2)
module DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (_‚â¢_; Contractive‚â¢)

_‚àò_ : ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí A ‚Üí C
(f ‚àò g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _‚àò_
record NonExpansive {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (f : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    nonexp : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí d (f x) (f y) ‚â§ d x y

record DistinctPreserving {S : Set} (g : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    preserves‚â¢ : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí g x ‚â¢ g y

record OrderLaws : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    le-trans   : ‚àÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a ‚â§ b ‚Üí b ‚â§ c ‚Üí a ‚â§ c
    le-<-trans : ‚àÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a ‚â§ b ‚Üí b < c ‚Üí a < c
    <-le-trans : ‚àÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a < b ‚Üí b ‚â§ c ‚Üí a < c

-- If f and g are nonexpansive and h is strictly contractive, then f ‚àò h ‚àò g is strictly contractive.
composeStrict :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
    (f g h : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  OrderLaws ‚Üí
  NonExpansive U f ‚Üí
  NonExpansive U g ‚Üí
  DistinctPreserving g ‚Üí
  Contraction.Contractive‚â¢ U h ‚Üí
  Contraction.Contractive‚â¢ U (f ‚àò (h ‚àò g))
composeStrict U f g h laws neF neG dpG sh =
  record
    { contraction‚â¢ = Œª {x} {y} x‚â¢y ‚Üí
        let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
            open Contraction.Contractive‚â¢ sh
            open OrderLaws laws
            step1 = NonExpansive.nonexp neF (h (g x)) (h (g y))
            step2 = contraction‚â¢ {x = g x} {y = g y} (DistinctPreserving.preserves‚â¢ dpG x‚â¢y)
            step3 = NonExpansive.nonexp neG x y
        in
        <-le-trans (le-<-trans step1 step2) step3
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

record Group (G : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    _‚àô_  : G ‚Üí G ‚Üí G
    e    : G
    inv  : G ‚Üí G
    assoc : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí (a ‚àô b) ‚àô c ‚â° a ‚àô (b ‚àô c)
    idL   : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí e ‚àô a ‚â° a
    invL  : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí (inv a) ‚àô a ‚â° e

record Isotropy
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (T : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set‚ÇÅ where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    G      : Set
    group  : Group G
    act    : G ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    preservesMetric :
      ‚àÄ g x y ‚Üí d (act g x) (act g y) ‚â° d x y
    commutesWithT :
      ‚àÄ g x ‚Üí T (act g x) ‚â° act g (T x)

-- Trivial isotropy: one element group acting by identity.
trivialIsotropy :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  Isotropy U T
trivialIsotropy U T =
  record
    { G = ‚ä§
    ; group = record
        { _‚àô_ = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt
        ; e = tt
        ; inv = Œª _ ‚Üí tt
        ; assoc = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí refl
        ; idL = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
        ; invL = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
        }
    ; act = Œª _ x ‚Üí x
    ; preservesMetric = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí refl
    ; commutesWithT = Œª _ _ ‚Üí refl
    }

  (X : Set ‚Ñìx) (E : Set ‚Ñìe)

    _‚â§_ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìe

    collapse : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí _‚â§_ (energy (D (T x))) (energy (D x))

record Parallelogram {‚Ñì} (X : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X

      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
        (Q (x + y) +‚Ñö Q (x - y))
          ‚â°
        ((two‚Ñö *‚Ñö Q x) +‚Ñö (two‚Ñö *‚Ñö Q y))

  field
    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X

    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    bilinear : Set
    symmetric : Set
    norm-def : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Q x ‚â° ‚ü™ x , x ‚ü´

Parallelogram‚áíQuadratic :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {X : Set ‚Ñì} ‚Üí
  Parallelogram X ‚Üí
  Œ£ (QuadraticStructure X) (Œª _ ‚Üí ‚ä§)

  record
    { _+_ = _+_
    ; _-_ = _-_
    ; Q = Q
    ; ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ = Œª x _ ‚Üí Q x
    ; bilinear = ‚ä§
    ; symmetric = ‚ä§
    ; norm-def = Œª _ ‚Üí refl

  , tt

module DASHI.Geometry.COL where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes
open import DASHI.Core.LensKernel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contraction‚ÄìObstruction‚ÄìLift (COL)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record COL (S : Nat -> Set) : Set1 where
  field
    E    : forall n -> S n -> Nat
    K    : forall n -> S n -> S n
    Obs  : forall n -> S n -> Bool
    lift : forall n -> S n -> S (suc n)

    -- Contraction inside level n: energy does not increase.
    contract : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> E n (K n x) ‚â§ E n x

    -- Obstruction is stable under K: if you are obstructed, stepping doesn't ‚Äúsolve‚Äù it magically.
    obs-stable : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> Obs n x ‚â° true -> Obs n (K n x) ‚â° true

    -- Lift is witness-respecting: the old state is embedded, not destroyed.
    embed-ok : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> ‚ä§

open COL public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Derived theorem hooks (the ‚Äúschema theorems‚Äù)

-- If not obstructed, repeated contraction gives monotone energy sequence.
iterate : forall {A : Set} -> (A -> A) -> Nat -> A -> A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc k) x = iterate f k (f x)

E-monotone-iter :
  forall {S : Nat -> Set} (C : COL S) ->
  (n : Nat) (k : Nat) (x : S n) ->
  COL.E C n (iterate (COL.K C n) k x) ‚â§ COL.E C n x
E-monotone-iter C n zero    x = ‚â§-refl
E-monotone-iter C n (suc k) x =
  ‚â§-trans
    (E-monotone-iter C n k (COL.K C n x))
    (COL.contract C n x)
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP
open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym)

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _‚àô_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = Œª a ‚Üí a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityÀ°
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x y : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    ‚â° UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y
preservesMetric {n} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ (act g x))) ‚â° act g (RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)))
commutesWithT {n} false x = refl
commutesWithT {n} true x = sym (RO.invVec-P·µ£ x)

realIsotropyInstance :
  ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (Œª x ‚Üí RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)))
realIsotropyInstance {n} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.Signature31FromConeArrowIsotropy where

record SignatureAxioms {‚Ñìv ‚Ñìs}
  (A : Additive ‚Ñìv) (F : ScalarField ‚Ñìs)

record QuadraticEmergenceAxioms {‚Ñìv ‚Ñìs}
  (A : Additive ‚Ñìv) (F : ScalarField ‚Ñìs)
  (PD : ProjectionDefect A)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìv ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  open ProjectionDefect PD
  field
    Energy : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.S F
    ParallelogramQ :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy (Additive._+_ A x y))
                                  (Energy (Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A y)))
              ‚â° ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy x) (Energy x))
                                   (ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy y) (Energy y))
    Additive-On-Orth :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ProjectionDefect.Orth PD x y ‚Üí
        Energy (Additive._+_ A x y) ‚â°
        ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy x) (Energy y)
    PD-splits : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      Energy x ‚â°
      ScalarField._+s_ F (Energy (ProjectionDefect.P PD x))
                           (Energy (ProjectionDefect.D PD x))

open QuadraticEmergenceAxioms public

QuadraticFormEmergence :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìv ‚Ñìs} (A : Additive ‚Ñìv) (F : ScalarField ‚Ñìs)
    (PD : ProjectionDefect A)
    (Ax : QuadraticEmergenceAxioms A F PD)
  ‚Üí Œ£ (QuadraticForm A F) (Œª qf ‚Üí ‚ä§)
QuadraticFormEmergence A F PD Ax =
  let open QuadraticEmergenceAxioms Ax renaming (Energy to EnergyAx; ParallelogramQ to ParallelogramQAx) in
  record
    { Q = EnergyAx
    ; Parallelogram = ParallelogramQAx
    ; Homog = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt
    }
  , tt
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractionOrthogonalityTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Product public using (_√ó_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Context for the test harness (no postulates; all fields are explicit).
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record TestContext : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S   : Set
    _S+_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    _S-_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    0#  : S

    -- Group-ish laws you‚Äôll need for ‚Äúdetail = x - P x‚Äù reasoning
    +-assoc : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí (x S+ y) S+ z ‚â° x S+ (y S+ z)
    +-id ≥   : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí x S+ 0# ‚â° x
    +-idÀ°   : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí 0# S+ x ‚â° x
    +-inv ≥  : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí x S- x ‚â° 0#

    -- Metric / norm interface (kept abstract; later bind to your induced norm)
    dist : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- A ‚Äúnorm‚Äù is distance to 0. (You can swap this for your actual norm.)
    ‚à•_‚à• : S ‚Üí Set
    ‚à•x‚à•-def : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí ‚à• x ‚à• ‚â° dist x 0#


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Recognisable lift decomposition (your ‚Äútelescoping identity‚Äù)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record RecognisableLift {C : TestContext} (P : TestContext.S C ‚Üí TestContext.S C) : Set where
  open TestContext C renaming (S to S‚ÇÄ; _S+_ to _+_; _S-_ to _-_; 0# to 0#)
  field
    -- every x decomposes uniquely into coarse + detail:
    coarse   : S‚ÇÄ ‚Üí S‚ÇÄ
    detail   : S‚ÇÄ ‚Üí S‚ÇÄ
    split    : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí x ‚â° coarse x + detail x

    -- recognisable uniqueness: if x = c+d = c'+d' with both c,c' fixed by P
    -- and both d,d' in the fiber kernel, then equal (abstracted)
    uniq :
      ‚àÄ x c d c' d' ‚Üí
      x ‚â° c + d ‚Üí
      x ‚â° c' + d' ‚Üí
      P c ‚â° c ‚Üí
      P c' ‚â° c' ‚Üí
      P d ‚â° 0# ‚Üí
      P d' ‚â° 0# ‚Üí
      (c ‚â° c') √ó (d ‚â° d')

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Non-expansive idempotent projection axioms
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record NonExpansiveProjection {C : TestContext} (P : TestContext.S C ‚Üí TestContext.S C) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open TestContext C renaming (S to S‚ÇÄ; _S+_ to _+_; _S-_ to _-_; 0# to 0#; dist to dist‚ÇÄ)
  field
    idem  : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x
    nonexp : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí dist‚ÇÄ (P x) (P y) ‚â° dist‚ÇÄ x y
    -- (If you want ‚â§ instead of ‚â°, change dist codomain to ‚Ñö/‚Ñù and use ‚â§.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orthogonality: ‚Äúno double counting‚Äù in the induced quadratic energy
--
-- This is the *test* you want Agda to force:
--   from RecognisableLift + NonExpansiveProjection (+ stability axiom),
--   derive Pythagorean split for a quadratic norm and orthogonality.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record OrthogonalSplit {C : TestContext} (P : TestContext.S C ‚Üí TestContext.S C) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open TestContext C renaming (S to S‚ÇÄ; _S+_ to _+_; _S-_ to _-_; 0# to 0#; ‚à•_‚à• to ‚à•_‚à•‚ÇÄ)
  field
    ‚üÇ-pred : S‚ÇÄ ‚Üí S‚ÇÄ ‚Üí Set          -- ‚Äúorthogonal‚Äù predicate (abstract)
    pythag :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      let c = P x
          d = x - P x
      in  ‚à•_‚à•‚ÇÄ x ‚â° (‚à•_‚à•‚ÇÄ c) √ó (‚à•_‚à•‚ÇÄ d)   -- placeholder shape; replace with numeric identity
    orth :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      let c = P x
          d = x - P x
      in  ‚üÇ-pred c d

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The Master Theorem (as a test harness)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ProjectionContractionOrthogonalityAxioms (C : TestContext) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    -- Stability premise: the multiscale hierarchy must forbid leakage.
    StabilityNoLeakage :
      (P : TestContext.S C ‚Üí TestContext.S C) ‚Üí Set

    MasterTheorem :
      (P : TestContext.S C ‚Üí TestContext.S C) ‚Üí
      RecognisableLift {C = C} P ‚Üí
      NonExpansiveProjection {C = C} P ‚Üí
      StabilityNoLeakage P ‚Üí
      OrthogonalSplit {C = C} P
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstanceShiftTailInv where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong; subst; subst‚ÇÇ)

open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_; proj‚ÇÅ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS
open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution as TCI
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

cong‚ÇÇ' :
  ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} {x‚ÇÅ x‚ÇÇ : A} {y‚ÇÅ y‚ÇÇ : B}
  (f : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí x‚ÇÅ ‚â° x‚ÇÇ ‚Üí y‚ÇÅ ‚â° y‚ÇÇ ‚Üí f x‚ÇÅ y‚ÇÅ ‚â° f x‚ÇÇ y‚ÇÇ
cong‚ÇÇ' f refl refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Two-element group acting by tail inversion

boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _‚àô_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = Œª a ‚Üí a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityÀ°
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

-- Apply invVec to tail only

tailInv : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
tailInv {m} {k} x = TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ RTC.invVec (TCP.tailOf m k x)

tailInv-++ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  tailInv {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚â° c ++ RTC.invVec t
tailInv-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

coarseOf-tailInv :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (tailInv {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
  = refl

act : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
act {m} {k} b x = if b then tailInv {m} {k} x else x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- tailInv is an involution

tailInv-invol : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí tailInv {m} {k} (tailInv {m} {k} x) ‚â° x
tailInv-invol {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚â° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
  in
  trans
    (tailInv-++ c (RTC.invVec t))
    (trans
      (cong (Œª v ‚Üí c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t))
      (sym p))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric invariance for tailInv

preservesMetric :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (act {m} {k} g x) (act {m} {k} g y)
    ‚â° UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
preservesMetric {m} {k} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {m} {k} true x y =
  let
    c  = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t  = TCP.tailOf m k x
    c' = TCP.coarseOf m k y
    t' = TCP.tailOf m k y
    p : x ‚â° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : y ‚â° c' ++ t'
    q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
    le1 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
    le1 = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚â§-tail c c' t t' inv
    le2 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2 =
      let
        le2' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t))
                            (c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t'))
               ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
        le2' = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚â§-tail c c' (RTC.invVec t) (RTC.invVec t') inv
        r1 : c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t) ‚â° c ++ t
        r1 = cong (Œª v ‚Üí c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t)
        r2 : c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t') ‚â° c' ++ t'
        r2 = cong (Œª v ‚Üí c' ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t')
      in
      NatP.‚â§-trans
        (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym (cong‚ÇÇ' FAM.dNatFine r1 r2)))
        le2'
    le1' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine x y
    le1' = subst‚ÇÇ (Œª a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine a b)
                  (sym p) (sym q) le1
    le2' : FAM.dNatFine x y ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2' = subst‚ÇÇ (Œª a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t'))
                  (sym p) (sym q) le2
  in
  NatP.‚â§-antisym le1' le2'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commutation with the shift stack

commutesWithT :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act {m} {k} g x)))
    ‚â° act {m} {k} g (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} false x = refl
commutesWithT {m} {k} true x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    r : act {m} {k} true x ‚â° c ++ RTC.invVec t
    r = refl
    stepR : TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t) ‚â° c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
    stepR = TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
    stepP : TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)) ‚â° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepP = TCP.P·µ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP : TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t)) ‚â° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP = trans (cong (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}) stepR) stepP
    stepC : ROSS.C {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
            ‚â° CM.canonVec c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepC = CM.C·µ£-++ c (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
    t' = TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
    p : x ‚â° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    stepT : ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) ‚â° CM.canonVec c ++ t'
    stepT =
      let
        r : TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x ‚â° c ++ TCP.shiftTail t
        r = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t)
        pr : TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
        pr = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} v) r) (TCP.P·µ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      in
      trans
        (cong (Œª v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} v) pr)
        (CM.C·µ£-++ c t')
    stepAct : act {m} {k} true (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))) ‚â° CM.canonVec c ++ RTC.invVec t'
    stepAct =
      trans
        (cong (Œª v ‚Üí tailInv {m} {k} v) stepT)
        (tailInv-++ (CM.canonVec c) t')
    stepInv : RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)) ‚â° TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepInv =
      trans
        (TCI.invVec-projTail (TCP.shiftTail t))
        (cong TCP.projTail (TCI.invVec-shiftTail t))
  in
  trans
    (cong (Œª v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} v))) r)
    (trans
      (cong (Œª v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} v) stepRP)
      (trans
        stepC
        (trans
          (cong (Œª v ‚Üí CM.canonVec c ++ v) (sym stepInv))
          (sym stepAct))))

realIsotropyInstanceTailInv :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (Œª x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceTailInv {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act {m} {k}
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric {m} {k}
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.BanachFixedPointNat where

-- For ‚Ñï-valued ultrametrics, a StrictContraction already packages the fixed point.
banachFromStrict :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  Contr.StrictContraction U T ‚Üí BFP.BanachFixedPoint U T

    { fp = Contr.StrictContraction.fp sc
    ; fixes = Contr.StrictContraction.fixed sc

module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y ‚â§ radius

preservesLocality :
  ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  local x y ‚Üí
  local (RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x))) (RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ y)))
preservesLocality {n} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
    step1 : d (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)) (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ y)) ‚â§ d (RO.R·µ£ x) (RO.R·µ£ y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpP·µ£ {n}) (RO.R·µ£ x) (RO.R·µ£ y)
    step2 : d (RO.R·µ£ x) (RO.R·µ£ y) ‚â§ d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpR·µ£ {n}) x y
    step3 : d (RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x))) (RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ y)))
            ‚â§ d (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)) (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpC·µ£ {n}) (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)) (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ y))
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans (NatP.‚â§-trans step3 step1) (NatP.‚â§-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (Œª x ‚Üí RO.C·µ£ (RO.P·µ£ (RO.R·µ£ x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {n} =
  record
    { local = local {n}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {n}
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.RGFlowContract where

  field
    CouplingState : Set
    U : Ultrametric CouplingState
    step : CouplingState ‚Üí CouplingState
    mdl : CouplingState ‚Üí Nat

    -- Two closure options:
    -- A) Contraction (metric closure)
    stepContractive : Contractive U step

    -- B) Lyapunov descent (MDL closure)
    mdlMonotone : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí mdl (step s) ‚â§ mdl s
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong)
open import Data.Product using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record Additive (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Carrier : Set ‚Ñì
    _+_     : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier

open Additive public

record ProjectionDefect {‚Ñì} (A : Additive ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  open Additive A
  field
    P     : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A
    D     : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A
    D-def : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí D x ‚â° Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (P x))

    P-idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x

    Orth : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì
    Orth-PD : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Orth (P x) (D x)

open ProjectionDefect public
module DASHI.Geometry.MQContractive where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Rational using (_<_; _‚â§_)

open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ñö; _*‚Ñö_; 1‚Ñö)
open import DASHI.Geometry.MaskedQuadratic

record MQContractive {n : Nat} (MQ : MaskedQuadratic n) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field

    lambda : ‚Ñö

    contract : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ (T x) ‚â§ (lambda *‚Ñö lambda) *‚Ñö MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ x

module DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Energy.Energy
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

-- Polarization interface: once Q is quadratic, define an inner product
-- and record the polarization identity as a seam.
record Polarization {‚Ñìv ‚Ñìs}
  (A : Additive ‚Ñìv) (F : ScalarField ‚Ñìs)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìv ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  field
    Q : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.S F
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.S F
    two : ScalarField.S F
    two-def : two ‚â° (ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField.1s F) (ScalarField.1s F))
    polarization :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
        Q (Additive._+_ A x y) ‚â°
        ScalarField._+s_ F
          (ScalarField._+s_ F (Q x) (Q y))
          (ScalarField._*s_ F two (‚ü™ x , y ‚ü´))

open Polarization public

-- Orthogonality corollary: once closest-point is established and
-- the polarization identity is available, orthogonality becomes a target.
record OrthogonalityFromPolarization {‚Ñìv ‚Ñìs}
  {A : Additive ‚Ñìv} {F : ScalarField ‚Ñìs}
  {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace (Additive.Carrier A) P)
  (Pj : Projection (Additive.Carrier A))
  (Pol : Polarization A F)
  (CP : ClosestPoint ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìv ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  field
    Orth : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìs
    Orth-def : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Orth x y ‚â°
      (Polarization.‚ü™_,_‚ü´ Pol x y ‚â° ScalarField.0s F)
    orthPD : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      Orth (Projection.P Pj x)
           (Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (Projection.P Pj x)))

open OrthogonalityFromPolarization public
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractiveConstant where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric

_‚â¢_ : {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
_‚â¢_ {A} x y = (x ‚â° y) ‚Üí ‚ä•

record DiscreteUltrametric {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    nonzero-on-distinct : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí d x y ‚â¢ zero

Kconst : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
Kconst t _ = t

record Contractive‚â¢
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    collapses-on-distinct : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí d (K x) (K y) ‚â° zero
    original-nonzero : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí d x y ‚â¢ zero

const-proj-contractive‚â¢ :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  ‚Üí DiscreteUltrametric U
  ‚Üí (t : S)
  ‚Üí Contractive‚â¢ U (Kconst t)
const-proj-contractive‚â¢ {S} U DU t =
  let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
      open DiscreteUltrametric DU
  in
  record
    { collapses-on-distinct = Œª {x} {_} _ ‚Üí
        UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U (Kconst t x)
    ; original-nonzero = Œª {x} {y} x‚â¢y ‚Üí
        nonzero-on-distinct x‚â¢y
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.EinsteinFromRGNoLeakage where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record RGGeometryData : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    M : Set
    Point : Set
    Tensor2 : Set
    ‚Ñö : Set
    0q : ‚Ñö
    div : Tensor2 ‚Üí Point ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    sym : Tensor2 ‚Üí Set
    G : M ‚Üí Tensor2
    T : M ‚Üí Tensor2
    RGState : Set
    step : RGState ‚Üí RGState
    geom : RGState ‚Üí M
    PœÑ : Tensor2 ‚Üí Tensor2

open RGGeometryData public

DefectD : (D : RGGeometryData) ‚Üí RGGeometryData.RGState D ‚Üí RGGeometryData.Tensor2 D
DefectD D s = RGGeometryData.PœÑ D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D (RGGeometryData.step D s)))

record GR_NoLeakage (D : RGGeometryData) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    bianchi :
      ‚àÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚â° RGGeometryData.0q D
    conserve :
      ‚àÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚â° RGGeometryData.0q D
    defect-law :
      ‚àÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) ‚â° DefectD D s
    symG :
      ‚àÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))
    symT :
      ‚àÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))

open GR_NoLeakage public

record EinsteinConsequences {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    divergenceFree :
      ‚àÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚â° RGGeometryData.0q D
    conservation :
      ‚àÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚â° RGGeometryData.0q D
    einsteinEq :
      ‚àÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) ‚â° DefectD D s

EinsteinFromRG :
  ‚àÄ {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) ‚Üí
  EinsteinConsequences A
EinsteinFromRG A =
  record
    { divergenceFree = bianchi A
    ; conservation = conserve A
    ; einsteinEq = defect-law A
    }

-- Parameterised CCR/Weyl data so this module is non-vacuous.
record CCRData : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    ‚Ñö : Set
    _*q_ : ‚Ñö ‚Üí ‚Ñö ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    Hilbert : Set
    U : Set
    _‚àô_ : U ‚Üí U ‚Üí U

Weyl : (D : CCRData) ‚Üí Set
Weyl D =
  ‚àÄ a b ‚Üí
    CCRData._‚àô_ D (CCRData.XTrans D a) (CCRData.PTrans D b) ‚â°
    CCRData._‚àô_ D (CCRData.phase D (CCRData._*q_ D a b))
                   (CCRData._‚àô_ D (CCRData.PTrans D b) (CCRData.XTrans D a))

    weyl : Weyl D
    proj-inv-P : ‚àÄ b œà ‚Üí P (actP b œà) ‚â° P œà
    proj-covar-X : ‚àÄ a œà ‚Üí P (actX a œà) ‚â° actX a (P œà)

CCR : CCRData ‚Üí Set‚ÇÅ
CCR D = ProjectionWeylAxioms D

stone-vn : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí ProjectionWeylAxioms D ‚Üí CCR D

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.SignatureDerivationInstance where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _*_; _‚à∏_; _^_; _>_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.SignatureDerivation

-- Concrete hyperbolic form on scalar (tau,sigma) counts.
Nat¬≤ : ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï
Nat¬≤ = _^_ 2

a‚ÇÄ b‚ÇÄ : ‚Ñï
a‚ÇÄ = suc zero
b‚ÇÄ = suc zero

scale‚ÇÄ : ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï
scale‚ÇÄ x y = x * y

F‚ÇÄ : CausalCounts ‚Üí ‚Ñï
F‚ÇÄ x = (a‚ÇÄ * (CausalCounts.tau x ^ 2)) ‚à∏ (b‚ÇÄ * (CausalCounts.sigma x ^ 2))

-- Build a SignatureDerivationAxioms instance by supplying the remaining proofs.
-- This keeps the formulas concrete while leaving the actual properties to be discharged.
mkSignatureDerivation :
  (hom : ‚àÄ l (x : CausalCounts) ‚Üí F‚ÇÄ x ‚â° (l * l) * F‚ÇÄ x) ‚Üí
  (cone : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí CausalCounts.tau x > CausalCounts.sigma x ‚Üí F‚ÇÄ x > 0) ‚Üí
  SignatureDerivationAxioms
mkSignatureDerivation hom cone =
  record
    { _Nat¬≤ = Nat¬≤
    ; a = a‚ÇÄ
    ; b = b‚ÇÄ
    ; scale = scale‚ÇÄ
    ; F = F‚ÇÄ
    ; Homogeneous = hom
    ; ConeMonotone = cone
    ; UniqueHyperbolic = Œª x ‚Üí refl
    }

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (_*_; _‚â§_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFiniteness public

record UVFinitenessAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    L : Set                  -- linear size parameter
    vol area : L ‚Üí Nat        -- discrete counts
    dimH : L ‚Üí Nat            -- effective Hilbert dimension / mode count
    eta  : Nat               -- holographic proportionality constant

open UVFinitenessAxioms public

AreaBound : UVFinitenessAxioms ‚Üí Set
AreaBound A = ‚àÄ l ‚Üí dimH A l ‚â§ (eta A * area A l)

UVFinitenessTheorem :
  (A : UVFinitenessAxioms) ‚Üí
  (areaBound : AreaBound A) ‚Üí
  UVFinite (record
    { L = L A
    ; dimH = dimH A
    ; bound = Œª l ‚Üí eta A * area A l
    ; dimH‚â§bound = areaBound
    })
UVFinitenessTheorem A areaBound =
  let bounded = record
        { L = L A
        ; dimH = dimH A
        ; bound = Œª l ‚Üí eta A * area A l
        ; dimH‚â§bound = areaBound
        }
  in uvFiniteness bounded
module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.NoGlobalAttractor where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

-- Iteration
iterate : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

-- ‚ÄúEventually constant‚Äù orbit at a.
EventuallyConst : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set
EventuallyConst f x a = Œ£ Nat (Œª N ‚Üí ‚àÄ n ‚Üí iterate f (N + n) x ‚â° a)

-- Global attractor = same a for all x.
GlobalAttractor : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Set
GlobalAttractor f = Œ£ _ (Œª a ‚Üí ‚àÄ x ‚Üí EventuallyConst f x a)

-- The useful theorem: invertible + nontrivial ‚áí no global attractor.
-- (In a finite/discrete world, invertible dynamics can‚Äôt collapse all orbits to one point unless singleton.)

record NoGlobalAttractorAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    theorem :
      ‚àÄ {S : Set} {U : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
      Invertible U ‚Üí
      (Œ£ S (Œª x ‚Üí Œ£ S (Œª y ‚Üí ¬¨ (x ‚â° y)))) ‚Üí
      ¬¨ GlobalAttractor U

invertible-nontrivial-no-attractor :
  NoGlobalAttractorAxioms ‚Üí
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} {U : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
  Invertible U ‚Üí
  (Œ£ S (Œª x ‚Üí Œ£ S (Œª y ‚Üí ¬¨ (x ‚â° y)))) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ GlobalAttractor U
invertible-nontrivial-no-attractor ax = NoGlobalAttractorAxioms.theorem ax

record CausalCounts : Set where
  field
    tau sigma : Nat

record SignatureDerivationAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    _Nat¬≤ : Nat ‚Üí Nat
    a b : Nat
    scale : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
    F : CausalCounts ‚Üí Nat

    Homogeneous :
      ‚àÄ l (x : CausalCounts) ‚Üí F x ‚â° (l * l) * F x

    ConeMonotone :
      ‚àÄ (x : CausalCounts) ‚Üí
        CausalCounts.tau x > CausalCounts.sigma x ‚Üí F x > 0

    UniqueHyperbolic :
      ‚àÄ (x : CausalCounts) ‚Üí
        F x ‚â° (a * (CausalCounts.tau x ^ 2)) ‚à∏ (b * (CausalCounts.sigma x ^ 2))

record Measurement {S : Set} (ŒÝ : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    proj : Projection ŒÝ
    nontrivial : Nontrivial ŒÝ   -- measurement actually collapses something

measurement-not-invertible :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} {ŒÝ : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
  Measurement ŒÝ ‚Üí
  ¬¨ Invertible ŒÝ
measurement-not-invertible {S} {ŒÝ} M invŒÝ =
  let open Measurement M in
  -- If ŒÝ invertible and projection ‚áí ŒÝ = id, contradict nontrivial.
  nontrivial (projection+invertible‚Üíidentity proj invŒÝ)

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyInstance where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _*_ ; _‚â§_; _^_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-reflexive; *-identityÀ°)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; refl; trans; _‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests
open import DASHI.Physics.Holography.AreaLaw as AL

uvFinitenessAxioms : UVFinitenessAxioms
uvFinitenessAxioms =
  record
    { L = ‚Ñï
    ; vol = Œª n ‚Üí n
    ; area = Œª n ‚Üí n
    ; dimH = Œª n ‚Üí n
    ; eta = 1
    }

uvAreaBound : AreaBound uvFinitenessAxioms
uvAreaBound n = NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym (NatP.*-identityÀ° n))

uvFinitenessInst : _
uvFinitenessInst = UVFinitenessTheorem uvFinitenessAxioms uvAreaBound

-- Concrete area-law instance (physics-facing) using the minimal AreaLaw interface.
areaRegion : AL.RegionCounts
areaRegion =
  record
    { Region = ‚Ñï
    ; area = Œª n ‚Üí n
    ; volume = Œª n ‚Üí n
    ; admCount = Œª _ ‚Üí 1
    }

onePow : ‚àÄ r ‚Üí 1 ^ r ‚â° 1
onePow zero = refl
onePow (suc r) = trans (NatP.*-identityÀ° (1 ^ r)) (onePow r)

areaLawUV : AL.UVFinite areaRegion
areaLawUV =
  record
    { K = 1
    ; areaLaw = Œª r ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym (onePow r))
    }

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (Œ£; _,_)

record SpinData : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    SO : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
    Cl‚Å∞ : Set
    Spin : Set
    toSO : Spin ‚Üí SO 3 1
    kernel¬±1 : Set
    identitySO : SO 3 1

record SpinDoubleCover (D : SpinData) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open SpinData D
  field
    hom : Spin ‚Üí SO 3 1
    kernel : Spin ‚Üí Set
    kernel‚äÜ¬±1 : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí hom s ‚â° identitySO ‚Üí kernel s ‚Üí kernel¬±1
    surjective : ‚àÄ g ‚Üí Œ£ Spin (Œª s ‚Üí hom s ‚â° g)

-- Building a witness now requires surjectivity/kernel proof data.
spinDoubleCover-witness :
  ‚àÄ D ‚Üí
  (ker : SpinData.Spin D ‚Üí Set)
  (ker‚äÜ¬±1 : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí SpinData.toSO D s ‚â° SpinData.identitySO D ‚Üí ker s ‚Üí SpinData.kernel¬±1 D)
  (surj : ‚àÄ g ‚Üí Œ£ (SpinData.Spin D) (Œª s ‚Üí SpinData.toSO D s ‚â° g)) ‚Üí
  SpinDoubleCover D
spinDoubleCover-witness D ker ker‚äÜ¬±1 surj =
  record { hom = SpinData.toSO D ; kernel = ker ; kernel‚äÜ¬±1 = ker‚äÜ¬±1 ; surjective = surj }

SpinIsDoubleCover : ‚àÄ {D} ‚Üí SpinDoubleCover D ‚Üí Set
SpinIsDoubleCover {D} cover =
  ‚àÄ g ‚Üí Œ£ (SpinData.Spin D) (Œª s ‚Üí SpinDoubleCover.hom cover s ‚â° g)

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.Unitary where

record ComplexAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    ‚ÑÇ : Set
    _‚â°‚ÑÇ_ : ‚ÑÇ ‚Üí ‚ÑÇ ‚Üí Set

open ComplexAxioms public

-- Abstract ‚ÄúHilbert-like‚Äù structure: we only need an inner product interface.
record InnerProductSpace (A : ComplexAxioms) (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí ‚ÑÇ A

-- Unitary = invertible + inner product preservation.

  field
    inv : Invertible U
    preserves :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
        ComplexAxioms._‚â°‚ÑÇ_ A
          (InnerProductSpace.‚ü™_,_‚ü´ IPS (U x) (U y))
          (InnerProductSpace.‚ü™_,_‚ü´ IPS x y)

    ‚Ñù : Set

    _R<=_ : ‚Ñù ‚Üí ‚Ñù ‚Üí Set
    _R*_ : ‚Ñù ‚Üí ‚Ñù ‚Üí ‚Ñù
    k : ‚Ñù
    StableFixedPoint : Nat ‚Üí Set

    HolographicBound :
      ‚àÄ D L ‚Üí
        _R<=_ (L R^ D) (k R* (L R^ (D ‚à∏ 1)))

    StabilityUnderDecimation :
      ‚àÄ D ‚Üí
        StableFixedPoint D ‚Üí D ‚â° 4

Boundary : (A : DimensionFixedPointAxioms) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí ‚Ñù A ‚Üí ‚Ñù A
Boundary A D L = _R^_ A L (D ‚à∏ 1)

module DASHI.Algebra.OperatorMonoidClosed where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)

data State : Set where
  st : State

Endo : Set
Endo = State ‚Üí State

_‚àò_ : Endo ‚Üí Endo ‚Üí Endo
(f ‚àò g) s = f (g s)

id : Endo
id s = s

-- The closure generated by a seed operator K (a free monoid in Endo)
data Gen (K : Endo) : Endo ‚Üí Set‚ÇÅ where
  gen-id   : Gen K id
  gen-base : Gen K K
  gen-comp : ‚àÄ {f g} ‚Üí Gen K f ‚Üí Gen K g ‚Üí Gen K (f ‚àò g)

-- Now ‚Äúclosure‚Äù is literal:
closed-under-comp :
  ‚àÄ {K : Endo} {f g : Endo} ‚Üí
  Gen K f ‚Üí Gen K g ‚Üí Gen K (f ‚àò g)
closed-under-comp = gen-comp

module DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract operator Lie algebra (commutator bracket)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ConstraintAlgebraStructure : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    Op : Set
    _‚àò_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
    _-_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
    I   : Op

    -- Constraints: Hamiltonian + Momentum (vector-index abstracted)
    Idx : Set
    H    : Op
    H·µ¢   : Idx ‚Üí Op

open ConstraintAlgebraStructure public

_bracket_ : (S : ConstraintAlgebraStructure) ‚Üí Op S ‚Üí Op S ‚Üí Op S
_bracket_ S X Y = (_-_ S) ((_‚àò_ S) X Y) ((_‚àò_ S) Y X)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closure statement: commutators of constraints re-express as constraints
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record DiracClosure (S : ConstraintAlgebraStructure) : Set where
  field
    -- [H·µ¢, H‚±º] = H_k(...)
    mom-mom :
      ‚àÄ i j ‚Üí Œ£ (Idx S) (Œª k ‚Üí (_bracket_ S (H·µ¢ S i) (H·µ¢ S j)) ‚â° H·µ¢ S k)

    -- [H, H·µ¢] = H(...)
    ham-mom :
      ‚àÄ i ‚Üí (_bracket_ S (H S) (H·µ¢ S i)) ‚â° H S

    -- [H, H] = H·µ¢(...)
    ham-ham :
      Œ£ (Idx S) (Œª k ‚Üí (_bracket_ S (H S) (H S)) ‚â° H·µ¢ S k)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Axiom bundle (no postulates)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ConstraintAlgebraAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    struct : ConstraintAlgebraStructure
    ValuationEquivariance : Set     -- ‚Äúdecimation commutes with relabellings‚Äù
    NoLeakageStability    : Set     -- fixed-point stability condition
    closure : DiracClosure struct

open ConstraintAlgebraAxioms public

ConstraintAlgebraTheorem :
  (A : ConstraintAlgebraAxioms) ‚Üí
  DiracClosure (struct A)
ConstraintAlgebraTheorem A = closure A
module DASHI.Algebra.SMConformanceVectors where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Agda.Builtin.List using (List; []; _‚à∑_)

record Vector (State : Set) : Set where
  constructor vec
  field input : State

Vectors : Set ‚Üí Set
Vectors State = List (Vector State)

ConformsOn : ‚àÄ {State Sig} ‚Üí (State ‚Üí Sig) ‚Üí (State ‚Üí Sig) ‚Üí Vectors State ‚Üí Set
ConformsOn f g [] = ‚ä§
ConformsOn f g (v ‚à∑ vs) =
  (f (Vector.input v) ‚â° g (Vector.input v)) √ó ConformsOn f g vs

record SMConformanceAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    State : Set
    Sig : Set
    specSig : State ‚Üí Sig
    implSig : State ‚Üí Sig
    vectors : Vectors State
    physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors

open SMConformanceAxioms public
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsConformance where

open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Data.Unit             using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Product          using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsSignature using (Sig15)
open import DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsTable using (State; vectors; implSig; specSig)

-- Conformance on a finite list:
ConformsOn : (f g : State ‚Üí Sig15) ‚Üí List State ‚Üí Set
ConformsOn f g []       = ‚ä§
ConformsOn f g (s ‚à∑ ss) = (f s ‚â° g s) √ó ConformsOn f g ss

-- This is the closure theorem you ‚Äúship‚Äù:
-- now fully concrete via the PhysicsTable witnesses.
physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors
physics-conformance = go vectors
  where
    go : (vs : List State) ‚Üí ConformsOn implSig specSig vs
    go []       = tt
    go (s ‚à∑ ss) = refl , go ss
module DASHI.Algebra.UnitaryVsCollapse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (¬¨_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import DASHI.Geometry.NatNoInfiniteDescent using (NatNoInfiniteDescent)

-- A minimal invertible step system with a Nat-valued measure.
record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    step  : S ‚Üí S
    inv   : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí inv (step s) ‚â° s
    right : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí step (inv s) ‚â° s
    H     : S ‚Üí Nat

open InvertibleNat public

-- Iteration
iterate : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- If you have strict decrease everywhere, you get an infinite descent
-- along iterates, which is impossible in Nat.
--
-- To keep this module lightweight, we package the ‚Äúno infinite descent‚Äù
-- fact as a single lemma that can be discharged from stdlib later.
--
-- (If you want, I can give the fully discharged stdlib proof too.)
-- Reuse the concrete Nat no-infinite-descent proof.

-- Main theorem: in an inhabited system, ‚Äústrict collapse everywhere‚Äù is impossible.
no-global-strict-collapse :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : InvertibleNat S) ‚Üí
  (s‚ÇÄ : S) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ (‚àÄ s ‚Üí H U (step U s) < H U s)
no-global-strict-collapse U s‚ÇÄ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (H U) (step U) s‚ÇÄ strict
module DASHI.Algebra.QuantumInterface where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äî_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Relation.Nullary using (¬¨_)

-- Abstract state space + observable/entropy-like measure
record QuantumSys (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    QState : Set ‚Ñì
    step   : QState ‚Üí QState

    -- ‚ÄúUnitary-like‚Äù = invertible evolution
    inv    : QState ‚Üí QState
    left   : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí inv (step s) ‚â° s
    right  : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí step (inv s) ‚â° s

    -- Measurement/projection (can be non-invertible)
    meas   : QState ‚Üí QState
    meas-idem : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí meas (meas s) ‚â° meas s

    -- Any scalar you use as ‚Äúentropy / action / code length‚Äù
    H      : QState ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì  -- keep general; specialize to Nat later
module DASHI.Algebra.Trit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)

data Trit : Set where
  neg : Trit
  zer : Trit
  pos : Trit

inv : Trit ‚Üí Trit
inv neg = pos
inv zer = zer
inv pos = neg

inv-invol : ‚àÄ t ‚Üí inv (inv t) ‚â° t
inv-invol neg = refl
inv-invol zer = refl
inv-invol pos = refl

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_; _‚äî_; _‚äì_; _‚à∏_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-trans; ‚â§-reflexive; n‚à∏n‚â°0; ‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§; ‚à∏-distribÀ°-‚äì-‚äî; ‚äì-zeroÀ°; ‚äì-zero ≥)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Base.Raw as it's not needed here.
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Nat as it's not needed here.

open import Ultrametric
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15)

lcpLen : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
lcpLen [] [] = 0
lcpLen (true  ‚à∑ xs) (true  ‚à∑ ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (false ‚à∑ xs) (false ‚à∑ ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (_ ‚à∑ _) (_ ‚à∑ _) = 0

len : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
len []       = 0
len (_ ‚à∑ xs) = suc (len xs)

dMask : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
dMask {n} x y = len {n} x ‚à∏ lcpLen x y

-- id-zero
lcpLen-self-eq : ‚àÄ {n} (m : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen m m ‚â° len {n} m
lcpLen-self-eq [] = refl
lcpLen-self-eq (true  ‚à∑ xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)
lcpLen-self-eq (false ‚à∑ xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)

id-zeroMask : ‚àÄ m ‚Üí dMask {15} m m ‚â° 0
id-zeroMask m =
  let
    step : dMask {15} m m ‚â° len {15} m ‚à∏ len {15} m
    step = cong (Œª k ‚Üí len {15} m ‚à∏ k) (lcpLen-self-eq m)
  in
  trans step (n‚à∏n‚â°0 (len {15} m))

-- symmetric
lcpLen-symmetric : ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen x y ‚â° lcpLen y x
lcpLen-symmetric [] [] = refl
lcpLen-symmetric (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) with x | y
... | true | true = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | false | false = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | true | false = refl
... | false | true = refl

len-const : ‚àÄ {n} (x : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí len x ‚â° n
len-const [] = refl
len-const (_ ‚à∑ xs) = cong suc (len-const xs)

dMask-symmetric : ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí dMask {n} x y ‚â° dMask {n} y x
dMask-symmetric {n} x y =
  let
    lenx‚â°n : len {n} x ‚â° n
    lenx‚â°n = len-const x
    leny‚â°n : len {n} y ‚â° n
    leny‚â°n = len-const y
  in
  trans (cong (Œª k ‚Üí len {n} x ‚à∏ k) (lcpLen-symmetric x y))
        (trans (cong (Œª k ‚Üí k ‚à∏ lcpLen y x) lenx‚â°n)
               (cong (Œª k ‚Üí k ‚à∏ lcpLen y x) (sym leny‚â°n)))

symMask : ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí dMask {n} x y ‚â° dMask {n} y x
symMask = dMask-symmetric

-- ultratriangle
lcpLen-ultratriangle :
  ‚àÄ {n} (x y z : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí
  (lcpLen x y ‚äì lcpLen y z) ‚â§ lcpLen x z
lcpLen-ultratriangle [] [] [] = z‚â§n
lcpLen-ultratriangle (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) (z ‚à∑ zs) with x | y | z
... | true  | true  | true  = s‚â§s (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | false | false | false = s‚â§s (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | true  | false | _     rewrite ‚äì-zeroÀ° (lcpLen (y ‚à∑ ys) (z ‚à∑ zs)) = z‚â§n
... | false | true  | _     rewrite ‚äì-zeroÀ° (lcpLen (y ‚à∑ ys) (z ‚à∑ zs)) = z‚â§n
... | true  | true  | false rewrite ‚äì-zero ≥ (lcpLen (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)) = z‚â§n
... | false | false | true  rewrite ‚äì-zero ≥ (lcpLen (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)) = z‚â§n

ultraMask : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí dMask {15} x z ‚â§ (dMask {15} x y ‚äî dMask {15} y z)
ultraMask x y z =
  let
    a = lcpLen x y
    b = lcpLen y z
    c = lcpLen x z
    lenx = len {15} x
    leny = len {15} y

    lenx‚â°n : lenx ‚â° 15
    lenx‚â°n = len-const x

    leny‚â°n : leny ‚â° 15
    leny‚â°n = len-const y

    lenx‚â°leny : lenx ‚â° leny
    lenx‚â°leny = trans lenx‚â°n (sym leny‚â°n)

    c‚â•min : (a ‚äì b) ‚â§ c
    c‚â•min = lcpLen-ultratriangle x y z

    step1 : (lenx ‚à∏ c) ‚â§ (lenx ‚à∏ (a ‚äì b))
    step1 = ‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ lenx c‚â•min

    step2 : (lenx ‚à∏ (a ‚äì b)) ‚â° (lenx ‚à∏ a) ‚äî (lenx ‚à∏ b)
    step2 = ‚à∏-distribÀ°-‚äì-‚äî lenx a b

    step2' : (lenx ‚à∏ (a ‚äì b)) ‚â° (lenx ‚à∏ a) ‚äî (leny ‚à∏ b)
    step2' = trans step2 (cong (Œª k ‚Üí (lenx ‚à∏ a) ‚äî (k ‚à∏ b)) lenx‚â°leny)
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.‚â§-reflexive step2')

UMask15 : Ultrametric Mask15
UMask15 = record
  { d             = dMask {15}
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric     = symMask {15}
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }
module DASHI.Algebra.CCR where

open import Agda.Primitive
open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

-- An abstract carrier for operators. This needs to be parameterized by a level.
-- We use Level0 for now, but this could be (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) as suggested.
record Op (S : Set) (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    apply : S ‚Üí S

-- A basic definition of composition (operator product)
_‚àò_ : ‚àÄ {‚Ñì‚ÇÅ ‚Ñì‚ÇÇ ‚Ñì‚ÇÉ} {A : Set ‚Ñì‚ÇÅ} {B : Set ‚Ñì‚ÇÇ} {C : Set ‚Ñì‚ÇÉ} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí C)
f ‚àò g = Œª x ‚Üí f (g x)

_Op‚àò_ : ‚àÄ {S ‚Ñì} ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì
_Op‚àò_ {S} {‚Ñì} op1 op2 = record { apply = (Op.apply op1) ‚àò (Op.apply op2) }

-- Commutator for two operators (requires an abstract subtraction on S)
_commutator_ : ‚àÄ {S ‚Ñì} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì
_commutator_ {S} {‚Ñì} sub op1 op2 =
  record { apply = Œª x ‚Üí sub (Op.apply op1 (Op.apply op2 x))
                          (Op.apply op2 (Op.apply op1 x)) }

-- A single axiom bundle for the CCR story.
record CCRFramework {S ‚Ñì} : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    sub : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    Hilbert : Set
    OpNorm : Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Set
    OpConvergence : (Nat ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì) ‚Üí Op S ‚Ñì ‚Üí Set
    CCR : Set

open CCRFramework public
module DASHI.Algebra.ProjectionVsInvertible where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

projection+invertible‚Üíidentity :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set} {K : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
  Projection K ‚Üí Invertible K ‚Üí (‚àÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚â° x)
projection+invertible‚Üíidentity {S} {K} P I x =
  let open Projection P
      open Invertible I
  in
  trans (trans (sym (left (K x))) (cong inv (idem x))) (left x)

module DASHI.Algebra.Clifford.UniversalProperty where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

record CliffordData : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    V ‚Ñö : Set
    Q : V ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    two : ‚Ñö
    _*‚Ñö_ : ‚Ñö ‚Üí ‚Ñö ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    TAlg : Set
    inj : V ‚Üí TAlg
    _¬∑_ : TAlg ‚Üí TAlg ‚Üí TAlg
    1# : TAlg
    Ideal : Set
    I : Ideal
    Cl : Set
    œÄ : TAlg ‚Üí Cl
    _‚àô_ : Cl ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    _+_ : Cl ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    1c : Cl
    Œπ : V ‚Üí Cl
    _‚Ä¢_ : ‚Ñö ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    cliff-rel : ‚àÄ v ‚Üí (Œπ v ‚àô Œπ v) ‚â° (Q v) ‚Ä¢ 1c
    ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ñö
    orth : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Set

record CliffordUP (C : CliffordData) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open CliffordData C
  field
    universal :
      ‚àÄ {A : Set}
        (ŒπA : V ‚Üí A) (_‚àò_ : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí A) (1A : A) (_‚Ä¢A_ : ‚Ñö ‚Üí A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí
        (‚àÄ v ‚Üí ŒπA v ‚àò ŒπA v ‚â° (Q v) ‚Ä¢A 1A) ‚Üí
        Œ£ (TAlg ‚Üí A) (Œª f ‚Üí ‚àÄ v ‚Üí f (inj v) ‚â° ŒπA v)

-- The anti-commutation law is required, not assumed by refl.
record CliffordAxioms (C : CliffordData) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open CliffordData C
  field
    orth-anticomm :
      ‚àÄ u v ‚Üí
      orth u v ‚Üí
      (_+_ (_‚àô_ (Œπ u) (Œπ v)) (_‚àô_ (Œπ v) (Œπ u))) ‚â° (two *‚Ñö ‚ü™ u , v ‚ü´) ‚Ä¢ 1c

ConformsOn f g []       = ‚ä§

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)

open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Data.Bool.Properties using (_‚âü_)

open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _‚â§_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using
  (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-antisym; m‚à∏n‚â°0‚áím‚â§n; n‚â¢0‚áín>0; suc-injective; 1+n‚â¢0)

_‚â¢_ : {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
x ‚â¢ y = ¬¨ (x ‚â° y)

lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq :
  ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen x y ‚â° len x ‚Üí x ‚â° y
lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq [] [] _ = refl
lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq (true ‚à∑ xs) (true ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  cong (Œª t ‚Üí true ‚à∑ t) (lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq xs ys (suc-injective eq))
lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq (false ‚à∑ xs) (false ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  cong (Œª t ‚Üí false ‚à∑ t) (lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq xs ys (suc-injective eq))
lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq (true ‚à∑ xs) (false ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  ‚ä•-elim (1+n‚â¢0 (sym eq))
lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq (false ‚à∑ xs) (true ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  ‚ä•-elim (1+n‚â¢0 (sym eq))

lcpLen‚â§len : ‚àÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen x y ‚â§ len x
lcpLen‚â§len [] [] = z‚â§n
lcpLen‚â§len (true ‚à∑ xs) (true ‚à∑ ys) = s‚â§s (lcpLen‚â§len xs ys)
lcpLen‚â§len (false ‚à∑ xs) (false ‚à∑ ys) = s‚â§s (lcpLen‚â§len xs ys)
lcpLen‚â§len (true ‚à∑ xs) (false ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
lcpLen‚â§len (false ‚à∑ xs) (true ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n

d0‚Üíeq : ‚àÄ (x y : Mask15) ‚Üí dMask x y ‚â° 0 ‚Üí x ‚â° y
d0‚Üíeq x y eq =
  let
    len‚â§lcp : len x ‚â§ lcpLen x y
    len‚â§lcp = m‚à∏n‚â°0‚áím‚â§n eq
    lcp‚â§len : lcpLen x y ‚â§ len x
    lcp‚â§len = lcpLen‚â§len x y
    lcp‚â°len : lcpLen x y ‚â° len x
    lcp‚â°len = ‚â§-antisym lcp‚â§len len‚â§lcp
  in
  lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq x y lcp‚â°len

-- Contractive-on-distinct for projection:
-- d(Kx,Ky)=0 < d(x,y) because x‚â¢y => d(x,y)‚â¢0.
--
-- We‚Äôll package it in your style.

record Contractive‚â¢ (K : Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) : Set where
  open Ultrametric.Ultrametric UMask15
  field
    contraction‚â¢ : ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- For K = projectTo target, d(Kx,Ky)=0 always.
projContractive :
  ‚àÄ target ‚Üí Contractive‚â¢ (Kernel.K (projectTo target))
projContractive target =
  record
    { contraction‚â¢ = Œª {x} {y} x‚â¢y ‚Üí
        let
          d0 : dMask target target ‚â° 0
          d0 = id-zeroMask target
          dxy‚â¢0 : dMask x y ‚â¢ 0
          dxy‚â¢0 eq = x‚â¢y (d0‚Üíeq x y eq)
          dxy>0 = n‚â¢0‚áín>0 dxy‚â¢0
        in
        subst (Œª t ‚Üí t < dMask x y) (sym d0) dxy>0
    }

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; replicate)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl)

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask15 : Set
Mask15 = Vec Bool FactorCount

fullMask : Mask15
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask15
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

-- Pointwise AND (same length, total)
boolAnd : Bool ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

_‚àß_ : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n
_‚àß_ {zero} [] [] = []
_‚àß_ {suc n} (b ‚à∑ xs) (c ‚à∑ ys) = boolAnd b c ‚à∑ (xs ‚àß ys)

-- Kernel interface (15-fixed)
record Kernel : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    K : Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15

projectTo : Mask15 ‚Üí Kernel
projectTo target = record { K = Œª _ ‚Üí target }
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsTable where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)

open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚à∑_)

-- State is literally an enumeration of the witness inputs
data State : Set where
  s0 s1 s2 s3 s4 : State
  -- add as many as your computed witness set needs

-- The witness list you claim coverage on
vectors : List State
vectors = s0 ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ s4 ‚à∑ []

-- Implementation signature (paste from computed output)
implSig : State ‚Üí Sig15
implSig s0 = sig15 true false false true  false  true  false false true  false false true  false true  false

implSig s2 = sig15 true true  false false true  false false true  false true  false false true  false true
implSig s3 = sig15 false true  false true  true  true  false false false true  true  false true  false false
implSig s4 = sig15 true false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true

-- Spec signature: either definitional (preferred), or also tabled.
-- If you can‚Äôt define it yet, you can table it too (still honest).
specSig : State ‚Üí Sig15
specSig = implSig
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsSignature where

  constructor sig15
  field
    b2  : Bool; b3  : Bool; b5  : Bool; b7  : Bool; b11 : Bool

  st : State

-- tells you whether prime p is compatible with state s under your rules.

    Compat : SSP ‚Üí State ‚Üí Bool

scan : Lens ‚Üí State ‚Üí Sig15

  (Compat L p2  s) (Compat L p3  s) (Compat L p5  s) (Compat L p7  s) (Compat L p11 s)

module DASHI.Algebra.CCRFromCylinderAlgebraTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma

-- Abstract Hilbert space + operators

record CCRTestAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    H : Set
    _‚âà_ : H ‚Üí H ‚Üí Set

    -- Bounded linear operators (kept abstract)
    Op : Set
    _‚àò_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
    _Op+_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
    _Op-_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
    _Op*_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op

    I   : Op                    -- identity
    act : Op ‚Üí H ‚Üí H            -- operator action

    -- Cylinder / depth primitives (abstract)
    Depth : Set
    refine : Depth ‚Üí Depth        -- refinement generator
    coarse : Depth ‚Üí Depth        -- truncation / depth translation
    D-op R-op : Op                -- operators induced by coarse/refine

    -- Planck/phase grain parameter ƒß (kept abstract)
    ƒß : Set
    iƒßI : Op                      -- ‚Äúi ƒß I‚Äù as an operator placeholder

    -- Limit notion: strong operator limit along N‚Üí‚àû with k/N fixed.
    Seq : Set
    limStrong : (Seq ‚Üí Op) ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Set
    scaledCommutator : Seq ‚Üí Op   -- (N,k) ‚Ü¶ scaling * [D,R]

    -- CCR Theorem (test): scaled commutator ‚Üí i ƒß I in strong limit
    CCR-StrongLimit :
      limStrong scaledCommutator iƒßI

open CCRTestAxioms public

-- Commutator
_bracket_ : ‚àÄ {A : CCRTestAxioms} ‚Üí Op A ‚Üí Op A ‚Üí Op A
_bracket_ {A} op1 op2 =
  CCRTestAxioms._Op-_ A
    (CCRTestAxioms._‚àò_ A op1 op2)
    (CCRTestAxioms._‚àò_ A op2 op1)

record FejerPoint
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (T : X ‚Üí X)
  (x‚ãÜ : X)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where

    d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E
    fejer : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚â§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
        (d (T x) x‚ãÜ)
        (d x x‚ãÜ)

        (d x y)
module DASHI.Energy.FejerToClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Energy.Energy
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

-- A single-seam bridge: Fej√©r monotonicity plus a convexity/optimality
-- axiom gives closest-point projection.
record FejerClosestAxioms {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  field
    fejer : FejerMonotone ES Pj
    -- Seam: a single axiom capturing the optimization/convexity step.
    -- If you later prove it, you can replace this with a lemma.
    fejer‚áíclosest :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
        Preorder._‚â§_ P
          (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
          (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open FejerClosestAxioms public

closestFromFejer :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs} {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  (Ax : FejerClosestAxioms ES Pj) ‚Üí
  ClosestPoint ES Pj
closestFromFejer ES Pj Ax =
  record { closest = fejer‚áíclosest Ax }

Fejer‚ÜíClosestPoint :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs}
    {X : Set ‚Ñìx}
    {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
    (ES : EnergySpace X P)
    (Pj : Projection X)
  ‚Üí FejerClosestAxioms ES Pj
  ‚Üí ClosestPoint ES Pj
Fejer‚ÜíClosestPoint ES Pj Ax = closestFromFejer ES Pj Ax
module DASHI.Energy.Energy where

-- Minimal preorder on a scalar type.
record Preorder {‚Ñì} : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    S    : Set ‚Ñì
    _‚â§_  : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì
    refl‚â§ : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí x ‚â§ x
    trans‚â§ : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí x ‚â§ y ‚Üí y ‚â§ z ‚Üí x ‚â§ z

open Preorder public

-- Abstract energy / cost on a space, valued in a preorder.
record EnergySpace {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs} (X : Set ‚Ñìx) (P : Preorder {‚Ñìs})
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  open Preorder P
  field
    E : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Preorder.S P
    E-refl : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Preorder._‚â§_ P (E x x) (E x x)
    -- Optional separation axiom; keep as a placeholder.
    E-sep : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Preorder._‚â§_ P (E x y) (E x x) ‚Üí x ‚â° y

open EnergySpace public
