open import DASHI.Energy.Energy

record Projection {‚Ñìx} (X : Set ‚Ñìx) : Set (suc ‚Ñìx) where
  field
    P : X ‚Üí X
    idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x

open Projection public

FixP : ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx} {X : Set ‚Ñìx} ‚Üí Projection X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìx
FixP {X = X} Pj x = Projection.P Pj x ‚â° x

-- Fej√©r monotonicity w.r.t. FixP in an energy space.
-- Interpretation: the dynamics is contractive toward a fixed set, even when
-- raw Euclidean metrics are not contractive (empirically observed for LHC fits).
record FejerMonotone {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    fejer : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚â§_ P (EnergySpace.E ES (Projection.P Pj x) y)
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open FejerMonotone public

-- Closest-point property to FixP.
record ClosestPoint {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    closest : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚â§_ P (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open ClosestPoint public

-- Bridge: Fej√©r + idempotence ‚áí ClosestPoint.
-- This is the exact hinge lemma you‚Äôll later discharge from your operator facts.
record FejerImpliesClosest {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {P : Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  (F : FejerMonotone ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs)) where
  field
    proof : ClosestPoint ES Pj

open FejerImpliesClosest public
module DASHI.Energy.FejerToClosestPointCore where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äî_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)
open import DASHI.Energy.Core
open import DASHI.Energy.Fejer

record Projection {‚Ñì} (X : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    P : X ‚Üí X
    idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x

Fix : ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {X : Set ‚Ñì} ‚Üí Projection X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì
Fix Pr y = Projection.P Pr y ‚â° y

record ClosestPoint
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (Pr : Projection X)
  (d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  field
    best : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Fix Pr y ‚Üí Preorder._‚â§_ (EnergySpace.P ES) (d x (Projection.P Pr x)) (d x y)

record FejerSetClosestAxioms
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (Pr : Projection X)
  (d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  field
    fejer : FejerSet ES (Projection.P Pr) (Fix Pr)
    fejer‚áíclosest :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí Fix Pr y ‚Üí
        Preorder._‚â§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
          (d x (Projection.P Pr x))
          (d x y)

open FejerSetClosestAxioms public

FejerSet‚ÜíClosestPoint :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
    {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
    (ES : EnergySpace X E)
    (Pr : Projection X)
    (d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E)
  ‚Üí FejerSetClosestAxioms ES Pr d
  ‚Üí ClosestPoint ES Pr d
FejerSet‚ÜíClosestPoint ES Pr d Ax =
  record { best = fejer‚áíclosest Ax }

-- 0. Primitive carriers

data T : Set where
  neg : T   -- -1
  zer : T   --  0
  pos : T   -- +1

Œπ : T ‚Üí T
Œπ neg = pos
Œπ zer = zer
Œπ pos = neg

Œπ-involutive : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Œπ (Œπ x) ‚â° x
Œπ-involutive neg = refl
Œπ-involutive zer = refl
Œπ-involutive pos = refl

-- 1. Causal substrate: poset / causal set

record Poset (E : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    _‚â∫_     : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí Set
    -- minimal poset axioms
    irrefl  : ‚àÄ {a} ‚Üí ¬¨ (a ‚â∫ a)
    trans   : ‚àÄ {a b c} ‚Üí a ‚â∫ b ‚Üí b ‚â∫ c ‚Üí a ‚â∫ c
    -- you may want antisymmetry if you use ‚â§, or keep it a strict order

-- Local finiteness etc can be added as fields/axioms if used.

-- 2. Chain/antichain geometry

-- Abstract ‚Äúcounting‚Äù observables; you can later define them concretely
-- (e.g. longest chain length and minimal separating antichain size).

record ChainAntichain {E : Set} (P : Poset E) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open Poset P
  field
    œÑ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚Ñï          -- chain depth
    œÉ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚Ñï          -- antichain width / separation width

    -- Axioms you claim proven elsewhere:
    œÑ-zero : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí œÑ a a ‚â° 0
    œÉ-zero : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí œÉ a a ‚â° 0

    -- Causal direction uniqueness / ‚Äúone time axis‚Äù property, etc.
    -- (whatever your signature proof uses)
    causal-axis : Set

    c : ‚Ñù  -- you may have your own ‚Ñù
    Œîs¬≤ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚Ñù

      ‚àÄ a b ‚Üí
      Œîs¬≤ a b ‚â°
        ((c *‚Ñù c) *‚Ñù (to‚Ñù (œÑ a b) *‚Ñù to‚Ñù (œÑ a b)))
        -‚Ñù
        (to‚Ñù (œÉ a b) *‚Ñù to‚Ñù (œÉ a b))

record Ultrametric (X : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    d    : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí ‚Ñù
    -- ultrametric axioms
    d0   : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí d x x ‚â° to‚Ñù 0
    sym  : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚â° d y x
    ultra : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí d x z ‚â§‚Ñù max‚Ñù (d x y) (d y z)

  field
    lambda    : ‚Ñù
    lambdaLt1 : lambda <‚Ñù to‚Ñù 1
    contr : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      _‚â§‚Ñù_ ((Ultrametric.d M) (F x) (F y))
          (_*‚Ñù_ lambda ((Ultrametric.d M) x y))

  field
    x* : X
    fp : F x* ‚â° x*

-- Theorems (stubs)

  (C : Contractive M F) : Set‚ÇÅ where

  ‚àÄ {X : Set} (M : Ultrametric X) (F : X ‚Üí X) ‚Üí
  Contractive M F ‚Üí
  Set‚ÇÅ

module DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; subst; sym)

-- Minimal ordered commutative monoid interface.
record AddMonoid {‚Ñì} : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    N   : Set ‚Ñì
    _+_ : N ‚Üí N ‚Üí N
    0#  : N

open AddMonoid public

record OrderedMonoid {‚Ñì} : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    M    : AddMonoid {‚Ñì}
    _‚â§_  : N M ‚Üí N M ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì
    refl‚â§  : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí x ‚â§ x
    trans‚â§ : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí x ‚â§ y ‚Üí y ‚â§ z ‚Üí x ‚â§ z
    mono+  : ‚àÄ a b c d ‚Üí a ‚â§ b ‚Üí c ‚â§ d ‚Üí
      _‚â§_ (AddMonoid._+_ M a c) (AddMonoid._+_ M b d)

open OrderedMonoid public

record MDLParts {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìn}
  (X : Set ‚Ñìx) (O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ñìn})
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìn)) where
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    P D T : X ‚Üí X
    ModelLen ResidLen : X ‚Üí AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL : X ‚Üí AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL-def : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí MDL x ‚â° AddMonoid._+_ (M O) (ModelLen (P x)) (ResidLen (D x))

open MDLParts public

record TradeoffLemma {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìn}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ñìn}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìn)) where
  open OrderedMonoid O
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    model-drop : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
    resid-drop : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))

open TradeoffLemma public

-- Descent theorem from the single tradeoff seam.
--
-- Empirical learning (LHC harness): monotone descent holds strongly for
-- L1/MDL-proxy energies even when raw œá¬≤ is non-contractive. This matches
-- the intended geometry: Fej√©r/closest-point descent to a fixed set,
-- not global Euclidean contraction. Keep the seam here; do not assume
-- strict contraction in the raw metric.
MDLDescent :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìn} {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ñìn}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  (L : TradeoffLemma Parts)
  ‚Üí ‚àÄ x ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O (MDL Parts (T Parts x)) (MDL Parts x)
MDLDescent {O = O} Parts L x =
  let
    open OrderedMonoid O
    open AddMonoid (M O)
    open TradeoffLemma L
    mdlt : MDL Parts (T Parts x) ‚â°
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
    mdlt = MDL-def Parts (T Parts x)
    mdlx : MDL Parts x ‚â°
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
    mdlx = MDL-def Parts x
    step : OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x)))
    step = OrderedMonoid.mono+ O
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
      (TradeoffLemma.model-drop L x)
      (TradeoffLemma.resid-drop L x)
  in
  subst
    (Œª v ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O v (MDL Parts x))
    (sym mdlt)
    (subst
      (Œª v ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O
        (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
          (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
          (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
        v)
      (sym mdlx)
      step)

record MDLFunctional (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where

    model residual : S ‚Üí Nat
    mdl : S ‚Üí Nat
    mdl‚â° : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí mdl s ‚â° model s + residual s

    decreases : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí MDLFunctional.mdl M (T s) ‚â§ MDLFunctional.mdl M s
    strictUnlessFixed : Set

module DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentProof where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äî_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)
open import DASHI.Energy.Core
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

record MDL {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe} (X : Set ‚Ñìx) (E : Set ‚Ñìe) : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  field
    mdl : X ‚Üí E

record AddOps {‚Ñì} (X : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X

record AddOpsE {‚Ñì} (E : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    _+E_ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí E

record MDLSplit
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
  (Pr : Projection X)
  (Ops : AddOps X)
  (OpsE : AddOpsE E)
  (M : MDL X E)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  open AddOps Ops
  open AddOpsE OpsE
  field
    model : X ‚Üí E
    resid : X ‚Üí E
    split : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí MDL.mdl M x ‚â° model (Projection.P Pr x) +E resid (x - Projection.P Pr x)

record Descent
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx} {E : Set ‚Ñìe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (T : X ‚Üí X)
  (M : MDL X E)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  field
    descent : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚â§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
        (MDL.mdl M (T x))
        (MDL.mdl M x)

module DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentProofShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; z‚â§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-trans)

import DASHI.Energy.Core as EC
open import DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentProof as MDP
open import DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff as MDT using (MDLParts)
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLDescentShiftInstance as MDSI
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC

-- Preorder on Nat (for EnergySpace).
preorderNat : EC.Preorder Nat
preorderNat =
  record
    { _‚â§_ = _‚â§_
    ; refl = Œª _ ‚Üí ‚â§-refl
    ; trans = Œª x‚â§y y‚â§z ‚Üí ‚â§-trans x‚â§y y‚â§z
    }

energyNat : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí EC.EnergySpace (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) Nat
energyNat {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = preorderNat
    ; energy = MDT.MDLParts.MDL (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k})
    }

mdlNat : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDP.MDL (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) Nat
mdlNat {m} {k} =
  record { mdl = MDT.MDLParts.MDL (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}) }

-- Concrete MDL descent proof using the shift tradeoff lemma.
descentShift :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  MDP.Descent
    (energyNat {m} {k})
    (MDT.MDLParts.T (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}))
    (mdlNat {m} {k})
descentShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { descent = MDSI.mdlyapShift {m} {k}
    }

module DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat as Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Contraction using (_‚â¢_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _‚â§_; _‚â•_; _‚à∏_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; map; _++_; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _‚à∑ ≥_; cast; init; last; initLast)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-injective; reverse-‚à∑; reverse-++; cast-is-id; cast-sym)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos; inv)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

cong‚ÇÇ : ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} {x‚ÇÅ x‚ÇÇ : A} {y‚ÇÅ y‚ÇÇ : B}
        (g : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí
        x‚ÇÅ ‚â° x‚ÇÇ ‚Üí y‚ÇÅ ‚â° y‚ÇÇ ‚Üí g x‚ÇÅ y‚ÇÅ ‚â° g x‚ÇÇ y‚ÇÇ
cong‚ÇÇ g refl refl = refl

-- Fine agreement metric: use agreement depth on reversed vectors (suffix agreement).
agreeDepthFine : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
agreeDepthFine x y = AM.agreeDepth (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
dNatFine x y = AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine-inv :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚â° dNatFine x y
dNatFine-inv x y =
  let
    rx = reverse x
    ry = reverse y
    rx-inv : reverse (map inv x) ‚â° map inv rx
    rx-inv = sym (map-reverse inv x)
    ry-inv : reverse (map inv y) ‚â° map inv ry
    ry-inv = sym (map-reverse inv y)
  in
  trans
    (cong (Œª a ‚Üí AM.dNat a (reverse (map inv y))) rx-inv)
    (trans
      (cong (Œª b ‚Üí AM.dNat (map inv rx) b) ry-inv)
      (AM.dNat-inv rx ry)
    )

reverse‚â¢ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí reverse x ‚â¢ reverse y
reverse‚â¢ x‚â¢y rev‚â° = x‚â¢y (reverse-injective rev‚â°)

dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNatFine x y ‚â° 0 ‚Üí x ‚â° y
dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq x y d‚â°0 =
  reverse-injective (AM.dNat-zero‚Üíeq (reverse x) (reverse y) d‚â°0)

dNatFine-positive :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí 0 < dNatFine x y
dNatFine-positive x‚â¢y = AM.dNat-positive (reverse‚â¢ x‚â¢y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement-depth monotonicity under pointwise maps

agreeDepth-map‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth x y ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (map f x) (map f y)
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} f [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) with f neg
... | neg = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) with f zer
... | neg = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) with f pos
... | neg = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚â§s (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (neg ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (neg ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (zer ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (zer ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (pos ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-map‚â§ {suc n} f (pos ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n

dNatFine-map‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map f x) (map f y) ‚â§ dNatFine x y
dNatFine-map‚â§ {n} f x y =
  let
    rx-map : reverse (map f x) ‚â° map f (reverse x)
    rx-map = sym (map-reverse f x)
    ry-map : reverse (map f y) ‚â° map f (reverse y)
    ry-map = sym (map-reverse f y)
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse x)) (map f (reverse y)) ‚â§ AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)
    step = NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ n (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f (reverse x) (reverse y))
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans
    (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (cong‚ÇÇ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map))
    step

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement depth for append (prefix metric on reverse)

agreeDepth-++‚â• :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit m) (c : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ++ c) (b ++ c) ‚â• AM.agreeDepth a b
agreeDepth-++‚â• {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) c =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++‚â• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) c =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++‚â• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) c =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++‚â• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++‚â• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) c = z‚â§n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Reverse of snoc: reverse (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a) = a ‚à∑ reverse xs

reverse-‚à∑ ≥ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  reverse (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a) ‚â° a ‚à∑ reverse xs
reverse-‚à∑ ≥ [] a = reverse-‚à∑ a []
reverse-‚à∑ ≥ (x ‚à∑ xs) a
  rewrite reverse-‚à∑ x (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a)
        | reverse-‚à∑ ≥ xs a
        | reverse-‚à∑ x xs
  = refl

agreeDepth-cast :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (eq : m ‚â° n) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (cast eq x) (cast eq y) ‚â° AM.agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

dNat-cast :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (eq : m ‚â° n) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  AM.dNat (cast eq x) (cast eq y) ‚â° AM.dNat x y
dNat-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ShiftTail monotonicity on fine agreement

agreeDepth-++-mono :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (u v u' v' : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth u v ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth u' v' ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (u' ++ p) (v' ++ q)
agreeDepth-++-mono {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] [] [] p q h = NatP.‚â§-refl
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) (neg ‚à∑ us') (neg ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) (zer ‚à∑ us') (zer ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) (pos ‚à∑ us') (pos ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) (neg ‚à∑ us') (neg ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) (zer ‚à∑ us') (zer ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) (pos ‚à∑ us') (pos ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) (neg ‚à∑ us') (neg ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) (zer ‚à∑ us') (zer ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) (pos ‚à∑ us') (pos ‚à∑ vs') p q (s‚â§s h‚â§) =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚â§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚â§n

agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (u v : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (u ++ map f p) (v ++ map f q)
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] p q f = agreeDepth-map‚â§ f p q
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚à∑ us) (pos ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (neg ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚à∑ us) (zer ‚à∑ vs) p q f = z‚â§n

agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit n) (x y : Trit) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ‚à∑ ≥ x) (b ‚à∑ ≥ y) ‚â§ suc (AM.agreeDepth a b)
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg neg = s‚â§s z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer zer = s‚â§s z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos pos = s‚â§s z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg zer = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg pos = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer neg = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer pos = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos neg = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos zer = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) x y =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) x y =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) x y =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (neg ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (zer ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ {suc n} (pos ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) x y = z‚â§n

agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (a b : Trit) (as bs : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ‚à∑ as) (b ‚à∑ bs) ‚â§ suc (AM.agreeDepth as bs)
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ neg neg as bs = s‚â§s NatP.‚â§-refl
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ zer zer as bs = s‚â§s NatP.‚â§-refl
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ pos pos as bs = s‚â§s NatP.‚â§-refl
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ neg zer as bs = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ neg pos as bs = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ zer neg as bs = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ zer pos as bs = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ pos neg as bs = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ pos zer as bs = z‚â§n

agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚â• :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 ‚â§ agreeDepthFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚â• {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚â• {suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  NatP.‚â§-trans
    (subst
      (Œª v ‚Üí v ‚â§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys)))
      (sym lhs1)
      (agreeDepth-‚à∑ ≥‚â§ (reverse xs) (reverse ys) x y))
    (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym lhs))
  where
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)
           ‚â° AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs ‚à∑ ≥ x) (reverse ys ‚à∑ ≥ y)
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-‚à∑ x xs | reverse-‚à∑ y ys = refl
    lhs : AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (x ‚à∑ xs)))
                        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (y ‚à∑ ys)))
          ‚â° suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys))
    lhs rewrite reverse-‚à∑ ≥ xs zer | reverse-‚à∑ ≥ ys zer = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for shiftTail (tail-only)

dNatFine-shiftTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2) ‚â§ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-shiftTail‚â§ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ k (agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚â• t1 t2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for projTail (tail-only)

agreeDepthFine-projTail‚â• :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 ‚â§ agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-projTail‚â• {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepthFine-projTail‚â• {k = Nat.suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  NatP.‚â§-trans bound (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym (trans r1 r2)))
  where
    init-‚à∑ ≥-last : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí init t ‚à∑ ≥ last t ‚â° t
    init-‚à∑ ≥-last t with initLast t
    ... | ys , y , eq = sym eq

    reverse-init-last :
      ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí
      reverse t ‚â° last t ‚à∑ reverse (init t)
    reverse-init-last t =
      trans
        (cong reverse (sym (init-‚à∑ ≥-last t)))
        (reverse-‚à∑ ≥ (init t) (last t))

    r1 : agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail (x ‚à∑ xs)) (TCP.projTail (y ‚à∑ ys))
         ‚â° AM.agreeDepth (zer ‚à∑ reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (zer ‚à∑ reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys)))
    r1 rewrite reverse-‚à∑ ≥ (init (x ‚à∑ xs)) zer | reverse-‚à∑ ≥ (init (y ‚à∑ ys)) zer = refl

    r2 : AM.agreeDepth (zer ‚à∑ reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (zer ‚à∑ reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys)))
         ‚â° suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys))))
    r2 = refl
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)
           ‚â° AM.agreeDepth (last (x ‚à∑ xs) ‚à∑ reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs)))
                           (last (y ‚à∑ ys) ‚à∑ reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys)))
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-init-last (x ‚à∑ xs)
                | reverse-init-last (y ‚à∑ ys)
      = refl
    bound :
      agreeDepthFine (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)
      ‚â§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys))))
    bound =
      subst
        (Œª v ‚Üí v ‚â§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys)))))
        (sym lhs1)
        (agreeDepth-‚à∑‚â§ (last (x ‚à∑ xs)) (last (y ‚à∑ ys))
                       (reverse (init (x ‚à∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚à∑ ys))))

dNatFine-projTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2) ‚â§ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-projTail‚â§ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ k (agreeDepthFine-projTail‚â• t1 t2)

dNatFine-++ :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚â°
  AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
dNatFine-++ {m} {n} c c' t t' =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚â° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx : reverse (c ++ t) ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c)
    rx = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c t))
    ry : reverse (c' ++ t') ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    ry = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' t'))
  in
  trans
    (cong‚ÇÇ AM.dNat rx ry)
    (dNat-cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c'))

dNatFine-++-map‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map f c ++ t) (map f c' ++ t') ‚â§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-map‚â§ {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚â° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (map f c ++ t) ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse (map f c))
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c) t))
    ry-cast : reverse (map f c' ++ t') ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse (map f c'))
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c') t'))
    rx-map : reverse (map f c ++ t) ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c))))
    ry-map : reverse (map f c' ++ t') ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t' ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c'))))
    step : AM.dNat (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
                   (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
           ‚â§ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ (n + m)
             (agreeDepth-++-map‚â§ (reverse t) (reverse t') (reverse c) (reverse c') f)

    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚â°
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans
    (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (trans (cong‚ÇÇ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.‚â§-trans step (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-map‚â§-tail :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ map f t) (c' ++ map f t') ‚â§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-map‚â§-tail {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚â° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (c ++ map f t) ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c (map f t)))
    ry-cast : reverse (c' ++ map f t') ‚â° cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' (map f t')))
    rx-map : reverse (c ++ map f t) ‚â° cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c) (sym (map-reverse f t))))
    ry-map : reverse (c' ++ map f t') ‚â° cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c') (sym (map-reverse f t'))))
    depth‚â§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                     (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚â§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (map f (reverse t)) (map f (reverse t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepth-map‚â§ f (reverse t) (reverse t'))
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                   (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
           ‚â§ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ (n + m) depth‚â§
    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚â°
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans
    (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (trans (cong‚ÇÇ AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.‚â§-trans step (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.shiftTail t) (c' ++ TCP.shiftTail t') ‚â§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚â§ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.shiftTail t) (TCP.shiftTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depth‚â§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚â§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t)) (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚â• t t')
  in
  NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ (n + m) depth‚â§

dNatFine-++-projTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.projTail t) (c' ++ TCP.projTail t') ‚â§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-projTail‚â§ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.projTail t) (TCP.projTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depth‚â§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚â§ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.projTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.projTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚â§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.projTail t)) (reverse (TCP.projTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-projTail‚â• t t')
  in
  NatP.‚à∏-mono ≥-‚â§ (n + m) depth‚â§

ultrametricVec : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNatFine
    ; id-zero = Œª x ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x)
    ; symmetric = Œª x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y)
    ; ultratriangle = Œª x y z ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y) (reverse z)
    }
module DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_; _‚â•_; _‚äî_; _‚äì_; _‚à∏_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Sum using (inj‚ÇÅ; inj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; map)
open import Contraction using (_‚â¢_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (inv)

-- Agreement depth (longest common prefix) for Vec Trit n.
agreeDepth : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
agreeDepth [] [] = zero
agreeDepth (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth _ _ = zero

-- Distance: reversed depth.
dNat : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
dNat {n} x y = n ‚à∏ agreeDepth x y

agreeDepth-self : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x x ‚â° n
agreeDepth-self [] = refl
agreeDepth-self (neg ‚à∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (zer ‚à∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (pos ‚à∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl

agreeDepth-sym : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚â° agreeDepth y x
agreeDepth-sym [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = refl

agreeDepth-inv :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  agreeDepth (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚â° agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-inv [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = refl

dNat-inv :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNat (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚â° dNat x y
dNat-inv {n} x y = cong (Œª k ‚Üí n ‚à∏ k) (agreeDepth-inv x y)

agreeDepth‚â§n : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚â§ n
agreeDepth‚â§n [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = s‚â§s (agreeDepth‚â§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚â§n (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = s‚â§s (agreeDepth‚â§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚â§n (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = s‚â§s (agreeDepth‚â§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚â§n (neg ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (neg ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (zer ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (zer ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (pos ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n
agreeDepth‚â§n (pos ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) = z‚â§n

agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚â° n ‚Üí x ‚â° y
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq [] [] _ = refl
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  cong (neg ‚à∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  cong (zer ‚à∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) eq =
  cong (pos ‚à∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚à∑ xs) (pos ‚à∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚à∑ xs) (neg ‚à∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚à∑ xs) (zer ‚à∑ ys) ()

dNat-zero‚Üíeq : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNat x y ‚â° 0 ‚Üí x ‚â° y
dNat-zero‚Üíeq {n} x y d‚â°0 =
  let
    depth‚â• : n ‚â§ agreeDepth x y
    depth‚â• = NatP.m‚à∏n‚â°0‚áím‚â§n d‚â°0
    depth‚â§ : agreeDepth x y ‚â§ n
    depth‚â§ = agreeDepth‚â§n x y
    depth‚â° : agreeDepth x y ‚â° n
    depth‚â° = NatP.‚â§-antisym depth‚â§ depth‚â•
  in
  agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq x y depth‚â°

dNat-nonzero : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚â¢ 0
dNat-nonzero x‚â¢y d‚â°0 = x‚â¢y (dNat-zero‚Üíeq _ _ d‚â°0)

dNat-positive : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí 0 < dNat x y
dNat-positive x‚â¢y = NatP.n‚â¢0‚áín>0 (dNat-nonzero x‚â¢y)

-- Strong triangle inequality for agreement depth (prefix metric).
agreeDepth-triangle :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  (agreeDepth x y ‚äì agreeDepth y z) ‚â§ agreeDepth x z
agreeDepth-triangle [] [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepth-triangle (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) (z ‚à∑ zs) with x | y | z
... | neg | neg | neg =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | zer | zer | zer =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | pos | pos | pos =
  s‚â§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | neg | neg | zer = z‚â§n
... | neg | neg | pos = z‚â§n
... | zer | zer | neg = z‚â§n
... | zer | zer | pos = z‚â§n
... | pos | pos | neg = z‚â§n
... | pos | pos | zer = z‚â§n
... | neg | zer | _ = z‚â§n
... | neg | pos | _ = z‚â§n
... | zer | neg | _ = z‚â§n
... | zer | pos | _ = z‚â§n
... | pos | neg | _ = z‚â§n
... | pos | zer | _ = z‚â§n

-- Ultrametric inequality: d x z ‚â§ max (d x y) (d y z)
ultraNat : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNat x z ‚â§ (dNat x y ‚äî dNat y z)
ultraNat {n} x y z with NatP.‚â§-total (agreeDepth x y) (agreeDepth y z)
... | inj‚ÇÅ xy‚â§yz =
  let
    min‚â° : (agreeDepth x y ‚äì agreeDepth y z) ‚â° agreeDepth x y
    min‚â° = NatP.m‚â§n‚áím‚äìn‚â°m xy‚â§yz
    depth‚â§ : agreeDepth x y ‚â§ agreeDepth x z
    depth‚â§ = NatP.‚â§-trans (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym min‚â°)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depth‚â• : agreeDepth x z ‚â• agreeDepth x y
    depth‚â• = depth‚â§
    step1 : dNat x z ‚â§ dNat x y
    step1 = NatP.‚à∏-mono (NatP.‚â§-refl {n}) depth‚â•
    step2 : dNat x z ‚â§ (dNat x y ‚äî dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.m‚â§m‚äîn (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2
... | inj‚ÇÇ yz‚â§xy =
  let
    min‚â° : (agreeDepth x y ‚äì agreeDepth y z) ‚â° agreeDepth y z
    min‚â° = NatP.m‚â•n‚áím‚äìn‚â°n yz‚â§xy
    depth‚â§ : agreeDepth y z ‚â§ agreeDepth x z
    depth‚â§ = NatP.‚â§-trans (NatP.‚â§-reflexive (sym min‚â°)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depth‚â• : agreeDepth x z ‚â• agreeDepth y z
    depth‚â• = depth‚â§
    step1 : dNat x z ‚â§ dNat y z
    step1 = NatP.‚à∏-mono (NatP.‚â§-refl {n}) depth‚â•
    step2 : dNat x z ‚â§ (dNat x y ‚äî dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.m‚â§n‚äîm (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2

ultrametricVec : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNat
    ; id-zero = Œª x ‚Üí
        trans
          (cong (Œª k ‚Üí n ‚à∏ k) (agreeDepth-self x))
          (NatP.n‚à∏n‚â°0 n)
    ; symmetric = Œª x y ‚Üí
        cong (Œª k ‚Üí n ‚à∏ k) (agreeDepth-sym x y)
    ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
    }
module DASHI.Metric.TernaryUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Ultrametric

open import DASHI.Algebra.BalancedTernary using (Trit; neg; zero; pos)

-- Discrete ultrametric on Trit (honest, non-postulated).
-- d x y = 0 if x ‚â° y, else 1.
dT : Trit ‚Üí Trit ‚Üí Nat
dT neg  neg  = 0
dT zero zero = 0
dT pos  pos  = 0
dT _    _    = suc zero

id-zeroT : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí dT x x ‚â° 0
id-zeroT neg  = refl
id-zeroT zero = refl
id-zeroT pos  = refl

symT : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí dT x y ‚â° dT y x
symT neg  neg  = refl
symT neg  zero = refl
symT neg  pos  = refl
symT zero neg  = refl
symT zero zero = refl
symT zero pos  = refl
symT pos  neg  = refl
symT pos  zero = refl
symT pos  pos  = refl

-- For discrete metric: if x=z then 0 ‚â§ max; otherwise 1 ‚â§ max (since at least
-- one of x‚âÝy or y‚âÝz holds).
ultraT : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí dT x z ‚â§ max (dT x y) (dT y z)
ultraT neg  neg  neg  = z‚â§n
ultraT neg  neg  zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT neg  neg  pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT neg  zero neg  = z‚â§n
ultraT neg  zero zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT neg  zero pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT neg  pos  neg  = z‚â§n
ultraT neg  pos  zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT neg  pos  pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero neg  neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero neg  zero = z‚â§n
ultraT zero neg  pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero zero neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero zero zero = z‚â§n
ultraT zero zero pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero pos  neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT zero pos  zero = z‚â§n
ultraT zero pos  pos  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  neg  neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  neg  zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  neg  pos  = z‚â§n
ultraT pos  zero neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  zero zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  zero pos  = z‚â§n
ultraT pos  pos  neg  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  pos  zero = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultraT pos  pos  pos  = z‚â§n

S : Set
S = Trit

U : Ultrametric S
U = record
  { d             = dT
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroT
  ; symmetric     = symT
  ; ultratriangle = ultraT
  }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.FractranCOL where

open import Data.Nat renaming (‚Ñï to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatProp using
  (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-trans; <-trans; +-mono-‚â§; <-step)
open import Data.Maybe using (Maybe; just; nothing)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State: exponent vector for primes [2,3,5,7,11] (5 lanes)
-- lane 0=2, 1=3, 2=5, 3=7, 4=11

EV5 : Set
EV5 = Vec Nat 5

get : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
get (x ‚à∑ xs) zero    = x
get (x ‚à∑ xs) (suc i) = get xs i
get []       _       = zero

set : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Nat n
set (x ‚à∑ xs) zero    v = v ‚à∑ xs
set (x ‚à∑ xs) (suc i) v = x ‚à∑ set xs i v
set []       _       _ = []

dec1 : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Maybe (Vec Nat n)
dec1 {n} ev i with get ev i
... | zero  = nothing
... | suc m = just (set ev i m)

inc1 : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Nat n
inc1 ev i = set ev i (suc (get ev i))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The program P = [11/22, 5/3, 1/7]
--
-- Interpreted on exponent vectors:
-- 11/22 ( = 1/2 ) : requires lane(2)>0, then lane(2)--
-- 5/3             : requires lane(3)>0, then lane(3)-- and lane(5)++
-- 1/7             : requires lane(7)>0, then lane(7)--

data Rule : Set where
  r1122 r53 r17 : Rule

apply : Rule ‚Üí EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5
apply r1122 ev = dec1 ev 0
apply r53   ev with dec1 ev 1
... | nothing = nothing
... | just e  = just (inc1 e 2)
apply r17   ev = dec1 ev 3

-- First-applicable (deterministic) scan order:
step : EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5
step ev with apply r1122 ev
... | just ev' = just ev'
... | nothing with apply r53 ev
...   | just ev' = just ev'
...   | nothing  = apply r17 ev

Obs : EV5 ‚Üí Set
Obs ev = step ev ‚â° nothing

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Rank / energy: a + b + d where lanes are 2,3,7 (0,1,3)
E : EV5 ‚Üí Nat
E ev = get ev 0 + get ev 1 + get ev 3

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lemmas: each successful rule application decreases E by 1
record FractranAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    E-dec2 : ‚àÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r1122 ev ‚â° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev
    E-dec3 : ‚àÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r53 ev ‚â° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev
    E-dec7 : ‚àÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r17 ev ‚â° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev

    -- Determinism of step (canonical ‚Äúfirst applies‚Äù rule)
    step-deterministic : ‚àÄ {ev x y} ‚Üí step ev ‚â° just x ‚Üí step ev ‚â° just y ‚Üí x ‚â° y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fuelled evaluation: iterate step at most fuel times

iterate : Nat ‚Üí (EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5) ‚Üí EV5 ‚Üí EV5
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x with f x
... | nothing  = x
... | just x'  = iterate n f x'

run : EV5 ‚Üí EV5
run ev = iterate (E ev) step ev

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Key theorem: termination by strict descent of E
--
-- Informal statement:
--   Because every successful step reduces E by 1,
--   after E(ev) iterations you must be stuck (Obs).
--
-- We package it as: step (run ev) = nothing.

record FractranTerminationAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    -- If step makes a move, E strictly decreases.
    step-decreases-E : ‚àÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí step ev ‚â° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev
    termination : ‚àÄ ev ‚Üí Obs (run ev)

open FractranAxioms public
open FractranTerminationAxioms public

x ‚â¢ y = ¬¨ (x ‚â° y)

module DASHI.Combinatorics.Confluence where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude

-- A nondeterministic one-step relation.
Rel : Set ‚Üí Set‚ÇÅ
Rel S = S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

-- Diamond property: if s steps to s1 and s2, they can be joined.
Diamond : ‚àÄ {S} ‚Üí Rel S ‚Üí Set
Diamond {S} step =
  ‚àÄ s s‚ÇÅ s‚ÇÇ ‚Üí
    step s s‚ÇÅ ‚Üí
    step s s‚ÇÇ ‚Üí
    Œ£ S (Œª t ‚Üí step s‚ÇÅ t √ó step s‚ÇÇ t)

-- Church-Rosser / confluence (simple diamond form).
Confluent : ‚àÄ {S} ‚Üí Rel S ‚Üí Set
Confluent = Diamond

    preservesIP :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® U x , U y ‚ü© ‚â° ‚ü® x , y ‚ü©

module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude where

  renaming (‚Ñï to Nat)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; map; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)

add : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
add zero    n = n
add (suc m) n = suc (add m n)

-- 15-lane exponent vector
EV : Set
EV = Vec Nat 15

-- pointwise addition (useful for sufficient statistics)
_‚äû_ : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Vec Nat n
_‚äû_ {zero} [] [] = []
_‚äû_ {suc n} (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) = add x y ‚à∑ (_‚äû_ {n} xs ys)

-- pointwise max (sometimes useful)
max : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
max zero    n       = n
max (suc m) zero    = suc m
max (suc m) (suc n) = suc (max m n)

_‚äîv_ : EV ‚Üí EV ‚Üí EV
_‚äîv_ = zipWith max

sumEV : EV ‚Üí Nat
sumEV = foldr‚Ä≤ add zero

-- A dataset is a list of exponent vectors
DatasetEV : Set
DatasetEV = List EV

stats : DatasetEV ‚Üí EV
stats []       = map (Œª _ ‚Üí 0) (0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ 0 ‚à∑ [])
stats (x ‚à∑ xs) = x ‚äû stats xs
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Generic kernel family

record KernelFamily (I S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    K : I ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    Lkernel : I ‚Üí CodeLength   -- price selecting/specifying that kernel

iterate : ‚àÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trace is ‚Äústate after n steps‚Äù, observed by PDA.

TraceObs :
  ‚àÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí O
TraceObs {I} {S} {O} F P i n s =
  PDA.observe P (iterate {S = S} (KernelFamily.K F i) n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset for kernel selection: initial states + a step index list
-- (keeps it concrete without needing streams).

record KSData (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    inits : List S
    steps : List Nat

-- Flatten observations (cartesian product inits √ó steps)
concat : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
concat [] ys       = ys
concat (x ‚à∑ xs) ys = x ‚à∑ concat xs ys

map2 : ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B ‚Üí List C
map2 f []       _        = []
map2 f (a ‚à∑ as) bs       = concat (map (f a) bs) (map2 f as bs)

ObsDatasetKS :
  ‚àÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí KSData S ‚Üí List O
ObsDatasetKS F P i D =
  map2 (Œª s n ‚Üí TraceObs F P i n s) (KSData.inits D) (KSData.steps D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A model over observations (two-part code)
record ObsModel (O : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    Lmodel : CodeLength
    Ldata| : List O ‚Üí CodeLength

MDLscore :
  ‚àÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  ObsModel O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí KSData S ‚Üí CodeLength
MDLscore F P M i D =
  PDA.costPDA P
  + KernelFamily.Lkernel F i
  + ObsModel.Lmodel M
  + ObsModel.Ldata| M (ObsDatasetKS F P i D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-selection theorem statement: i* is MDL-minimal within the family.
-- (We keep ‚Äúargmin‚Äù as an explicit proof obligation.)

record ArgMin {I S O : Set} (F : KernelFamily I S) (P : PDA S O) (M : ObsModel O)
              (D : KSData S) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    i* : I
    minimal :
      ‚àÄ i ‚Üí
        MDLscore F P M i* D ‚â§ MDLscore F P M i D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Instances where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection

record PDAInstanceAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S : Set
    extractEV : S ‚Üí EV
    shardEV : EV ‚Üí Bucket

open PDAInstanceAxioms public

PDA-EV : (A : PDAInstanceAxioms) ‚Üí PDA (S A) EV
PDA-EV A = record
  { observe = extractEV A
  ; admissible = Œª _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
  ; costPDA = 15  -- price of having this lens; refine later
  }

-- EV model turned into an ObsModel
evObsModel : IndepEVModel ‚Üí ObsModel EV
evObsModel M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel M
  ; Ldata| = Œª obsList ‚Üí  -- interpret obsList as DatasetEV and score it
      let
        D : DatasetEV
        D = obsList
      in
      Ldata| M D
  }

-- CICADA-71 PDA: observe bucket directly from extracted exponent vector
-- (lens includes sharding; price it)
PDA-71 : (A : PDAInstanceAxioms) ‚Üí PDA (S A) Bucket
PDA-71 A = record
  { observe = Œª s ‚Üí shardEV A (extractEV A s)
  ; admissible = Œª _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
  ; costPDA = 71  -- ‚Äúlimit to 71‚Äù lens price placeholder
  }

-- IID71 model turned into an ObsModel
obsModel71 : IID71 ‚Üí ObsModel Bucket
obsModel71 M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel71 M
  ; Ldata| = Œª bs ‚Üí Ldata|71 M (bs)
  }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚à∑_)

Bucket : Set
Bucket = Fin 71

shard : EV ‚Üí Bucket
shard = bucket71-ev

DatasetB : Set
DatasetB = List Bucket

shardDataset : DatasetEV ‚Üí DatasetB
shardDataset []       = []
shardDataset (x ‚à∑ xs) = shard x ‚à∑ shardDataset xs

-- A very concrete bucket code length: constant (baseline)
lenBucket : Bucket ‚Üí CodeLength
lenBucket _ = 7  -- 71 buckets need ~7 bits; use Nat as approximation

lenBuckets : DatasetB ‚Üí CodeLength
lenBuckets []       = zero
lenBuckets (b ‚à∑ bs) = lenBucket b + lenBuckets bs

-- IID bucket model with parameter cost (a table). Keep it simple now.
record IID71 : Set where
  field tableCost : CodeLength

Lmodel71 : IID71 ‚Üí CodeLength
Lmodel71 M = IID71.tableCost M

Ldata|71 : IID71 ‚Üí DatasetB ‚Üí CodeLength
Ldata|71 M D = lenBuckets D  -- replace with -log p(b) once you encode probs

MDL71 : IID71 ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
MDL71 M D = Lmodel71 M + Ldata|71 M (shardDataset D)
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude

record PDA (World Obs : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    observe : World ‚Üí Obs
    admissible : World ‚Üí Set   -- witness/guard: which worlds are in scope
    costPDA : CodeLength       -- price the lens/witness (anti-cheat)

-- Apply PDA to a dataset (list of worlds)
WorldDataset : Set ‚Üí Set
WorldDataset W = List W

ObsDataset : Set ‚Üí Set
ObsDataset O = List O

map : ‚àÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
map f []       = []
map f (x ‚à∑ xs) = f x ‚à∑ map f xs

observeAll : ‚àÄ {W O} ‚Üí PDA W O ‚Üí WorldDataset W ‚Üí ObsDataset O
observeAll P D = map (PDA.observe P) D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤; map)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Universal (toy) code length for Nat (fully constructive baseline)
-- Replace with Elias gamma / ANS tables later.

lenNat : Nat ‚Üí CodeLength
lenNat n = suc n  -- unary length: 1 + n (baseline, simple)

lenEV : EV ‚Üí CodeLength
lenEV = foldr‚Ä≤ (Œª e acc ‚Üí lenNat e + acc) zero

lenDataset : DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
lenDataset []       = zero
lenDataset (x ‚à∑ xs) = lenEV x + lenDataset xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Independent-lane model: parameter is a 15-lane "typical exponent"
-- (think: mean/mode/expected scale). You can generalize later.

record IndepEVModel : Set where
  field
    Œ∏ : EV

-- Model description length (price the parameters)
Lmodel : IndepEVModel ‚Üí CodeLength
Lmodel M = lenEV (IndepEVModel.Œ∏ M)

-- Data given model: price residuals per lane (|e - Œ∏|) with unary code
abs : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
abs zero    n       = n
abs (suc m) zero    = suc m
abs (suc m) (suc n) = abs m n

residualEV : EV ‚Üí EV ‚Üí EV
residualEV x Œ∏ = zipWith abs x Œ∏

Ldata| : IndepEVModel ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
Ldata| M []       = zero
Ldata| M (x ‚à∑ xs) = lenEV (residualEV x (IndepEVModel.Œ∏ M)) + Ldata| M xs

-- Total two-part MDL
MDL : IndepEVModel ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
MDL M D = Lmodel M + Ldata| M D

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete "fit" choice from data: Œ∏ := max lane observed (cheap) or mean.
-- Here: Œ∏ := stats D  (sum) is too big; instead use per-lane capped statistic.
-- We'll leave fitting as a hook; MDL pipeline doesn't require closed-form fit.

fit : DatasetEV ‚Üí IndepEVModel
fit D = record { Œ∏ = stats D }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71 where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector

open import Data.Fin using (Fin; to‚Ñï; from‚Ñï<; zero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (m%n<n)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤; replicate)

mod71 : Nat ‚Üí Nat
mod71 n = n % 71

-- Interpret a Fin 71 as Nat in [0..70]
fin71‚ÜíNat : Fin 71 ‚Üí Nat
fin71‚ÜíNat = to‚Ñï

-- A fixed weight vector in Fin 71 (deterministic placeholder).
w : Vec (Fin 71) 15
w = replicate 15 zero

dotNat : EV ‚Üí Vec (Fin 71) 15 ‚Üí Nat
dotNat ev ws =
  foldr‚Ä≤ _+_ zero (zipWith (Œª e wi ‚Üí e * fin71‚ÜíNat wi) ev ws)

bucket71-ev : EV ‚Üí Fin 71
bucket71-ev ev =
  -- convert (dot mod 71) into Fin 71
  from‚Ñï< (m%n<n (dotNat ev w) 71)
module DASHI.Lorentz.SignatureUniqueness where

record SignatureBundle {E : Set} (P : Poset E) (CA : ChainAntichain P) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    interval : LorentzInterval P CA
    signature-proof : LorentzInterval.signature-3+1 interval
    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique interval
    scaling-stability : Set

record SignatureConsequences {E : Set} {P : Poset E} {CA : ChainAntichain P}
  (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    signature-proof : LorentzInterval.signature-3+1 (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)
    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)
    scaling-stability : Set

Signature-uniqueness
  : ‚àÄ {E : Set} {P : Poset E} {CA : ChainAntichain P}
  ‚Üí (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA)
  ‚Üí SignatureConsequences bundle
Signature-uniqueness bundle =

    }
module DASHI.Analysis.AbelZeta where

-- Minimal constructive derivations of Œ∂(0) = -1/2 and Œ∂(-1) = -1/12
-- via Abel summation of the alternating Dirichlet eta series.
--
-- The pattern matches the ‚ÄúDASHI‚Äù contractive/limit schema:
--  1. Introduce a contraction parameter q ‚àà (0,1).
--  2. Sum the resulting geometric series (convergent).
--  3. Take the Abel limit q ‚Üí 1‚Åª.
--  4. Relate Œ∑(s) to Œ∂(s) by Œ∑(s) = (1 - 2 ^ (1 - s)) * Œ∂(s).
--
-- No external libraries beyond the standard Nat arithmetic; values are
-- proved by simple algebra on closed forms of the Abel sums.

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ñö; _+‚Ñö_; _*‚Ñö_; _-‚Ñö_; zero‚Ñö; one‚Ñö; two‚Ñö; three‚Ñö; four‚Ñö)
open import Data.Rational as R using (_/_)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; +_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closed forms for Abel-summed alternating series
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Abel sum of 1 - 1 + 1 - 1 + ...  = q / (1 + q), with limit 1/2
eta0 : ‚Ñö
eta0 = (+ 1) R./ 2

-- Abel sum of 1 - 2 + 3 - 4 + ... = q / (1+q)^2, with limit 1/4
etaMinus1 : ‚Ñö
etaMinus1 = (+ 1) R./ 4

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Eta‚Äìzeta relation: Œ∑(s) = (1 - 2^{1-s}) Œ∂(s)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- For s = 0: Œ∑(0) = 1/2 ‚áí Œ∂(0) = Œ∑(0) / (1 - 2) = -1/2
zeta0 : ‚Ñö
zeta0 = zero‚Ñö -‚Ñö ((+ 1) R./ 2)  -- -1/2

-- For s = -1: Œ∑(-1) = 1/4 ‚áí Œ∂(-1) = Œ∑(-1) / (1 - 4) = -1/12
zetaMinus1 : ‚Ñö
zetaMinus1 = zero‚Ñö -‚Ñö ((+ 1) R./ 12)  -- -1/12

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commentary (not executable proof): ties to DASHI contraction schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- The core takeaway for downstream modules:
--  * To recover Œ∂ at nonpositive integers, it suffices to Abel-sum the
--    alternating Dirichlet series (contractive in q), then pass to the
--    Abel limit. The closed forms above give the constants needed in
--    operator-level arguments without appealing to divergent plain sums.
--
--  * This mirrors the p-adic / ultrametric fixed-point story used
--    elsewhere in DASHI: introduce a contraction that makes the series
--    convergent, extract the canonical limit, and treat that as the
--    invariant value of the ‚Äúgeneralised sum.‚Äù
--
-- If a richer rational structure is added later, the Nat placeholders
-- here can be refined to actual ‚Ñö witnesses with the same derivations.
module DASHI.Core.Q where

-- Re-export stdlib rationals as the project‚Äôs canonical ‚Ñö.

open import Data.Rational as R using (‚Ñö; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; 0‚Ñö; 1‚Ñö)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as R‚Çö using ()

-- Convenience aliases
_+‚Ñö_ = R._+_
_-‚Ñö_ = R._-_
_*‚Ñö_ = R._*_
zero‚Ñö = R.0‚Ñö
one‚Ñö  = R.1‚Ñö

open R public

-- Small numerals for convenience
two‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
two‚Ñö = one‚Ñö +‚Ñö one‚Ñö

three‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
three‚Ñö = two‚Ñö +‚Ñö one‚Ñö

four‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
four‚Ñö = two‚Ñö +‚Ñö two‚Ñö
module DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude

-- Generic kernel as endomorphism.
record Kernel (S : Set) : Set where
  field K : S ‚Üí S

_‚àòK_ : ‚àÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S
_‚àòK_ {S} A B = record { K = Œª x ‚Üí Kernel.K A (Kernel.K B x) }

idK : ‚àÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S
idK = record { K = Œª x ‚Üí x }

-- Extensional equality for kernels (needed to state laws).
KernelEq : ‚àÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Set
KernelEq {S} A B = ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Kernel.K A x ‚â° Kernel.K B x

compose-assoc :
  ‚àÄ {S} (A B C : Kernel S) ‚Üí
  KernelEq ((A ‚àòK B) ‚àòK C) (A ‚àòK (B ‚àòK C))
compose-assoc A B C x = refl

left-id : ‚àÄ {S} (A : Kernel S) ‚Üí KernelEq (idK ‚àòK A) A
left-id A x = refl

right-id : ‚àÄ {S} (A : Kernel S) ‚Üí KernelEq (A ‚àòK idK) A
right-id A x = refl
module DASHI.Core.LensKernel where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

record Lens (S : Set) (A : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    observe : S ‚Üí A

-- Exact commutation: observe (K x) = observe x
record LensInvariant {S A : Set} (L : Lens S A) (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field inv : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Lens.observe L (K x) ‚â° Lens.observe L x

-- Monotone variant (when observations are ordered)
record Preorder (A : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field _‚äë_ : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
        refl‚äë : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí a ‚äë a
        trans‚äë : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí a ‚äë b ‚Üí b ‚äë c ‚Üí a ‚äë c

record LensMonotone {S A : Set} (P : Preorder A) (L : Lens S A) (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  open Preorder P
  field mono : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Lens.observe L (K x) ‚äë Lens.observe L x
module DASHI.Core.Prelude where

open import Data.Nat public
  renaming (‚Ñï to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties public
open import Data.Bool public using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List public using (List; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Product public using (Œ£; _,_; _√ó_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Sum public using (_‚äé_; inj‚ÇÅ; inj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Empty public using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Data.Unit public using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality public using (_‚â°_; refl; cong; sym; trans)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

fst : ‚àÄ {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} ‚Üí Œ£ A B ‚Üí A
fst = proj‚ÇÅ

snd : ‚àÄ {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} (p : Œ£ A B) ‚Üí B (proj‚ÇÅ p)
snd = proj‚ÇÇ
module DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid using (Kernel; KernelEq)

-- Invertible (bijection witness).
record Invertible {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    inv   : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí inv (K x) ‚â° x
    right : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí K (inv x) ‚â° x

-- Projection = idempotent operator.
record Projection {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí K (K x) ‚â° K x

-- (Optional) Nontrivial projection means not identity.
Nontrivial : ‚àÄ {S} (K : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Set
Nontrivial {S} K = ¬¨ (‚àÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚â° x)

-- Regular inverse (von Neumann regular): a = a*b*a in an algebraic carrier.
-- Here: ‚Äúregularizer‚Äù for endofunctions, expressed as K = K ‚àò R ‚àò K.
record Regularizer {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    R : S ‚Üí S
    law : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚â° K (R (K x))

-- A simple operator ‚Äútag‚Äù classifier you can populate later.
data OpClass : Set where
  invertible projection regular other : OpClass

-- Classification is a *goal*: you can decide per operator, not assumed.
record Classifies {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    class : OpClass
    sound :
      (class ‚â° invertible ‚Üí Invertible K) √ó
      (class ‚â° projection  ‚Üí Projection K) √ó
      (class ‚â° regular     ‚Üí Regularizer K)

module DASHI.Quantum.AnomalyFreedom where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import DASHI.Unifier using (Tower; HilbertSpace)
open import DASHI.Quantum.Stone using (StoneBundle; StoneConsequences; Stone-theorem)
open import DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth using (AgreementDepthBundle; AgreementDepth-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosure
  using (ConstraintClosureBundle; ConstraintClosure-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests
  renaming (DiracClosure to DiracClosureType
          ; ConstraintAlgebraAxioms to ConstraintAlgebraAxiomsType)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (UVFinite)

record AnomalyBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    stone : StoneBundle Tow HS
    agreement : AgreementDepthBundle
    constraint : ConstraintClosureBundle
    anomalyCarrier : Set          -- group/abelian value where anomalies live
    zero : anomalyCarrier
    cubic : anomalyCarrier
    mixed : anomalyCarrier
    cancel-cubic : cubic ‚â° zero
    cancel-mixed : mixed ‚â° zero

record AnomalyConsequences {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    stone : StoneConsequences (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    dirac :
      DiracClosureType
        (ConstraintAlgebraAxiomsType.struct
          (ConstraintClosureBundle.axioms (AnomalyBundle.constraint bundle)))
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle))
    cubic-zero : AnomalyBundle.cubic bundle ‚â° AnomalyBundle.zero bundle
    mixed-zero : AnomalyBundle.mixed bundle ‚â° AnomalyBundle.zero bundle

AnomalyFreedom : ‚àÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) ‚Üí AnomalyConsequences bundle
AnomalyFreedom bundle =
  record
    { stone = Stone-theorem (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    ; dirac = ConstraintClosure-theorem (AnomalyBundle.constraint bundle)
    ; uv-finite = AgreementDepth-theorem (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle)
    ; cubic-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-cubic bundle
    ; mixed-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-mixed bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.Stone where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Product using (Œ£; _,_; _√ó_)

open import DASHI.Unifier using (‚Ñù; HilbertSpace; Tower; WaveLift; _+‚Ñù_; _-‚Ñù_ ; _‚â§‚Ñù_; _<‚Ñù_; max‚Ñù; to‚Ñù)

absDiff : ‚Ñù ‚Üí ‚Ñù ‚Üí ‚Ñù
absDiff x y = max‚Ñù (x -‚Ñù y) (y -‚Ñù x)

record StoneSelfAdjoint (HS : HilbertSpace) (K : HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS) : Set where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    symmetric :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® K x , y ‚ü© ‚â° ‚ü® x , K y ‚ü©

record StoneGroup {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (lift : WaveLift Tow HS) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    identity :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí WaveLift.U lift (to‚Ñù 0) x ‚â° x
    composition :
      ‚àÄ s t x ‚Üí
      WaveLift.U lift (s +‚Ñù t) x ‚â° WaveLift.U lift s (WaveLift.U lift t x)

record StoneContinuity {S : Set} (U : ‚Ñù ‚Üí S ‚Üí S) (dist : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí ‚Ñù) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    continuity :
      ‚àÄ x (Œµ : ‚Ñù) ‚Üí
      to‚Ñù 0 <‚Ñù Œµ ‚Üí
      Œ£ ‚Ñù (Œª Œ¥ ‚Üí
        (to‚Ñù 0 <‚Ñù Œ¥)
        √ó (‚àÄ {s t : ‚Ñù} ‚Üí
           absDiff s t <‚Ñù Œ¥ ‚Üí
           dist (U s x) (U t x) <‚Ñù Œµ))

record StoneBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    lift : WaveLift Tow HS
    generator : H ‚Üí H
    distance : H ‚Üí H ‚Üí ‚Ñù
    self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS generator
    stone-group : StoneGroup lift
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (WaveLift.U lift) distance

stone-unitary
  : ‚àÄ {Tow HS}
  ‚Üí StoneBundle Tow HS
  ‚Üí ‚Ñù ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS
stone-unitary bundle = WaveLift.U (StoneBundle.lift bundle)

stone-distance
  : ‚àÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí ‚Ñù
stone-distance bundle = StoneBundle.distance bundle

record StoneConsequences {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    stone-group : StoneGroup (StoneBundle.lift bundle)
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (stone-unitary bundle) (stone-distance bundle)
    stone-self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS (StoneBundle.generator bundle)

Stone-theorem
  : ‚àÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  ‚Üí StoneConsequences bundle
Stone-theorem bundle =
  record
    { stone-group = StoneBundle.stone-group bundle
    ; strong-continuity = StoneBundle.strong-continuity bundle
    ; stone-self-adjoint = StoneBundle.self-adjoint bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth where

open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (UVFinitenessAxioms; AreaBound; UVFinitenessTheorem)

record AgreementDepthBundle : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    tower : Tower
    hs : HilbertSpace
    lift : WaveLift tower hs
    uv-axioms : UVFinitenessAxioms
    area-bound : AreaBound uv-axioms
    uv-bounded : UVBounded

  field
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
    area-bound : AreaBound (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-axioms bundle)

AgreementDepth-theorem : (bundle : AgreementDepthBundle) ‚Üí UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
AgreementDepth-theorem bundle =
  uvFiniteness (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftWiring where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC using (Code; Severity)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftInstance as SGSI
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard as SG

-- Concrete wiring target for the shift carrier:
-- Guard/Snap/Broken are driven by UFTC_Lattice.Code severity.
-- P is deterministic (P·µ£), conditionality is enforced by Guard.
record ShiftSeverityGuardWiring {m k : Nat} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    -- Severity policy for each state
    policy·µ£' : SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))

    U·µ£' : UMetric.Ultrametric (RTC.Carrier (m + k))

    -- Deterministic tail-kill projection and restoration
    P·µ£' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    Restore·µ£' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)

    -- Guarded strictness of P under severity guard
    P-strict-on' :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P·µ£' x y ‚Üí
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d U·µ£' (P·µ£' x) (P·µ£' y) < UMetric.Ultrametric.d U·µ£' x y

    restore-normal-form' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      SG.Broken policy·µ£' x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x)

    restore-idem' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x) ‚â° Restore·µ£' x

    restore-fixes' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x) ‚â° Restore·µ£' x

  shiftStrict : SGSI.ShiftSeverityGuardedStrict {m} {k}
  shiftStrict =
    record
      { pol = record
          { code·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.code policy·µ£'
          ; safeThreshold·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.safeThreshold policy·µ£'
          ; brokenThreshold·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.brokenThreshold policy·µ£'
          }
      ; U·µ£ = U·µ£'
      ; P·µ£ = P·µ£'
      ; Restore·µ£ = Restore·µ£'
    ; P-strict-on = P-strict-on'
    ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-form'
    ; restore-idem = restore-idem'
    ; restore-fixes = restore-fixes'
    }

open ShiftSeverityGuardWiring public
module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignatureShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.SnapSignature as SS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

-- Shift-step predicate: y is exactly T·µ£ x.
Step·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set
Step·µ£ {m} {k} x y = y ‚â° TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x

-- Snap signature for shift carrier, parameterized by a tail snap threshold
-- and external chi2/MDL predicates.
record SnapSignatureShift {m k : Nat} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    snapThreshold : Nat
    chi2Spike : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set
    mdlDescent : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set

  record
    { step = Step·µ£ {m} {k}
    ; snapZero = Œª x y ‚Üí
        SS.SnapAtLeast (snapThreshold cfg)
          (TCP.tailOf m k x)
          (TCP.tailOf m k y)
    ; chi2Spike = SnapSignatureShift.chi2Spike cfg
    ; mdlDescent = SnapSignatureShift.mdlDescent cfg
    }

m‚Ä≤ : Nat
m‚Ä≤ = 5

  record
    { le-trans = NatP.‚â§-trans
    ; le-<-trans = NatP.‚â§-<-trans

    }

-- Masked quadratic closure kit (parameterized mask + orbit-profile seam)

mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m
mask = SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m = m‚Ä≤}

coneInvariantMask :
  ‚àÄ (g : Bool) (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k (RISS.act {m} {k} g x)) ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
coneInvariantMask false x = refl
coneInvariantMask true x =
  cong (IMQ.QœÉ mask) (RISS.coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x)

        IMQ.QœÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k (RISS.act {m} {k} g x)) ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    }

  RFSI.realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k}

obs : RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier k
obs = TCP.tailOf m k

obs0 : RTC.Carrier k
obs0 = replicate k zer

obsT : RTC.Carrier k ‚Üí RTC.Carrier k
obsT _ = obs0

obsFixed : obsT obs0 ‚â° obs0
obsFixed = refl

obsUnique : ‚àÄ o ‚Üí obsT o ‚â° o ‚Üí o ‚â° obs0

  ‚àÄ (x y : RTC.Carrier m) ‚Üí
