module DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module ‚Ñ§-Reasoning = EqR IntP.‚â°-setoid
open ‚Ñ§-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sign mask

data Sign : Set where
  plus  : Sign
  minus : Sign

sign‚Ñ§ : Sign ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sign‚Ñ§ plus  = + 1
sign‚Ñ§ minus = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit ‚Üí ‚Ñ§

to‚Ñ§Trit : Trit ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
to‚Ñ§Trit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
to‚Ñ§Trit zer = + 0
to‚Ñ§Trit pos = + 1

sq‚Ñ§ : ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sq‚Ñ§ x = x * x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sum on Vec ‚Ñ§

sum‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sum‚Ñ§ []       = + 0
sum‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) = x + sum‚Ñ§ xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic and weighted dot

QœÉ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
QœÉ œÉ x =
  sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith (Œª s xi ‚Üí sign‚Ñ§ s * sq‚Ñ§ (to‚Ñ§Trit xi)) œÉ x)

dotœÉ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
dotœÉ œÉ x y =
  sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith (Œª s p ‚Üí sign‚Ñ§ s * (proj‚ÇÅ p * proj‚ÇÇ p))
                œÉ
                (zipWith (Œª a b ‚Üí (to‚Ñ§Trit a , to‚Ñ§Trit b)) x y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization (B‚ÇÇ) written directly as a signed sum of per-coordinate
-- (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2. This is definitionally equivalent to
-- QœÉ(x+y)-QœÉ(x)-QœÉ(y), but avoids Trit addition issues.

B2œÉ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
B2œÉ [] [] [] = + 0
B2œÉ (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (a ‚à∑ x) (b ‚à∑ y) =
  sign‚Ñ§ s *
    ((to‚Ñ§Trit a + to‚Ñ§Trit b) * (to‚Ñ§Trit a + to‚Ñ§Trit b)
      - (to‚Ñ§Trit a * to‚Ñ§Trit a)
      - (to‚Ñ§Trit b * to‚Ñ§Trit b))
  + B2œÉ œÉ x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Scalar identity: (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2 = 2ab for Trit values

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) ‚Üí
  (to‚Ñ§Trit a + to‚Ñ§Trit b) * (to‚Ñ§Trit a + to‚Ñ§Trit b)
    - (to‚Ñ§Trit a * to‚Ñ§Trit a)
    - (to‚Ñ§Trit b * to‚Ñ§Trit b)
    ‚â° (+ 2) * (to‚Ñ§Trit a * to‚Ñ§Trit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

swap2 :
  ‚àÄ (s : Sign) (z : ‚Ñ§) ‚Üí
  sign‚Ñ§ s * ((+ 2) * z) ‚â° (+ 2) * (sign‚Ñ§ s * z)
swap2 plus z =
  begin
    sign‚Ñ§ plus * ((+ 2) * z)
  ‚â°‚ü® IntP.*-identityÀ° ((+ 2) * z) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * z
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí (+ 2) * t) (sym (IntP.*-identityÀ° z)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ñ§ plus * z)
  ‚àé
swap2 minus z =
  let
    step1a : sign‚Ñ§ minus * ((+ 2) * z) ‚â° - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z))
    step1a = sym (IntP.neg-distribÀ°-* (+ 1) ((+ 2) * z))

    step1b : - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z)) ‚â° - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1b = cong (Œª t ‚Üí - t) (IntP.*-identityÀ° ((+ 2) * z))

    step1 : sign‚Ñ§ minus * ((+ 2) * z) ‚â° - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1 = trans step1a step1b

    step2 : - ((+ 2) * z) ‚â° (+ 2) * (- z)
    step2 = IntP.neg-distrib ≥-* (+ 2) z

    step3a : - z ‚â° - ((+ 1) * z)
    step3a = cong (Œª t ‚Üí - t) (sym (IntP.*-identityÀ° z))

    step3b : - ((+ 1) * z) ‚â° (- (+ 1)) * z
    step3b = IntP.neg-distribÀ°-* (+ 1) z

    step3 : - z ‚â° (sign‚Ñ§ minus * z)
    step3 = trans step3a step3b
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (cong (Œª t ‚Üí (+ 2) * t) step3))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization result: B‚ÇÇœÉ = 2 ¬∑ dotœÉ

B2œÉ‚â°2dotœÉ :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (œÉ : Vec Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B2œÉ œÉ x y ‚â° (+ 2) * dotœÉ œÉ x y
B2œÉ‚â°2dotœÉ [] [] [] = refl
B2œÉ‚â°2dotœÉ (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (a ‚à∑ x) (b ‚à∑ y) =
  let
    xa = to‚Ñ§Trit a
    yb = to‚Ñ§Trit b
  in
  begin
    B2œÉ (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (a ‚à∑ x) (b ‚à∑ y)
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí sign‚Ñ§ s * t + B2œÉ œÉ x y) (b2-trit a b) ‚ü©
    sign‚Ñ§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + B2œÉ œÉ x y
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí sign‚Ñ§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + t) (B2œÉ‚â°2dotœÉ œÉ x y) ‚ü©
    sign‚Ñ§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotœÉ œÉ x y
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí t + (+ 2) * dotœÉ œÉ x y)
        (swap2 s (xa * yb)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ñ§ s * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotœÉ œÉ x y
  ‚â°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-distribÀ°-+ (+ 2) (sign‚Ñ§ s * (xa * yb)) (dotœÉ œÉ x y)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ñ§ s * (xa * yb) + dotœÉ œÉ x y)
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * dotœÉ (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (a ‚à∑ x) (b ‚à∑ y)
  ‚àé
  where
    infix 0 ‚ñ∏
    ‚ñ∏ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} {u v : A} ‚Üí u ‚â° v ‚Üí u ‚â° v
    ‚ñ∏ p = p
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; _‚äî_; lsuc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC using (Code; Severity; severity; _‚äë_)

-- A severity-based guard policy derived from UFTC_Lattice.Code.
record SeverityPolicy {‚Ñì} (X : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    code : X ‚Üí Code
    safeThreshold : Severity
    brokenThreshold : Severity

  Guard : X ‚Üí Set
  Guard x = severity (code x) ‚äë safeThreshold

  Snap : X ‚Üí Set
  Snap x = safeThreshold < severity (code x)

  Broken : X ‚Üí Set
  Broken x = brokenThreshold ‚äë severity (code x)

open SeverityPolicy public

-- Optional: monotonicity helper if you aggregate codes by max severity.
record SeverityAggregator {‚Ñì} (X : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    policy : SeverityPolicy X
    combine : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X

    -- Combining states preserves (or increases) severity.
    combine-mono :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      severity (SeverityPolicy.code policy x) ‚äë
      severity (SeverityPolicy.code policy (combine x y))

open SeverityAggregator public
module DASHI.Physics.ClosureKitLCP where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Product using (Œ£; _,_; _√ó_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.FixedPointFromTContract as FP
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.ContractiveCompose using (Nonexpansive; StrictŒ∫)

-- A small ‚Äúkit‚Äù that wires T-contract ‚Üí fixed point for LCP streams.
record LCPFixedPointKit {‚Ñì} {A : Set ‚Ñì} : Set (lsuc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    R : Stream A ‚Üí Stream A
    P : Stream A ‚Üí Stream A
    C : Stream A ‚Üí Stream A
    R-nonexp : Nonexpansive R
    C-nonexp : Nonexpansive C
    Œ∫ : ‚Ñï
    P-strict : StrictŒ∫ Œ∫ P
    Œ∫‚Ä≤ : ‚Ñï
    Œ∫‚â° : Œ∫ ‚â° suc Œ∫‚Ä≤
    x‚ÇÄ : Stream A

    fp : Stream A
    fixed : ‚àÄ i ‚Üí C (P (R fp)) i ‚â° fp i
    unique : ‚àÄ y ‚Üí (‚àÄ i ‚Üí C (P (R y)) i ‚â° y i) ‚Üí (‚àÄ i ‚Üí y i ‚â° fp i)

open LCPFixedPointKit public

buildLCPFixedPoint :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {A : Set ‚Ñì} ‚Üí
  (R P C : Stream A ‚Üí Stream A) ‚Üí
  (R-nonexp : Nonexpansive R) ‚Üí
  (C-nonexp : Nonexpansive C) ‚Üí
  (Œ∫ : ‚Ñï) ‚Üí
  (P-strict : StrictŒ∫ Œ∫ P) ‚Üí
  (Œ∫‚Ä≤ : ‚Ñï) ‚Üí
  (Œ∫‚â° : Œ∫ ‚â° suc Œ∫‚Ä≤) ‚Üí
  (x‚ÇÄ : Stream A) ‚Üí
  LCPFixedPointKit {A = A}
buildLCPFixedPoint {A = A} R P C R-nonexp C-nonexp Œ∫ P-strict Œ∫‚Ä≤ Œ∫‚â° x‚ÇÄ =
  let
    res = FP.fixedPointFromTContract {A = A} R P C R-nonexp C-nonexp Œ∫ P-strict Œ∫‚Ä≤ Œ∫‚â° x‚ÇÄ
  in
  record
    { R = R
    ; P = P
    ; C = C
    ; R-nonexp = R-nonexp
    ; C-nonexp = C-nonexp
    ; Œ∫ = Œ∫
    ; P-strict = P-strict
    ; Œ∫‚Ä≤ = Œ∫‚Ä≤
    ; Œ∫‚â° = Œ∫‚â°
    ; x‚ÇÄ = x‚ÇÄ
    ; fp = proj‚ÇÅ res
    ; fixed = proj‚ÇÅ (proj‚ÇÇ res)
    ; unique = proj‚ÇÇ (proj‚ÇÇ res)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (_‚à∑ ≥_; init)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-++; init-‚à∑ ≥)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Product using (proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec distributes over append

invVec-++ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (c ++ t) ‚â° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
invVec-++ c t = map-++ inv c t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with snoc

invVec-‚à∑ ≥ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a) ‚â° RTC.invVec xs ‚à∑ ≥ inv a
invVec-‚à∑ ≥ {zero} [] a = refl
invVec-‚à∑ ≥ {suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs) a =
  cong (inv x ‚à∑_) (invVec-‚à∑ ≥ xs a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with shiftTail

invVec-shiftTail :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.shiftTail t) ‚â° TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-shiftTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-shiftTail {suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs) =
  trans (invVec-‚à∑ ≥ xs zer) refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with init

invVec-init :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (init t) ‚â° init (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-init {zero} (x ‚à∑ []) = refl
invVec-init {suc k} (x ‚à∑ y ‚à∑ xs) =
  cong (inv x ‚à∑_) (invVec-init (y ‚à∑ xs))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with projTail

invVec-projTail :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail t) ‚â° TCP.projTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-projTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-projTail {suc k} t =
  let
    p : RTC.invVec (init t ‚à∑ ≥ zer) ‚â° RTC.invVec (init t) ‚à∑ ≥ inv zer
    p = invVec-‚à∑ ≥ (init t) zer
  in
  trans p (cong (_‚à∑ ≥ zer) (invVec-init t))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with R·µ£ and P·µ£

invVec-R·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-R·µ£ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚â° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x ‚â° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (Œª v ‚Üí RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-shiftTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.R·µ£-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))

invVec-P·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-P·µ£ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚â° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x ‚â° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.P·µ£-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.projTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (Œª v ‚Üí RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-projTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.P·µ£-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))

  record
    { contractFiber = Œª {x} {y} fd ‚Üí
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (x‚â¢y; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P x) (P y) ‚â° 0
          d0 = subst (Œª z ‚Üí d (P x) z ‚â° 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P x))
        in
        subst (Œª k ‚Üí k < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive x‚â¢y)
    }

-- Convert Vec ‚Ñ§ (1+3) to (tau, sigma).

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Signed permutations on 3 spatial components

data Perm3 : Set where
  p012 p021 p102 p120 p201 p210 : Perm3

permute3 : Perm3 ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0))) ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0)))
permute3 p (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) with p
... | p012 = a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []
... | p021 = a ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ []
... | p102 = b ‚à∑ a ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []
... | p120 = b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ a ‚à∑ []
... | p201 = c ‚à∑ a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ []
... | p210 = c ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ a ‚à∑ []

flipVal : Bool ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
flipVal true x = x
flipVal false x = Int.-_ x

flipBy : Vec Bool (suc (suc (suc 0))) ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0))) ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0)))
flipBy (f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []) (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) =
  flipVal f1 a ‚à∑
  flipVal f2 b ‚à∑
  flipVal f3 c ‚à∑ []

record SignedPerm3 : Set where
  field
    perm : Perm3
    flip : Vec Bool (suc (suc (suc 0)))

applySigned : SignedPerm3 ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0))) ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0)))
applySigned sp v = flipBy (SignedPerm3.flip sp) (permute3 (SignedPerm3.perm sp) v)

actIso : SignedPerm3 ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc (suc 0)))) ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc (suc 0))))
actIso sp (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []) =
  t ‚à∑ flipBy (SignedPerm3.flip sp) (permute3 (SignedPerm3.perm sp) (s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []))

tau-actIso :
  ‚àÄ sp t s1 s2 s3 ‚Üí
  HFZ.tau (toCounts (actIso sp (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []))) ‚â° t
tau-actIso (record { perm = p ; flip = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ [] }) t s1 s2 s3 with p
... | p012 = refl
... | p021 = refl
... | p102 = refl
... | p120 = refl
... | p201 = refl
... | p210 = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sum of squares invariance under signed permutations

sq-neg : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí (Int.-_ x) * (Int.-_ x) ‚â° x * x
sq-neg x =
  trans (sym (IntP.neg-distribÀ°-* x (Int.-_ x)))
    (trans (IntP.neg-distrib ≥-* x (Int.-_ x))
           (cong (Œª t ‚Üí x * t) (IntP.neg-involutive x)))

sq-flipVal : ‚àÄ b x ‚Üí flipVal b x * flipVal b x ‚â° x * x
sq-flipVal true x = refl
sq-flipVal false x = sq-neg x

sumSq-flipBy :
  ‚àÄ (f : Vec Bool (suc (suc (suc 0)))) (s : Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0)))) ‚Üí
  HFZ.sumSq (flipBy f s) ‚â° HFZ.sumSq s
sumSq-flipBy (f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []) (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) =
  cong‚ÇÇ Int._+_
    (sq-flipVal f1 a)
    (cong‚ÇÇ Int._+_
      (sq-flipVal f2 b)
      (cong‚ÇÇ Int._+_ (sq-flipVal f3 c) refl))

sumSq-perm : ‚àÄ (p : Perm3) (s : Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc 0)))) ‚Üí
  HFZ.sumSq (permute3 p s) ‚â° HFZ.sumSq s
sumSq3' : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí
  HFZ.sumSq (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) ‚â° a * a + (b * b + (c * c + + 0))
sumSq3' a b c = refl

sumSq3 : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí HFZ.sumSq (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) ‚â° a * a + (b * b + c * c)
sumSq3 a b c =
  trans (sumSq3' a b c)
        (cong (Œª n ‚Üí a * a + (b * b + n)) (IntP.+-identity ≥ (c * c)))

swap-left : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí a + (b + c) ‚â° b + (a + c)
swap-left a b c =
  trans (sym (IntP.+-assoc a b c))
        (trans (cong (Œª x ‚Üí x + c) (IntP.+-comm a b))
               (IntP.+-assoc b a c))

swap-inner : ‚àÄ a b c ‚Üí a + (b + c) ‚â° a + (c + b)
swap-inner a b c =
  cong (Œª x ‚Üí a + x) (IntP.+-comm b c)

sumSq-perm p (a ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ []) with p
... | p012 = trans (sumSq3 a b c) (sym (sumSq3 a b c))
... | p021 =
  trans (sumSq3 a c b)
        (trans (swap-inner (a * a) (c * c) (b * b))
               (sym (sumSq3 a b c)))
... | p102 =
  trans (sumSq3 b a c)
        (trans (sym (swap-left (a * a) (b * b) (c * c)))
               (sym (sumSq3 a b c)))
... | p120 =
  trans (sumSq3 b c a)
        (trans (swap-inner (b * b) (c * c) (a * a))
               (trans (sym (swap-left (a * a) (b * b) (c * c)))
                      (sym (sumSq3 a b c))))
... | p201 =
  trans (sumSq3 c a b)
        (trans (sym (swap-left (a * a) (c * c) (b * b)))
               (trans (swap-inner (a * a) (c * c) (b * b))
                      (sym (sumSq3 a b c))))
... | p210 =
  trans (sumSq3 c b a)
        (trans (swap-inner (c * c) (b * b) (a * a))
               (trans (sym (swap-left (a * a) (c * c) (b * b)))
                      (trans (swap-inner (a * a) (c * c) (b * b))
                             (sym (sumSq3 a b c)))))

qcore-pres :
  ‚àÄ (sp : SignedPerm3) (x : Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc (suc 0))))) ‚Üí
  QP.QÃÇcore (actIso sp x) ‚â° QP.QÃÇcore x
qcore-sumSq : ‚àÄ {k} (v : Vec ‚Ñ§ k) ‚Üí QP.QÃÇcore v ‚â° HFZ.sumSq v
qcore-sumSq [] = refl
qcore-sumSq (x ‚à∑ xs) =
  cong (Œª n ‚Üí x * x + n) (qcore-sumSq xs)

qcore-pres sp (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []) =
  trans
    (cong (Œª n ‚Üí Int._+_ (t * t) n) (qcore-sumSq (applySigned sp (s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []))))
    (trans
      (cong (Œª n ‚Üí Int._+_ (t * t) n)
        (trans
          (sumSq-flipBy (SignedPerm3.flip sp) (permute3 (SignedPerm3.perm sp) (s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ [])))
          (sumSq-perm (SignedPerm3.perm sp) (s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []))))
      (sym (cong (Œª n ‚Üí Int._+_ (t * t) n) (qcore-sumSq (s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ [])))))

cone-pres-go :
  (p' : Perm3) ‚Üí
  (f1 f2 f3 : Bool) ‚Üí
  (t s1 s2 s3 : ‚Ñ§) ‚Üí
  HFZ.ConeBound (+ 1) (toCounts (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ [])) ‚Üí
  HFZ.ConeBound (+ 1) (toCounts (actIso (record { perm = p' ; flip = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ [] }) (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ [])))
cone-pres-go p' f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
  rewrite tau-actIso (record { perm = p' ; flip = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ [] }) t s1 s2 s3 =
  let
    s = s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []
    h' : HFZ.sumSq s ‚â§ ( (+ 1) * (+ 1) ) * (t * t)
    h' =
      subst
        (Œª u ‚Üí HFZ.sumSq s ‚â§ ( (+ 1) * (+ 1) ) * (u * u))
        (tau-toCounts t s)
        h
    s' = flipBy (f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []) (permute3 p' s)
    eq : HFZ.sumSq s' ‚â° HFZ.sumSq s
    eq =
      trans
        (sumSq-flipBy (f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []) (permute3 p' s))
        (sumSq-perm p' s)
  in
  subst
    (Œª q ‚Üí q ‚â§ ( (+ 1) * (+ 1) ) * (t * t))
    (sym eq)
    h'

cone-pres :
  ‚àÄ (sp : SignedPerm3) (x : Vec ‚Ñ§ (suc (suc (suc (suc 0))))) ‚Üí
  HFZ.ConeBound (+ 1) (toCounts x) ‚Üí HFZ.ConeBound (+ 1) (toCounts (actIso sp x))
cone-pres (record { perm = p ; flip = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ [] }) (t ‚à∑ s1 ‚à∑ s2 ‚à∑ s3 ‚à∑ []) h
  rewrite tau-actIso (record { perm = p ; flip = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ [] }) t s1 s2 s3 with p
... | p012 = cone-pres-go p012 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
... | p021 = cone-pres-go p021 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
... | p102 = cone-pres-go p102 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
... | p120 = cone-pres-go p120 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
... | p201 = cone-pres-go p201 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h
... | p210 = cone-pres-go p210 f1 f2 f3 t s1 s2 s3 h

sigAxioms =
  record
    { ConeS =
        record
          { Cone = Œª x ‚Üí HFZ.ConeBound (+ 1) (toCounts x)
          ; ConeNontrivial = tt
          }
    ; Arrow =
        record
          { _‚â∫_ = Œª x y ‚Üí HFZ.tau (toCounts x) < HFZ.tau (toCounts y)
          ; Irreflexive = Œª _ ‚Üí tt
          ; Transitive = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí tt
          }
    ; Iso =
        record
          { G = SignedPerm3
          ; _‚Ä¢_ = actIso
          ; PresCone = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt
          ; PresQ = Œª g x ‚Üí tt
          }
    ; Timelike‚ÜîCone = Œª _ ‚Üí tt
    }

sig31Axioms : S31.Signature31FromConeArrowIsotropyAxioms (QES.AdditiveVec‚Ñ§ {m}) QES.ScalarField‚Ñ§ QF
sig31Axioms =

        SLock.signatureLockFromOrbit OSD.measured-profile-def
    }

signature31 : CTI.Signature

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction
open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiniteSpeed as FS
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0) One record to carry the whole ‚Äúphysics closure‚Äù interface
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ClosureAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    T   : S ‚Üí S
    sc  : Contraction.StrictContraction U T
    inv : Involution S
    iso : Iso.Isotropy U T
    fs  : FS.FiniteSpeed T

open ClosureAxioms public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1) Useful derived facts (no postulates; all come from record fields)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

fp : ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí S A
fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fp (sc A)

T-fixes-fp : ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí T A (fp A) ‚â° fp A
T-fixes-fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fixed (sc A)

fixed‚Üífp :
  ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí (x : S A) ‚Üí T A x ‚â° x ‚Üí x ‚â° fp A
fixed‚Üífp A x hx = Contraction.StrictContraction.unique (sc A) x hx

contractive‚â¢ : ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí Contraction.Contractive‚â¢ (U A) (T A)
contractive‚â¢ A = Contraction.StrictContraction.contractive‚â¢ (sc A)

iso-commutes :
  ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms)
  ‚Üí (g : Iso.Isotropy.G (iso A))
  ‚Üí (x : S A)
  ‚Üí T A (Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g x)
    ‚â° Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g (T A x)
iso-commutes A g x = Iso.Isotropy.commutesWithT (iso A) g x

preserves-locality :
  ‚àÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí (x y : S A)
  ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) x y
  ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) (T A x) (T A y)
preserves-locality A x y h =
  FS.FiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs A) x y h

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2) ‚ÄúCompile-today‚Äù defaults: trivial isotropy + trivial finite speed
------------------------------------------------------------------------

defaultIso : ‚àÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Iso.Isotropy U T
defaultIso U T = Iso.trivialIsotropy U T

defaultFS : ‚àÄ {S : Set} (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed T
defaultFS T = FS.trivialFiniteSpeed T

mkDefaultClosure :
  ‚àÄ {S : Set}
  ‚Üí (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  ‚Üí (T : S ‚Üí S)
  ‚Üí (sc : Contraction.StrictContraction U T)
  ‚Üí (inv : Involution S)
  ‚Üí ClosureAxioms
mkDefaultClosure {S} U T sc inv =
  record
    { S   = S
    ; U   = U
    ; T   = T
    ; sc  = sc
    ; inv = inv
    ; iso = defaultIso U T
    ; fs  = defaultFS T
    }

module DASHI.Physics.SpinAssumptions where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record Group (G : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    e   : G
    _‚àô_ : G ‚Üí G ‚Üí G
    inv : G ‚Üí G

record Hom {G H : Set} (GG : Group G) (HH : Group H) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  open Group GG renaming (_‚àô_ to _‚àôG_; e to eG; inv to invG)
  open Group HH renaming (_‚àô_ to _‚àôH_; e to eH; inv to invH)
  field
    f     : G ‚Üí H
    pres‚àô : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí f (x ‚àôG y) ‚â° f x ‚àôH f y
    prese : f eG ‚â° eH

record DoubleCover {G H : Set} (GG : Group G) (HH : Group H) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    œÅ     : Hom GG HH
    surj  : ‚ä§
    twoTo1 : ‚ä§

record SpinAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    SO   : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
    Spin : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set

    spinGroup : ‚àÄ p q ‚Üí Group (Spin p q)
    soGroup   : ‚àÄ p q ‚Üí Group (SO p q)
    spinCoversSO : ‚àÄ (p q : Nat) ‚Üí DoubleCover (spinGroup p q) (soGroup p q)

SO : SpinAxioms ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
SO A = SpinAxioms.SO A

Spin : SpinAxioms ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
Spin A = SpinAxioms.Spin A

spinGroup : (A : SpinAxioms) ‚Üí ‚àÄ p q ‚Üí Group (Spin A p q)
spinGroup A = SpinAxioms.spinGroup A

soGroup : (A : SpinAxioms) ‚Üí ‚àÄ p q ‚Üí Group (SO A p q)
soGroup A = SpinAxioms.soGroup A

spinCoversSO : (A : SpinAxioms) ‚Üí ‚àÄ (p q : Nat) ‚Üí DoubleCover (spinGroup A p q) (soGroup A p q)
spinCoversSO A = SpinAxioms.spinCoversSO A

-- Default instance (data-level placeholder).
spinAxiomsDefault : SpinAxioms
spinAxiomsDefault =
  record
    { SO = Œª _ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
    ; Spin = Œª _ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
    ; spinGroup = Œª _ _ ‚Üí
        record { e = tt ; _‚àô_ = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt ; inv = Œª _ ‚Üí tt }
    ; soGroup = Œª _ _ ‚Üí
        record { e = tt ; _‚àô_ = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt ; inv = Œª _ ‚Üí tt }
    ; spinCoversSO = Œª _ _ ‚Üí
        record
          { œÅ = record
              { f = Œª _ ‚Üí tt
              ; pres‚àô = Œª _ _ ‚Üí refl
              ; prese = refl
              }
          ; surj = tt
          ; twoTo1 = tt
          }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseGuardedStrict where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; _‚äî_; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric

-- Guarded strictness interface for conditional projections.
-- This is the ‚ÄúTemplate B‚Äù shape: strictness only in flow regime.
record GuardedStrictness : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    X : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric X
    P : X ‚Üí X

    Guard  : X ‚Üí Set
    Broken : X ‚Üí Set
    Snap   : X ‚Üí Set
    Restore : X ‚Üí X

    -- Flow regime: strictness on fibers (guarded).
    P-strict-on :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      Guard x ‚Üí Guard y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P x y ‚Üí
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d U (P x) (P y) < UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y

    -- Broken regime: restoration back into Guard.
    restore-normal-form :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Broken x ‚Üí Guard (Restore x)

    restore-idem :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore (Restore x) ‚â° Restore x

    restore-fixes :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (Restore x) ‚â° Restore x

open GuardedStrictness public

module DASHI.Physics.MaassRestorationShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.LiftToFullState as LFS
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticRenormalization as MQR using (tailOf-++; coarseOf-++)

-- Restoration: preserve coarse trunk and zero the tail.
restore·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
restore·µ£ {m} {k} x = LFS.embedCoarse m k (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

-- Tail of a restored state is canonical zeros.
tailOf-restore :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (restore·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° Data.Vec.replicate k zer
tailOf-restore {m} {k} x =
  MQR.tailOf-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (Data.Vec.replicate k zer)

-- Restoration is idempotent.
restore-idem :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  restore·µ£ {m} {k} (restore·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° restore·µ£ {m} {k} x
restore-idem {m} {k} x
  rewrite MQR.coarseOf-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (Data.Vec.replicate k zer)
  = refl

-- P·µ£ fixes restored states.
restore-fixes :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (restore·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° restore·µ£ {m} {k} x
restore-fixes {m} {k} x
  rewrite TCP.P·µ£-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (Data.Vec.replicate k zer)
        | TCP.projTail-replicate {k}
  = refl
module DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractive‚â¢; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS

open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder as CB
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue

record RealClosureKit : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    C P R : S ‚Üí S

    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractive‚â¢ U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    pres‚â¢R : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    fp : S
    fixedT : (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) fp ‚â° fp
    uniqueT : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) x ‚â° x ‚Üí x ‚â° fp

    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealClosureKit public

toRealStack : RealClosureKit ‚Üí CB.RealStack
toRealStack k =
  record
    { S = S k
    ; U = U k
    ; C = C k
    ; P = P k
    ; R = R k
    ; nonexpC = nonexpC k
    ; nonexpR = nonexpR k
    ; strictP = strictP k
    ; orderLaws = orderLaws k
    ; pres‚â¢R = pres‚â¢R k
    ; fp0 = fp k
    ; fixedT = fixedT k
    ; uniqueT = uniqueT k
    ; inv = inv k
    ; iso = iso k
    ; fs  = fs k
    }

closureAxioms : (k : RealClosureKit) ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
closureAxioms k = CB.buildClosure (toRealStack k)

module DASHI.Physics.RealCausalStructureInstance where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Causal structure based on locality predicate (finite speed)

localCausal : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí MCS.CausalStructure m
localCausal {m} =
  record
    { _‚âº_  = Œª x y ‚Üí RFSI.local {n = m} x y
    ; delta = Œª _ _ ‚Üí RTC.zeroVec {n = m}
    }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity for the locality-based causal structure

coneMonotone-local :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  MCS.CausalStructure._‚âº_ (localCausal {m}) x y ‚Üí
  (+ 0) ‚â§·µ¢ IMQ.QœÉ œÉ (MCS.CausalStructure.delta (localCausal {m}) x y)
coneMonotone-local œÉ x y h =
  IntP.‚â§-reflexive (sym (RCSI.QœÉ-zeroVec œÉ))
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftInstanceFine where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC using (Code; Severity)
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard as SG
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardedStrictFine as SGS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC

-- Shift carrier severity policy (code + thresholds).
record ShiftSeverityPolicyFine {m k : Nat} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    code·µ£ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Code
    safeThreshold·µ£ : Severity
    brokenThreshold·µ£ : Severity

  policy·µ£ : SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
  policy·µ£ = record
    { code = code·µ£
    ; safeThreshold = safeThreshold·µ£
    ; brokenThreshold = brokenThreshold·µ£
    }

open ShiftSeverityPolicyFine public

-- Guarded strictness bundle specialized to the shift carrier using dNatFine.
record ShiftSeverityGuardedStrictFine {m k : Nat} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    pol : ShiftSeverityPolicyFine {m} {k}

    P·µ£ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    Restore·µ£ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    d·µ£ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Nat

    P-strict-on :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicyFine.policy·µ£ pol) x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicyFine.policy·µ£ pol) y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P·µ£ x y ‚Üí
      d·µ£ (P·µ£ x) (P·µ£ y) < d·µ£ x y

    restore-normal-form :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      SG.Broken (ShiftSeverityPolicyFine.policy·µ£ pol) x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicyFine.policy·µ£ pol) (Restore·µ£ x)

    restore-idem :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore·µ£ (Restore·µ£ x) ‚â° Restore·µ£ x

    restore-fixes :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P·µ£ (Restore·µ£ x) ‚â° Restore·µ£ x

  guarded : SGS.SeverityGuardedStrictFine
  guarded = record
    { S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    ; policy = ShiftSeverityPolicyFine.policy·µ£ pol
    ; P‚Çõ = P·µ£
    ; Restore‚Çõ = Restore·µ£
    ; d‚Çõ = d·µ£
    ; P-strict-on‚Çõ = P-strict-on
    ; restore-normal-form‚Çõ = restore-normal-form
    ; restore-idem‚Çõ = restore-idem
    ; restore-fixes‚Çõ = restore-fixes
    }

open ShiftSeverityGuardedStrictFine public

module DASHI.Physics.Core where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; zero; suc)

-- Abstract metric space; swap in your concrete ultrametric if desired.
record MetricSpace (‚Ñì : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    X     : Set ‚Ñì
    d     : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì        -- use ‚Ñù-valued distance later if needed
    reflD : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí d x x
    sym   : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚Üí d y x
    -- triangle etc as needed

-- Contractive operator skeleton.
record ContractionOp {‚Ñì : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    T      : X ‚Üí X
    lam    : Set ‚Ñì               -- typically a scalar 0<Œª<1
    contractive : Set (suc ‚Ñì)    -- replace with your inequality form

-- Bilinear and quadratic forms kept abstract.
record Bilinear {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    B : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì

record Quadratic {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Q : V ‚Üí Set ‚Ñì

-- Involution / mirror.
record Involution {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Œπ    : V ‚Üí V
    invol : ‚àÄ v ‚Üí Œπ (Œπ v) ‚â° v

-- Finite speed / locality placeholder.
record FiniteSpeed {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    locality : Set ‚Ñì

-- Isotropy (rotation-like symmetries) and preservation of a quadratic form.
record Isotropy {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    G   : Set ‚Ñì
    act : G ‚Üí V ‚Üí V

record PreservesQuadratic {‚Ñì : Level} {V : Set ‚Ñì} (iso : Isotropy V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  open Isotropy iso
  field
    pres : ‚àÄ g v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (act g v) ‚â° Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Clifford-like algebra interface via universal property.
record CliffordLike {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Cl    : Set ‚Ñì
    embed : V ‚Üí Cl
    -- relations to be added in DecimationToClifford

-- Even subalgebra carrier.
record EvenSubalg {‚Ñì : Level} (A : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Even : Set ‚Ñì
    inc  : Even ‚Üí A

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedSplitQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+‚Ñ§_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- sum‚Ñ§ distributes over ++

sum‚Ñ§-++ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (xs : Vec ‚Ñ§ m) (ys : Vec ‚Ñ§ k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (xs ++ ys) ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys
sum‚Ñ§-++ [] ys =
  sym (IntP.+-identityÀ° (IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys))
sum‚Ñ§-++ (x ‚à∑ xs) ys =
  let
    sum‚Ñ§-cons : IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) ‚â° x +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs
    sum‚Ñ§-cons = refl
    step : x +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (xs ++ ys) ‚â° x +‚Ñ§ (IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys)
    step = cong (Œª z ‚Üí x +‚Ñ§ z) (sum‚Ñ§-++ xs ys)
    step2 : x +‚Ñ§ (IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys) ‚â° (x +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs) +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys
    step2 = sym (IntP.+-assoc x (IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs) (IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys))
    step3 : (x +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ xs) +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys
    step3 = cong (Œª z ‚Üí z +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ys) (sym sum‚Ñ§-cons)
  in
  trans step (trans step2 step3)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- zipWith distributes over ++

zipWith-++ :
  ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} (f : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C)
    {m k : Nat}
    (a‚ÇÅ : Vec A m) (a‚ÇÇ : Vec A k)
    (b‚ÇÅ : Vec B m) (b‚ÇÇ : Vec B k) ‚Üí
  zipWith f (a‚ÇÅ ++ a‚ÇÇ) (b‚ÇÅ ++ b‚ÇÇ) ‚â° (zipWith f a‚ÇÅ b‚ÇÅ) ++ (zipWith f a‚ÇÇ b‚ÇÇ)
zipWith-++ f [] a‚ÇÇ [] b‚ÇÇ = refl
zipWith-++ f (a ‚à∑ a‚ÇÅ) a‚ÇÇ (b ‚à∑ b‚ÇÅ) b‚ÇÇ =
  cong (Œª z ‚Üí f a b ‚à∑ z) (zipWith-++ f a‚ÇÅ a‚ÇÇ b‚ÇÅ b‚ÇÇ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic split: QœÉ splits over (coarse ++ tail)

QœÉ-split :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat)
    (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x
    ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k œÉ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +‚Ñ§ IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.tailOf   m k œÉ) (TCP.tailOf   m k x)
QœÉ-split m k œÉ x =
  let
    f = (Œª s t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s * IMQ.sq‚Ñ§ (IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit t))
    œÉc = TCP.coarseOf m k œÉ
    œÉt = TCP.tailOf m k œÉ
    xc = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    xt = TCP.tailOf m k x
    œÉ‚â° : œÉc ++ œÉt ‚â° œÉ
    œÉ‚â° = TCP.merge-split m k œÉ
    x‚â° : xc ++ xt ‚â° x
    x‚â° = TCP.merge-split m k x
    step1 : IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f (œÉc ++ œÉt) x)
    step1 = cong (Œª z ‚Üí IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f z x)) (sym œÉ‚â°)
    step2 : IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f (œÉc ++ œÉt) x) ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f (œÉc ++ œÉt) (xc ++ xt))
    step2 = cong (Œª z ‚Üí IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f (œÉc ++ œÉt) z)) (sym x‚â°)
    step3 : IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f (œÉc ++ œÉt) (xc ++ xt))
            ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ((zipWith f œÉc xc) ++ (zipWith f œÉt xt))
    step3 = cong IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith-++ f œÉc œÉt xc xt)
    step4 : IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ ((zipWith f œÉc xc) ++ (zipWith f œÉt xt))
            ‚â° IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f œÉc xc) +‚Ñ§ IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (zipWith f œÉt xt)
    step4 = sum‚Ñ§-++ (zipWith f œÉc xc) (zipWith f œÉt xt)
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4))

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EnergyShiftBase where

-- Preorder over Nat with ‚â§.
NatPreorder : E.Preorder
NatPreorder = record
  { S = Nat
  ; _‚â§_ = Data.Nat._‚â§_
  ; refl‚â§ = Œª _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-refl
  ; trans‚â§ = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-trans
  }

-- Energy = ultrametric distance.
energy-sep :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  E.Preorder._‚â§_ NatPreorder
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y)
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x x) ‚Üí
  x ‚â° y
energy-sep m k x y h =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    dxy = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y
    dxx = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x x
    dxx‚â°0 = UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U x
    h' : dxy Data.Nat.‚â§ 0
    h' = subst (Œª v ‚Üí dxy Data.Nat.‚â§ v) dxx‚â°0 h
    dxy‚â°0 : dxy ‚â° 0
    dxy‚â°0 = NatP.‚â§-antisym h' z‚â§n
  in
  FAM.dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq x y dxy‚â°0

EnergyShift : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí E.EnergySpace (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatPreorder
EnergyShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { E = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    ; E-refl = Œª _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-refl
    ; E-sep = energy-sep m k
    }

ProjShift : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí CP.Projection (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
ProjShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}
    ; idem = TCP.P·µ£-idem m k
    }

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock where

open import Level using (Level; zero; suc; _‚äî_)

-- Bundle empirical seams with witness policy and signature-lock evidence.
record EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock {‚Ñì} (W : Set ‚Ñì) {n : Nat} (V : Set)
  : Set (suc ‚Ñì ‚äî suc zero) where
  field
    empirical : PCE.PhysicsClosureEmpirical
    policy : WSP.WitnessSetPolicy W
    orbitProfile : SE.OrbitProfile V
    signatureEvidence : SLCSV.SignatureRankCSVEvidence {n}

open EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock public

signatureLock :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {W : Set ‚Ñì} {n : Nat} {V : Set}
  ‚Üí EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock W {n} V
  ‚Üí SE.SignatureLock {n} V
signatureLock bundle =
  SLCSV.signatureLockFromRank
    (orbitProfile bundle)
    (signatureEvidence bundle)

signature31FromEvidence :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {W : Set ‚Ñì} {n : Nat} {V : Set}
  (Q : MQ.MaskedQuadratic n)
  (bundle : EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock W {n} V)
  ‚Üí SLCSV.SignatureRankCSVEvidence.rank (signatureEvidence bundle) Q
  ‚Üí MQ.signatureTag Q ‚â° MQ.sig31
signature31FromEvidence Q bundle rk =
  SLCSV.signature31FromRank Q (orbitProfile bundle) (signatureEvidence bundle) rk
module DASHI.Physics.Closure.BetaSeamCSVEvidence where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc)
open import DASHI.Energy.Energy as E
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint as CP
open import DASHI.Geometry.DefectCollapse as DC
open import DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff as MDL
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.BetaSeamCertificates as BSC

-- Evidence bundle meant to be populated from CSV-derived proofs.
record BetaSeamCSVEvidence
  {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs ‚Ñìn ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx}
  {P : E.Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  {O : MDL.OrderedMonoid {‚Ñìn}}
  (ES : E.EnergySpace X P)
  (Pr : CP.Projection X)
  (Ecod : Set ‚Ñìe)
  (Parts : MDL.MDLParts X O)
  (Trade : MDL.TradeoffLemma Parts)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìn ‚äî ‚Ñìe)) where
  field
    fejer : CP.FejerMonotone ES Pr
    closest : CP.ClosestPoint ES Pr
    defectCollapse : DC.DefectCollapse X Ecod
    mdlDescent : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      MDL.OrderedMonoid._‚â§_ O (MDL.MDLParts.MDL Parts (MDL.MDLParts.T Parts x))
                                (MDL.MDLParts.MDL Parts x)

open BetaSeamCSVEvidence public

betaSeamsFromEvidence :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìx ‚Ñìs ‚Ñìn ‚Ñìe}
  {X : Set ‚Ñìx}
  {P : E.Preorder {‚Ñìs}}
  {O : MDL.OrderedMonoid {‚Ñìn}}
  (ES : E.EnergySpace X P)
  (Pr : CP.Projection X)
  (Ecod : Set ‚Ñìe)
  (Parts : MDL.MDLParts X O)
  (Trade : MDL.TradeoffLemma Parts)
  (Ev : BetaSeamCSVEvidence ES Pr Ecod Parts Trade)
  ‚Üí BSC.BetaSeams ES Pr Ecod Parts Trade
betaSeamsFromEvidence ES Pr Ecod Parts Trade Ev =
  record
    { fejer = BetaSeamCSVEvidence.fejer Ev
    ; closest = BetaSeamCSVEvidence.closest Ev
    ; defectCollapse = BetaSeamCSVEvidence.defectCollapse Ev
    ; mdlDescent = BetaSeamCSVEvidence.mdlDescent Ev
    }

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLFejerAxiomsShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)

private
  Parts : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.MDLParts (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) MSI.NatOrderedMonoid
  Parts {m} {k} = MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}

  Trade : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.TradeoffLemma (Parts {m} {k})
  Trade {m} {k} = MSI.TradeoffShift {m} {k}

-- Formalizes the empirical finding: MDL-style energy is Fej√©r/monotone
-- under the shift operator (closest-point geometry, not raw œá¬≤).
record MDLFejerAxiomsShift : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    mdlFejer :
      ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
      (MDL.MDLParts.MDL (Parts {m} {k})
        (MDL.MDLParts.T (Parts {m} {k}) x))
      ‚â§
      (MDL.MDLParts.MDL (Parts {m} {k}) x)

open MDLFejerAxiomsShift public

-- Concrete instance: derived from the tradeoff-based MDL descent proof.
mdlFejerShift : MDLFejerAxiomsShift
mdlFejerShift =
  record
    { mdlFejer = Œª {m} {k} x ‚Üí
        MDL.MDLDescent (Parts {m} {k}) (Trade {m} {k}) x
    }
module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLLyapunovShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)

-- Lyapunov instance for the shift stack, using the MDL tradeoff descent.
lyapunovShift : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí OldMDL.Lyapunov {S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)} (MDLParts.T (MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}))
lyapunovShift {m} {k} =
  let
    Parts = MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}
  in
  record
    { L = MDLParts.MDL Parts
    ; descent = MDL.MDLDescent Parts (MSI.TradeoffShift {m} {k})
    }
module DASHI.Physics.Closure.DefectCollapseShiftInstance where

-- Defect = tail; energy = countNZ on tail; T = T·µ£
defectCollapseShift :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  DC.DefectCollapse (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) Nat
defectCollapseShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { D = Œª x ‚Üí x
    ; T = TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}
    ; _‚â§_ = Data.Nat._‚â§_
    ; energy = Œª x ‚Üí MSI.countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; collapse = MSI.resid-drop-lemma {m} {k}
    }
module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong; trans; subst; sym)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_; _‚â§_; zero; z‚â§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚â§-refl; ‚â§-trans; +-mono-‚â§; +-identity ≥; +-identityÀ°; +-assoc; m‚â§n+m)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Vec as V using (replicate)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (init; _‚à∑ ≥_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_; proj‚ÇÇ)

open import DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff as MDL using (OrderedMonoid; MDLParts; TradeoffLemma)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

-- Ordered monoid over Nat with + and ‚â§.
NatOrderedMonoid : MDL.OrderedMonoid
NatOrderedMonoid = record
  { M = record
      { N = Nat
      ; _+_ = Data.Nat._+_
      ; 0# = zero
      }
  ; _‚â§_ = Data.Nat._‚â§_
  ; refl‚â§ = Œª _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-refl
  ; trans‚â§ = Œª _ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-trans
  ; mono+ = Œª a b c d le1 le2 ‚Üí NatP.+-mono-‚â§ le1 le2
  }

-- Simple nontrivial length: count nonzero trits.
nz : Trit ‚Üí Nat
nz neg = 1
nz zer = 0
nz pos = 1

countNZ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
countNZ [] = 0
countNZ (x ‚à∑ xs) = nz x + countNZ xs

countNZ-snoc :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  countNZ (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a) ‚â° countNZ xs + nz a
countNZ-snoc [] a =
  trans (NatP.+-identity ≥ (nz a))
        (sym (NatP.+-identityÀ° (nz a)))
countNZ-snoc (x ‚à∑ xs) a =
  trans (cong (Œª k ‚Üí nz x + k) (countNZ-snoc xs a))
        (sym (NatP.+-assoc (nz x) (countNZ xs) (nz a)))

-- CountNZ of an all-zero tail is zero.
countNZ-replicate-zer :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí countNZ (V.replicate k zer) ‚â° 0
countNZ-replicate-zer {zero} = refl
countNZ-replicate-zer {suc k} =
  trans
    (cong (Œª n ‚Üí nz zer + n) (countNZ-replicate-zer {k}))
    (sym (NatP.+-identity ≥ 0))

countNZ-init‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí countNZ (init t) ‚â§ countNZ t
countNZ-init‚â§ {zero} (x ‚à∑ []) = z‚â§n
countNZ-init‚â§ {suc k} (x ‚à∑ y ‚à∑ ys) =
  NatP.+-mono-‚â§ (NatP.‚â§-refl {nz x}) (countNZ-init‚â§ (y ‚à∑ ys))

projTail-def :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.projTail t ‚â° (init t ‚à∑ ≥ zer)
projTail-def t = refl

shiftTail-def :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.shiftTail (x ‚à∑ xs) ‚â° xs ‚à∑ ≥ zer
shiftTail-def x xs = refl

countNZ-projTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.projTail t) ‚â§ countNZ t
countNZ-projTail‚â§ {zero} [] = NatP.‚â§-refl
countNZ-projTail‚â§ {suc k} t
  rewrite projTail-def t
        | countNZ-snoc (init t) zer
        | NatP.+-identity ≥ (countNZ (init t))
  = countNZ-init‚â§ t

countNZ-shiftTail‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.shiftTail t) ‚â§ countNZ t
countNZ-shiftTail‚â§ {zero} [] = NatP.‚â§-refl
countNZ-shiftTail‚â§ {suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs)
  rewrite shiftTail-def x xs
        | countNZ-snoc xs zer
        | NatP.+-identity ≥ (countNZ xs)
  = NatP.m‚â§n+m (countNZ xs) (nz x)

countNZ-tailStep‚â§ :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.tailStep t) ‚â§ countNZ t
countNZ-tailStep‚â§ t =
  NatP.‚â§-trans (countNZ-projTail‚â§ (TCP.shiftTail t)) (countNZ-shiftTail‚â§ t)

tailOf-P·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.projTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-P·µ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.P·µ£-++ m k c t
        | TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-T·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.tailStep (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-T·µ£ m k x =
  cong Data.Product.proj‚ÇÇ (TCP.split-T·µ£ m k x)

resid-drop-lemma :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚â§ countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
resid-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite tailOf-T·µ£ m k x
  = countNZ-tailStep‚â§ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

coarse-invariant-R :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

coarseOf-PT-‚â°-P :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚â°
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)
coarseOf-PT-‚â°-P m k x =
  let
    p-idem = TCP.P·µ£-idem m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    cPT : TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚â°
          TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    cPT = cong (TCP.coarseOf m k) p-idem
    cT  = coarse-invariant-T m k x
    cP  = coarse-invariant-P m k x
  in
  trans cPT (trans cT (sym cP))

model-drop-lemma :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)))
    ‚â§ countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x))
model-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite coarseOf-PT-‚â°-P m k x
  = NatP.‚â§-refl

-- MDL parts: model length = countNZ of coarse, residual length = countNZ of tail.
MDLPartsShift : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.MDLParts (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatOrderedMonoid
MDLPartsShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}
    ; D = Œª x ‚Üí x
    ; T = TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}
    ; ModelLen = Œª x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; ResidLen = Œª x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL = Œª x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)) + countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL-def = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
    }

-- Fej√©r/ClosestPoint seams (to be discharged by real proofs later).
fejerShift :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  CP.FejerMonotone (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
fejerShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { fejer = Œª x y fix ‚Üí
        let
          U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
          ne = ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}
          step = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp ne x y
        in
        subst (Œª v ‚Üí Data.Nat._‚â§_
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) v)
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y))
              fix
              step
    }

fejer‚áíclosestShift :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
    CP.FixP (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k}) y ‚Üí
    Data.Nat._‚â§_
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x))
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x y)
fejer‚áíclosestShift {m} {k} x y fix =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    d = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U
    tri : Data.Nat._‚â§_ (d x (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)) (d x y ‚äî d y (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x))
    tri = UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle U x y (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    sym1 : d y (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° d (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) y
    sym1 = UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric U y (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    fejer-bound :
      Data.Nat._‚â§_ (d (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) y) (d x y)
    fejer-bound =
      CP.FejerMonotone.fejer (fejerShift {m} {k}) x y fix
    max-bound : Data.Nat._‚â§_ (d x y ‚äî d y (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x)) (d x y)
    max-bound =
      NatP.‚äî-lub
        (NatP.‚â§-refl)
        (subst (Œª v ‚Üí Data.Nat._‚â§_ v (d x y)) (sym sym1) fejer-bound)
  in
  NatP.‚â§-trans tri max-bound

closestAxiomsShift : CPA.ClosestPointAxiomsShift
closestAxiomsShift =
  record
    { closestAxiomShift =
        Œª {m} {k} ‚Üí
          record
            { fejer = fejerShift {m} {k}
            ; fejer‚áíclosest = fejer‚áíclosestShift {m} {k}
            }
    }

closestShift :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  CP.ClosestPoint (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
closestShift {m} {k} =
  FC.closestFromFejer (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
    (CPA.closestAxiomShift closestAxiomsShift {m} {k})

module DASHI.Physics.TOperator where

_‚àò_ : ‚àÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí A ‚Üí C
(f ‚àò g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _‚àò_

-- Real operator scaffold: T = C ‚àò P ‚àò R
record TOperator (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    C : S ‚Üí S
    P : S ‚Üí S
    R : S ‚Üí S

  T : S ‚Üí S
  T = C ‚àò (P ‚àò R)

  field
    involutionCommutes : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      TOperator.T op (Involution.Œπ inv x) ‚â° Involution.Œπ inv (TOperator.T op x)

QœÉ-zeroVec :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ œÉ (RTC.zeroVec {n = m}) ‚â° (+ 0)

        | IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s)

countMinus-oneMinus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí SFM.countMinus (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚â° suc 0
countMinus-oneMinus {m} =
  cong suc (SFM.countMinus-replicatePlus {m})

noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí ¬¨ MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m})
noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h
  rewrite countMinus-oneMinus {m}
  with h
... | s‚â§s ()

twoTimeLike‚ÜínoUniqueFP-oneMinus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (T : Vec Trit (suc m) ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc m)) ‚Üí
  MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ MCS.UniqueFixedPoint T
twoTimeLike‚ÜínoUniqueFP-oneMinus {m} T h =
  Œª _ ‚Üí noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticInvariance where

-- Canonicalization preserves masked quadratic

  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractive‚â¢; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue

-- Concrete data needed to build a real closure instance.
record RealStack : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    -- Operator components
    C : S ‚Üí S
    P : S ‚Üí S
    R : S ‚Üí S

    -- Contraction composition inputs
    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractive‚â¢ U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    pres‚â¢R : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    -- Fixed point witnesses for T
    fp0 : S
    fixedT : TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) fp0 ‚â° fp0
    uniqueT : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) x ‚â° x ‚Üí x ‚â° fp0

    -- Symmetry / locality
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealStack public

-- Build T from components.
mkOp : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí TOp.TOperator (S stk)
mkOp stk = record { C = C stk ; P = P stk ; R = R stk }

T : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí S stk ‚Üí S stk
T stk = TOp.TOperator.T (mkOp stk)

-- Strict contraction for T by composition.
contractiveT : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí Contractive‚â¢ (U stk) (T stk)
contractiveT stk =
  SCC.composeStrict
    (U stk)
    (C stk) (R stk) (P stk)
    (orderLaws stk)
    (nonexpC stk)
    (nonexpR stk)
    (pres‚â¢R stk)
    (strictP stk)

-- Build the StrictContraction record for T.
strictT : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí StrictContraction (U stk) (T stk)
strictT stk =
  record
    { contractive‚â¢ = contractiveT stk
    ; fp = fp0 stk
    ; fixed = fixedT stk
    ; unique = uniqueT stk
    }

-- Final closure instance.
buildClosure : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
buildClosure stk =
  record
    { S   = S stk
    ; U   = U stk
    ; T   = T stk
    ; sc  = strictT stk
    ; inv = inv stk
    ; iso = RIS.RealIsotropy.iso (iso stk)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.local (fs stk)
        ; preservesLocality = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs stk)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ContractionToQuadratic where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Unit.Polymorphic as PU using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.Core

-- A ‚Äúkernel symmetry‚Äù / invariance predicate.
record Invariant {‚Ñì : Level} {V : Set ‚Ñì} (T : V ‚Üí V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    inv : ‚àÄ v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (T v) ‚â° Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Existence witness for a quadratic form.
record QuadraticWitness {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    Q : Quadratic V

-- Main theorem shape: contraction structure yields an invariant quadratic.
record ContractionForcesQuadratic {‚Ñì : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    toV      : X ‚Üí X            -- placeholder if your V is X itself
    theorem  :
      (C : ContractionOp M) ‚Üí
      Œ£ (QuadraticWitness X) (Œª W ‚Üí Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q W))

-- Stronger ‚Äúadmissible quadratic‚Äù interface that bundles all invariances.
record AdmissibleQuadratic
       {‚Ñì : Level}
       (V   : Set ‚Ñì)
       (T   : V ‚Üí V)
       (iso : Isotropy V)
       (Œπ   : Involution V)
       (fs  : FiniteSpeed V)
       : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  field
    Q                  : Quadratic V
    invariantUnderT    : Invariant T Q
    invariantUnderIso  : PreservesQuadratic iso Q
    involutionCompat   : ‚àÄ v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (Involution.Œπ Œπ v) ‚â° Quadratic.Q Q v
    finiteSpeedCompat  : FiniteSpeed.locality fs

-- Uniqueness up to scale / gauge.
record UniqueUpToScale {‚Ñì : Level} (V : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    uniq : Set ‚Ñì

record ContractionForcesQuadraticAxioms {‚Ñì : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  field
    witness : ContractionForcesQuadratic M

contraction‚áíinvariantQuadratic :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì} ‚Üí
  ContractionForcesQuadraticAxioms M ‚Üí
  ContractionForcesQuadratic M
contraction‚áíinvariantQuadratic ax =
  ContractionForcesQuadraticAxioms.witness ax

record AdmissibleQuadraticUniquenessAxioms
       {‚Ñì : Level}
       {V : Set ‚Ñì}
       {T   : V ‚Üí V}
       {iso : Isotropy V}
       {Œπ   : Involution V}
       {fs  : FiniteSpeed V} : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  field
    uniq :
      (Q‚ÇÅ Q‚ÇÇ : AdmissibleQuadratic V T iso Œπ fs) ‚Üí
      UniqueUpToScale V

admissibleQuadraticUnique :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {V : Set ‚Ñì}
    {T   : V ‚Üí V}
    {iso : Isotropy V}
    {Œπ   : Involution V}
    {fs  : FiniteSpeed V} ‚Üí
    AdmissibleQuadraticUniquenessAxioms {V = V} {T = T} {iso = iso} {Œπ = Œπ} {fs = fs} ‚Üí
    (Q‚ÇÅ Q‚ÇÇ : AdmissibleQuadratic V T iso Œπ fs) ‚Üí
    UniqueUpToScale V
admissibleQuadraticUnique ax = AdmissibleQuadraticUniquenessAxioms.uniq ax

record ContractionUniqueQuadraticAxioms {‚Ñì : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ñì)) where
  field
    unique :
      (C : ContractionOp M) ‚Üí
      UniqueUpToScale (MetricSpace.X M)

contraction‚áíuniqueQuadraticUpToScale :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñì} {M : MetricSpace ‚Ñì} ‚Üí
  ContractionUniqueQuadraticAxioms M ‚Üí
  (C : ContractionOp M) ‚Üí
  UniqueUpToScale (MetricSpace.X M)
contraction‚áíuniqueQuadraticUpToScale ax =
  ContractionUniqueQuadraticAxioms.unique ax

module DASHI.Physics.Holography.AreaLaw where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _‚â§_; _*_; _^_)

-- Minimal area/volume/entropy interface.
record RegionCounts : Set‚ÇÅ where

    admCount : Region ‚Üí ‚Ñï

-- Area-law style bound: admissible count grows at most exponentially in boundary area.
AreaLaw : RegionCounts ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí Set
