module DASHI.Physics.RealOperators where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-involutive)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer; inv; neg; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _‚â•_; z‚â§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail is fine detail: projection zeroes the last digit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n)
setHead (_ ‚à∑ xs) = zer ‚à∑ xs

P·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
P·µ£ {zero} [] = []
P·µ£ {suc n} x = reverse (setHead (reverse x))

-- Canonicalization / renormalization (currently identity).
C·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
C·µ£ x = x

R·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
R·µ£ x = x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution commutation lemmas for P·µ£.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead-inv : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí
  map inv (setHead xs) ‚â° setHead (map inv xs)
setHead-inv (x ‚à∑ xs) = refl

invVec-P·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (P·µ£ x) ‚â° P·µ£ (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-P·µ£ {zero} [] = refl
invVec-P·µ£ {suc n} x =
  let
    rx = reverse x
  in
  trans
    (map-reverse inv (setHead rx))
    (trans
      (cong reverse (setHead-inv rx))
      (cong (Œª v ‚Üí reverse (setHead v)) (map-reverse inv x))
    )

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive proofs under the fine agreement metric.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

agreeDepthFine-nondecrease :
  ‚àÄ {n : Nat} (x y : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  FAM.agreeDepthFine (P·µ£ x) (P·µ£ y) ‚â• FAM.agreeDepthFine x y
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {zero} [] [] = z‚â§n
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {suc n} x y
  rewrite reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse x))
        | reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse y))
  = lemma (reverse x) (reverse y)
  where
    lemma : ‚àÄ {m} (rx ry : Vec Trit (suc m)) ‚Üí
      AM.agreeDepth (setHead rx) (setHead ry) ‚â• AM.agreeDepth rx ry
    lemma (neg ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) = NatP.‚â§-refl
    lemma (zer ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) = NatP.‚â§-refl
    lemma (pos ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) = NatP.‚â§-refl
    lemma (neg ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n
    lemma (neg ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n
    lemma (zer ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n
    lemma (zer ‚à∑ as) (pos ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n
    lemma (pos ‚à∑ as) (neg ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n
    lemma (pos ‚à∑ as) (zer ‚à∑ bs) = z‚â§n

nonexpP·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (P·µ£ {n})
nonexpP·µ£ {n} =
  record
    { nonexp = Œª x y ‚Üí
        let
          depth‚â• = agreeDepthFine-nondecrease x y
        in
        NatP.‚à∏-mono (NatP.‚â§-refl {n}) depth‚â•
    }

nonexpC·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (C·µ£ {n})
nonexpC·µ£ {n} = record { nonexp = Œª _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-refl }

nonexpR·µ£ : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (R·µ£ {n})
nonexpR·µ£ {n} = record { nonexp = Œª _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚â§-refl }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarizationCoreInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _+_; _-_; _*_; +_; -_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Data.Integer.Tactic.RingSolver as IntRS
import Tactic.RingSolver.NonReflective as NR

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization as OP
open import DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization as QP

open QP.‚Ñ§-Reasoning

module RingZ = NR IntRS.ring
open RingZ using (Expr; Œö; Œô; _‚äï_; _‚äó_; ‚äù_; _‚äú_; solve)

-- Scalar field instance for ‚Ñ§ (minimal, for polarization only).
ScalarField‚Ñ§ : ScalarField _
ScalarField‚Ñ§ =
  record
    { S = ‚Ñ§
    ; _+s_ = _+_
    ; _*s_ = _*_
    ; 0s = + 0
    ; 1s = + 1
    ; -s_ = -_
    }

-- Proof: QÃÇcore(x+y) = QÃÇcore x + QÃÇcore y + 2¬∑dot x y  (for ‚Ñ§ vectors).
square-sum :
  ‚àÄ (x y : ‚Ñ§) ‚Üí
    (x + y) * (x + y) ‚â° (x * x + y * y) + ((+ 2) * (x * y))
square-sum x y =
  RingZ.solve 2
    (Œª x y ‚Üí
       ( ((x ‚äï y) ‚äó (x ‚äï y))
       , ((x ‚äó x ‚äï y ‚äó y) ‚äï ((Œö (+ 2)) ‚äó (x ‚äó y))) ))
    refl x y

rearrange :
  ‚àÄ (x2 y2 xy qx qy dot : ‚Ñ§) ‚Üí
    (x2 + y2 + ((+ 2) * xy)) + (qx + qy + ((+ 2) * dot))
      ‚â°
    (x2 + qx) + (y2 + qy) + ((+ 2) * (xy + dot))
rearrange x2 y2 xy qx qy dot =
  RingZ.solve 6
    (Œª x2 y2 xy qx qy dot ‚Üí
       ( ((x2 ‚äï y2 ‚äï (Œö (+ 2) ‚äó xy)) ‚äï (qx ‚äï qy ‚äï (Œö (+ 2) ‚äó dot)))
       , ((x2 ‚äï qx) ‚äï (y2 ‚äï qy) ‚äï (Œö (+ 2) ‚äó (xy ‚äï dot))) ))
    refl x2 y2 xy qx qy dot

polarization-core :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (x y : Vec ‚Ñ§ m) ‚Üí
    QP.QÃÇcore (QP._+·µ•_ x y)
      ‚â°
    (QP.QÃÇcore x + QP.QÃÇcore y)
      + ((+ 2) * QP.dot‚Ñ§ x y)
polarization-core {m = Nat.zero} [] [] = refl
polarization-core {m = Nat.suc n} (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  begin
    QP.QÃÇcore (QP._+·µ•_ (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    ((x + y) * (x + y)) + QP.QÃÇcore (QP._+·µ•_ xs ys)
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí t + QP.QÃÇcore (QP._+·µ•_ xs ys)) (square-sum x y) ‚ü©
    ((x * x + y * y) + ((+ 2) * (x * y))) + QP.QÃÇcore (QP._+·µ•_ xs ys)
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí ((x * x + y * y) + ((+ 2) * (x * y))) + t)
          (polarization-core xs ys) ‚ü©
    ((x * x + y * y) + ((+ 2) * (x * y))) +
    ((QP.QÃÇcore xs + QP.QÃÇcore ys) + ((+ 2) * QP.dot‚Ñ§ xs ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® rearrange (x * x) (y * y) (x * y) (QP.QÃÇcore xs) (QP.QÃÇcore ys) (QP.dot‚Ñ§ xs ys) ‚ü©
    (x * x + QP.QÃÇcore xs) + (y * y + QP.QÃÇcore ys) + ((+ 2) * (x * y + QP.dot‚Ñ§ xs ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QP.QÃÇcore (x ‚à∑ xs) + QP.QÃÇcore (y ‚à∑ ys)) + ((+ 2) * QP.dot‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys))
  ‚àé

-- Polarization instance for Qcore‚Ñ§ using the dot product over ‚Ñ§.
polarizationCore :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí
  OP.Polarization (record
    { Carrier = Vec ‚Ñ§ m
    ; _+_ = QP._+·µ•_
    ; 0# = QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}
    ; -_ = Œª v ‚Üí v  -- additive inverse not used in polarization proof here
    })
    ScalarField‚Ñ§
polarizationCore {m} =
  record
    { Q = QP.QÃÇcore
    ; ‚ü™_,_‚ü´ = QP.dot‚Ñ§
    ; two = + 2
    ; two-def = refl
    ; polarization = polarization-core
    }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; cong‚ÇÇ; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_)
import Data.Integer.Tactic.RingSolver as IntRS
import Tactic.RingSolver.NonReflective as NR

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module ‚Ñ§-Reasoning = EqR IntP.‚â°-setoid
open ‚Ñ§-Reasoning

module Ring = NR IntRS.ring
open Ring using (Expr; Œö; Œô; _‚äï_; _‚äó_; ‚äù_; _‚äú_; solve)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit ‚Üí ‚Ñ§ embedding (for polarization we want ‚Ñ§, not Trit)

intOfTrit : Trit ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
intOfTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
intOfTrit zer = + 0
intOfTrit pos = + 1

vec‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m
vec‚Ñ§ = map intOfTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ‚Ñ§ vector ops

_+·µ•_ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m
_+·µ•_ = zipWith _+_

dot‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
dot‚Ñ§ []       []       = + 0
dot‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) = (x * y) + dot‚Ñ§ xs ys

sum‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sum‚Ñ§ []       = + 0
sum‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs) = x + sum‚Ñ§ xs

replicateTrit0 : (m : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit m
replicateTrit0 zero    = []
replicateTrit0 (suc n) = zer ‚à∑ replicateTrit0 n

zeroVec‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m
zeroVec‚Ñ§ {zero} = []
zeroVec‚Ñ§ {suc m} = + 0 ‚à∑ zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}

vec‚Ñ§-replicateTrit0 :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m) ‚â° zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}
vec‚Ñ§-replicateTrit0 {zero} = refl
vec‚Ñ§-replicateTrit0 {suc m} = cong (Œª t ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚à∑ t) (vec‚Ñ§-replicateTrit0 {m})

zeroVec‚Ñ§+·µ• :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (v : Vec ‚Ñ§ m) ‚Üí zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m} +·µ• v ‚â° v
zeroVec‚Ñ§+·µ• {zero} [] = refl
zeroVec‚Ñ§+·µ• {suc m} (x ‚à∑ xs) =
  cong‚ÇÇ _‚à∑_ (IntP.+-identityÀ° x) (zeroVec‚Ñ§+·µ• {m} xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic form on core: sum of squares in ‚Ñ§

Qcore‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
Qcore‚Ñ§ {m} x =
  let v = vec‚Ñ§ x in
  sum‚Ñ§ (map (Œª z ‚Üí z * z) v)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correct polarization over the ‚Ñ§-embedding:
-- B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§(Q)(x,y) = QÃÇ(v(x)+v(y)) - QÃÇ(v(x)) - QÃÇ(v(y))
-- where QÃÇ is a quadratic on Vec ‚Ñ§ m.

QÃÇcore : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
QÃÇcore v = sum‚Ñ§ (map (Œª z ‚Üí z * z) v)

B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m : Nat}
    ‚Üí (QÃÇ : Vec ‚Ñ§ m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§)
    ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇ x y =
  (QÃÇ (vec‚Ñ§ x +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ y)) - (QÃÇ (vec‚Ñ§ x)) - (QÃÇ (vec‚Ñ§ y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helpers for constructive polarization

-- Scalar polarization identity, specialized to trits.
-- We prove by case split over (neg/zer/pos) √ó (neg/zer/pos);
-- all goals reduce by computation.

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) ‚Üí
  (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b) * (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b)
    - (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit a)
    - (intOfTrit b * intOfTrit b)
    ‚â° (+ 2) * (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

split-B‚ÇÇ :
  (A R X RX Y RY : ‚Ñ§) ‚Üí
  (A + R) - (X + RX) - (Y + RY) ‚â° (A - X - Y) + (R - RX - RY)
split-B‚ÇÇ A R X RX Y RY =
  Ring.solve 6
    (Œª A R X RX Y RY ‚Üí
       ( ((A ‚äï R) ‚äï (‚äù (X ‚äï RX)) ‚äï (‚äù (Y ‚äï RY)))
       , ((A ‚äï (‚äù X) ‚äï (‚äù Y)) ‚äï (R ‚äï (‚äù RX) ‚äï (‚äù RY))) ))
    refl A R X RX Y RY
------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sanity property for QÃÇcore (constructive)

QÃÇcore-zero :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m)) ‚â° + 0
QÃÇcore-zero {zero} = refl
QÃÇcore-zero {suc m} =
  cong (Œª n ‚Üí (+ 0 * + 0) + n) (QÃÇcore-zero {m})

B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-zeroL :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (x : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore (replicateTrit0 m) x ‚â° + 0
B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-zeroL {m} x =
  begin
    B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore (replicateTrit0 m) x
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m) +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ x)) - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª v ‚Üí QÃÇcore v - QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m)) - QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
        (trans (cong (Œª t ‚Üí t +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ x) (vec‚Ñ§-replicateTrit0 {m}))
               (zeroVec‚Ñ§+·µ• (vec‚Ñ§ x))) ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)) - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª z ‚Üí QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x) - z - QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
        (QÃÇcore-zero {m}) ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)) - (+ 0) - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x) + (- (+ 0))) + (- QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x) + t + (- QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)))
        (refl) ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x) + (+ 0)) + (- QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí t + (- QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)))
        (IntP.+-identity ≥ (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))) ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)) + (- QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x))
  ‚â°‚ü® IntP.+-inverse ≥ (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ x)) ‚ü©
    + 0
  ‚àé

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Main target theorem to chase:
-- For QÃÇcore(v)=‚àë v·µ¢¬≤ we should have:
--   B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore x y = 2 * dot‚Ñ§ (vec‚Ñ§ x) (vec‚Ñ§ y)

B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-QÃÇcore-dot2 :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore x y ‚â° ((+ 2) * dot‚Ñ§ (vec‚Ñ§ x) (vec‚Ñ§ y))
B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-QÃÇcore-dot2 [] [] =
  begin
    B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore [] []
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    + 0
  ‚â°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-zero ≥ (+ 2)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (+ 0)
  ‚àé
B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-QÃÇcore-dot2 (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  begin
    B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QÃÇcore ((vec‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs)) +·µ• (vec‚Ñ§ (y ‚à∑ ys))))
      - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (x ‚à∑ xs)))
      - (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ (y ‚à∑ ys)))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      + QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ ys))
      - ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x) + QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs))
      - ((intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y) + QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® split-B‚ÇÇ
        ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y))
        (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ ys))
        (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
        (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs))
        (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y)
        (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ ys)) ‚ü©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      - (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
      - (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y))
      + (QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs +·µ• vec‚Ñ§ ys) - QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ xs) - QÃÇcore (vec‚Ñ§ ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí t + (B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore xs ys)) (b2-trit x y) ‚ü©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + (B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§ QÃÇcore xs ys)
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + t) (B‚ÇÇ‚Ñ§-QÃÇcore-dot2 xs ys) ‚ü©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + ((+ 2) * dot‚Ñ§ (vec‚Ñ§ xs) (vec‚Ñ§ ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-distribÀ°-+ (+ 2) (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) (dot‚Ñ§ (vec‚Ñ§ xs) (vec‚Ñ§ ys))) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) + dot‚Ñ§ (vec‚Ñ§ xs) (vec‚Ñ§ ys))
  ‚àé
  where
    open ‚Ñ§-Reasoning
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputedTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List.Base using (List; []; _‚à∑_; map; filter·µá; length)
open import Relation.Nullary using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (_‚â§?_)
open import Data.Integer.Base using (‚Ñ§; +_; -1‚Ñ§)
open import Data.Integer using (_‚âü_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; head; tail)
open import Data.Fin as Fin using (Fin)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate as OSP
open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA
open import DASHI.Physics.ShellOrbitProfileGenerator as SOPG
open import DASHI.Geometry.ShiftIsotropyTailPerm as TP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n (3^n)

concat : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List (List A) ‚Üí List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs ‚à∑ xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x ‚à∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚à∑ (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : ‚àÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí List B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg ‚à∑ zer ‚à∑ pos ‚à∑ []

allVecTrit : ‚àÄ (n : Nat) ‚Üí List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] ‚à∑ []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (Œª t ‚Üí map (Œª v ‚Üí t ‚à∑ v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Vec Trit (needed for orbit partitioning)

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (Œª eq ‚Üí neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (Œª eq ‚Üí neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell list and orbit sizes

isShell1 : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Bool
isShell1 œÉ x with IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚âü (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚âü -1‚Ñ§
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} œÉ = filter·µá (isShell1 œÉ) (allVecTrit m)

member : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí ((x y : A) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)) ‚Üí A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y ‚à∑ ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí ((x y : A) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x ‚à∑ xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x ‚à∑ nub dec xs

orbitSizes :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  List (TP.Perm k) ‚Üí
  List (Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  List Nat
orbitSizes {m} {k} ps xs =
  map (Œª x ‚Üí length (nub decEqVec (map (Œª p ‚Üí TP.actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ps))) xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sort sizes descending (simple insertion sort)

insertDesc : Nat ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x ‚à∑ []
insertDesc x (y ‚à∑ ys) with x NatP.‚â§? y
... | yes _ = y ‚à∑ insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x ‚à∑ y ‚à∑ ys

sortDesc : List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x ‚à∑ xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile under tail permutations

allPerms : (k : Nat) ‚Üí List (TP.Perm k)
allPerms zero = [] ‚à∑ []
allPerms (suc zero) =
  let f0 : Fin 1
      f0 = Fin.zero
  in (f0 ‚à∑ []) ‚à∑ []
allPerms (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) =
  let
    f0 : Fin 4
    f0 = Fin.zero
    f1 : Fin 4
    f1 = Fin.suc Fin.zero
    f2 : Fin 4
    f2 = Fin.suc (Fin.suc Fin.zero)
    f3 : Fin 4
    f3 = Fin.suc (Fin.suc (Fin.suc Fin.zero))

    -- all 24 permutations of [f0,f1,f2,f3]
    p0  = f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p1  = f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p2  = f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p3  = f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []
    p4  = f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p5  = f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []

    p6  = f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p7  = f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p8  = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p9  = f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []
    p10 = f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p11 = f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []

    p12 = f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p13 = f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []
    p14 = f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ []
    p15 = f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []
    p16 = f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []
    p17 = f2 ‚à∑ f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []

    p18 = f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p19 = f3 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []
    p20 = f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ []
    p21 = f3 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []
    p22 = f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ []
    p23 = f3 ‚à∑ f2 ‚à∑ f1 ‚à∑ f0 ‚à∑ []
  in
  p0  ‚à∑ p1  ‚à∑ p2  ‚à∑ p3  ‚à∑ p4  ‚à∑ p5  ‚à∑
  p6  ‚à∑ p7  ‚à∑ p8  ‚à∑ p9  ‚à∑ p10 ‚à∑ p11 ‚à∑
  p12 ‚à∑ p13 ‚à∑ p14 ‚à∑ p15 ‚à∑ p16 ‚à∑ p17 ‚à∑
  p18 ‚à∑ p19 ‚à∑ p20 ‚à∑ p21 ‚à∑ p22 ‚à∑ p23 ‚à∑ []
allPerms _ = []

orbitProfileTailPerm :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k) ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile (m + k)
orbitProfileTailPerm {m} {k} œÉ =
  let
    shell = shell1List œÉ
    sizes = orbitSizes {m} {k} (allPerms k) shell
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted (sortDesc sizes)

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardedStrict where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

-- Adapter: build Guard/Broken/Snap from a SeverityPolicy, while leaving
-- Restore/P/proj abstract for the concrete instance.
record SeverityGuardedStrict : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S : Set
    policy : SG.SeverityPolicy S

    U‚Çõ : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    P‚Çõ : S ‚Üí S
    Restore‚Çõ : S ‚Üí S

    P-strict-on‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy x ‚Üí SG.Guard policy y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P‚Çõ x y ‚Üí
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d U‚Çõ (P‚Çõ x) (P‚Çõ y) < UMetric.Ultrametric.d U‚Çõ x y

    restore-normal-form‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí SG.Broken policy x ‚Üí SG.Guard policy (Restore‚Çõ x)

    restore-idem‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore‚Çõ (Restore‚Çõ x) ‚â° Restore‚Çõ x

    restore-fixes‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P‚Çõ (Restore‚Çõ x) ‚â° Restore‚Çõ x

  toGuardedStrict : TG.GuardedStrictness
  toGuardedStrict =
    let p = policy in
    record
      { X = S
      ; U = U‚Çõ
      ; P = P‚Çõ
      ; Guard = SG.SeverityPolicy.Guard p
      ; Broken = SG.SeverityPolicy.Broken p
      ; Snap = SG.SeverityPolicy.Snap p
      ; Restore = Restore‚Çõ
      ; P-strict-on = Œª {x} {y} gx gy fd ‚Üí P-strict-on‚Çõ {x = x} {y = y} gx gy fd
      ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-form‚Çõ
      ; restore-idem = restore-idem‚Çõ
      ; restore-fixes = restore-fixes‚Çõ
      }

open SeverityGuardedStrict public

module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseMetricProof where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail collapse implies distance-to-neutral is zero

tailCollapse-distance0 :
  ‚àÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate k TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) ‚â° 0
tailCollapse-distance0 k t =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (Œª x ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine x (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailCollapse k t))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

tailCollapse-finiteTime :
  ‚àÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  Œ£ Nat (Œª N ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate N TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) ‚â° 0)
tailCollapse-finiteTime k t = (k , tailCollapse-distance0 k t)

tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}) x)) (replicate k zer) ‚â° 0
tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 m k x =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (Œª y ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine y (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

-- Guarded strictness interface for conditional projections using a Nat-valued metric.
record GuardedStrictnessFine : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    X : Set
    P : X ‚Üí X
    d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Nat

    Guard  : X ‚Üí Set
    Broken : X ‚Üí Set
    Snap   : X ‚Üí Set
    Restore : X ‚Üí X

    -- Flow regime: strict contraction in the Nat-valued ultrametric.
    P-strict-on :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      Guard x ‚Üí Guard y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P x y ‚Üí
      d (P x) (P y) < d x y

    -- Broken regime: restoration back into Guard.
    restore-normal-form :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Broken x ‚Üí Guard (Restore x)

    restore-idem :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore (Restore x) ‚â° Restore x

    restore-fixes :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (Restore x) ‚â° Restore x

policy·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))

-- Guarded strictness for P·µ£ under severity guard.
P-strict-on :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} {x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)} ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) x ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) y ‚Üí
  FC.FiberDistinct (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}) x y ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} y)
    <
    UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
P-strict-on {m} {k} {x} {y} _ _ fd =
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers.contractFiber (ROSS.strictP-fiber {m} {k}) fd

restore-normal-form'' :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  SG.Broken (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) x ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) (MR.restore·µ£ {m} {k} x)
restore-normal-form'' {m} {k} x _ rewrite MR.tailOf-restore {m} {k} x | MSI.countNZ-replicate-zer {k} =
  -- Guard is severity ‚â§ safeThreshold; for restored state severity is 0.
  z‚â§n

module DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans; subst‚ÇÇ)

open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; _++_; map)

open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal nontrivial canonicalization on a single Trit

canonTrit : Trit ‚Üí Trit
canonTrit neg = pos
canonTrit zer = zer
canonTrit pos = pos

canonVec : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n
canonVec = map canonTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization on the full state: act only on the coarse core

C·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
C·µ£ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) = canonVec c ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansiveness (constructive)

C·µ£-++ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  C·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚â° canonVec c ++ t
C·µ£-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

nonexpC·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C·µ£ {m} {k})
nonexpC·µ£ {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C·µ£ {m} {k} x) (C·µ£ {m} {k} y)
                       ‚â§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        p : x ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : C·µ£ {m} {k} x ‚â° canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        r = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí C·µ£ {m} {k} v) p)
                  (C·µ£-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k x))
        s : C·µ£ {m} {k} y ‚â° canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        s = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí C·µ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                  (C·µ£-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k y) (TCP.tailOf m k y))
        lhs : FAM.dNatFine (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                            (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
              ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        lhs = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚â§
                (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
                (TCP.tailOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k y)
                canonTrit
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (C·µ£ {m} {k} x) (C·µ£ {m} {k} y)
                ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                               (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        step1 =
          subst‚ÇÇ
            (Œª a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                                     (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y))
            (sym r) (sym s) lhs
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                             ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 =
          subst‚ÇÇ
            (Œª x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                   (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                                   ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
            (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.‚â§-reflexive step2)

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _‚äî_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

-- Minimal additive structure.
record Additive {‚Ñì} (S : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    _+_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    -_  : S ‚Üí S
    0s  : S


-- Bilinear form (abstract; choose ‚Ñö/‚Ñù in instances).
record Bilinear {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìr} (S : Set ‚Ñìs) (R : Set ‚Ñìr) : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìr)) where
  field
    ‚ü®_,_‚ü© : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí R
    symm  : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® x , y ‚ü© ‚â° ‚ü® y , x ‚ü©
    0r    : R


-- Quadratic energy from the bilinear form.
record Quadratic {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìr} (S : Set ‚Ñìs) (R : Set ‚Ñìr) : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìr)) where
  field
    Q     : S ‚Üí R

record AdditiveR {‚Ñìr} (R : Set ‚Ñìr) : Set (suc ‚Ñìr) where
  field
    _+r_ : R ‚Üí R ‚Üí R

record Projection {‚Ñì} (S : Set ‚Ñì) : Set (suc ‚Ñì) where
  field
    P    : S ‚Üí S
    idem : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚â° P x


-- Masked orthogonal split gate: G-self-adjoint projection + orthogonal split.
record MaskedOrthogonalSplit
  {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìr}
  {S : Set ‚Ñìs} {R : Set ‚Ñìr}
  (A : Additive S)
  (B : Bilinear S R)
  (QF : Quadratic S R)
  (AR : AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : Projection S)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìr)) where
  open Additive A using (_+_; -_; 0s)
  open Bilinear B using (‚ü®_,_‚ü©; symm; 0r)
  open Quadratic QF using (Q)
  open AdditiveR AR using (_+r_)
  open Projection Pr using (P; idem)

  -- Complement.
  Qc : S ‚Üí S
  Qc x = _+_ x (- (P x))

  field
    -- G-self-adjointness
    selfAdjoint : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® P x , y ‚ü© ‚â° ‚ü® x , P y ‚ü©

    -- Orthogonality of the split
    orthogonal : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí ‚ü® P x , Qc x ‚ü© ‚â° 0r

    -- Energy split
    split : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Q x ‚â° (Q (P x) +r Q (Qc x))

open MaskedOrthogonalSplit public

open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; subst; trans; cong; subst‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _‚â§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _++_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)

C : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
C {m} {k} = CM.C·µ£ {m} {k}

P : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
P {m} {k} = TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}

R : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
R {m} {k} = TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k}

nonexpC : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C {m} {k})
nonexpC {m} {k} = CM.nonexpC·µ£ {m} {k}

nonexpR : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k})
nonexpR {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                       ‚â§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x ‚â° cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚â° cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : R {m} {k} x ‚â° cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx
        r = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí R {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.R·µ£-++ m k cx tx)
        s : R {m} {k} y ‚â° cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty
        s = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí R {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.R·µ£-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty)
               ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚â§ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                 ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          subst‚ÇÇ
            (Œª a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = subst‚ÇÇ
          (Œª x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.‚â§-reflexive step2)

nonexpP : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
nonexpP {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
        ‚â§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x ‚â° cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚â° cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : P {m} {k} x ‚â° cx ++ TCP.projTail tx
        r = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí P {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.P·µ£-++ m k cx tx)
        s : P {m} {k} y ‚â° cy ++ TCP.projTail ty
        s = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí P {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.P·µ£-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.projTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.projTail ty)
               ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-projTail‚â§ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
                 ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          subst‚ÇÇ
            (Œª a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚â§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = subst‚ÇÇ
          (Œª x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚â° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚â§-trans step1 (NatP.‚â§-reflexive step2)

strictP-fiber :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
strictP-fiber {m} {k} =
  record
    { contractFiber = Œª {x} {y} fd ‚Üí
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (x‚â¢y; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y) ‚â° 0
          d0 = subst (Œª z ‚Üí d (P {m} {k} x) z ‚â° 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P {m} {k} x))
        in
        subst (Œª u ‚Üí u < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive x‚â¢y)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticCore where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Product using (proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic ‚Äúenergy‚Äù density per trit: squares of {-1,0,+1}
-- Encoded directly as Nat: 1 for ¬±, 0 for 0.

sqTrit : Trit ‚Üí Nat
sqTrit neg = 1
sqTrit zer = 0
sqTrit pos = 1

sumNat : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Nat m ‚Üí Nat
sumNat [] = 0
sumNat (x ‚à∑ xs) = x + sumNat xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic invariant on the core: sum of squares

Qcore : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Nat
Qcore c = sumNat (map sqTrit c)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization preserves squares pointwise

sq-canon : ‚àÄ t ‚Üí sqTrit (CM.canonTrit t) ‚â° sqTrit t
sq-canon neg = refl
sq-canon zer = refl
sq-canon pos = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Qcore invariance under canonVec

Qcore-canonVec : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí Qcore (CM.canonVec c) ‚â° Qcore c
Qcore-canonVec [] = refl
Qcore-canonVec (t ‚à∑ ts)
  rewrite sq-canon t
  = cong (Œª n ‚Üí sqTrit t + n) (Qcore-canonVec ts)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift Qcore to the full state via the coarse split

Qfull : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Nat
Qfull {m} {k} x = Qcore (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

Qfull-invariant-C·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  Qfull {m} {k} (CM.C·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° Qfull {m} {k} x
Qfull-invariant-C·µ£ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | p
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k (CM.canonVec (proj‚ÇÅ p)) (proj‚ÇÇ p)
        | TCP.split-++ m k (proj‚ÇÅ p) (proj‚ÇÇ p)
  = Qcore-canonVec (proj‚ÇÅ p)
module DASHI.Physics.BianchiEinsteinAssumptions where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)

-- Abstract ‚Äúdiscrete geometry‚Äù interface for the Einstein gate

record DiscreteManifoldLike (V : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where

    Metric    : Set
    Tensor2   : Set

-- Gate seams
------------------------------------------------------------------------

  open DiscreteManifoldLike M
  field
    R      : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar
    G      : Tensor2
    T      : Tensor2
    bianchi : Div G ‚â° zeroS
    symG    : Sym G
    lovelock-unique : ‚ä§

record EinsteinAxioms : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    EinsteinEquation :
      ‚àÄ {Dim : Nat} {V : Set} ‚Üí
      DiscreteManifoldLike V ‚Üí Set

EinsteinEquation :
  (A : EinsteinAxioms) ‚Üí
  ‚àÄ {Dim : Nat} {V : Set} ‚Üí
  DiscreteManifoldLike V ‚Üí Set
EinsteinEquation A {Dim} {V} = EinsteinAxioms.EinsteinEquation A {Dim} {V}

einsteinAxiomsDefault : EinsteinAxioms
einsteinAxiomsDefault =
  record
    { EinsteinEquation = Œª {Dim} {V} _ ‚Üí ‚ä§ }

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftWiringFine where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC

open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftInstanceFine as SGSI
open import DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuard as SG

-- Concrete wiring target for the shift carrier using dNatFine strictness.
record ShiftSeverityGuardWiringFine {m k : Nat} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    -- Severity policy for each state
    policy·µ£' : SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))

    -- Deterministic tail-kill projection and restoration
    P·µ£' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    Restore·µ£' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)

    -- FineAgreement distance on the carrier
    d·µ£' : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Nat

    -- Guarded strictness of P under severity guard
    P-strict-on' :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P·µ£' x y ‚Üí
      d·µ£' (P·µ£' x) (P·µ£' y) < d·µ£' x y

    restore-normal-form' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      SG.Broken policy·µ£' x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x)

    restore-idem' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x) ‚â° Restore·µ£' x

    restore-fixes' :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P·µ£' (Restore·µ£' x) ‚â° Restore·µ£' x

  shiftStrict : SGSI.ShiftSeverityGuardedStrictFine {m} {k}
  shiftStrict =
    record
      { pol = record
          { code·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.code policy·µ£'
          ; safeThreshold·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.safeThreshold policy·µ£'
          ; brokenThreshold·µ£ = SG.SeverityPolicy.brokenThreshold policy·µ£'
          }
      ; P·µ£ = P·µ£'
      ; Restore·µ£ = Restore·µ£'
      ; d·µ£ = d·µ£'
      ; P-strict-on = P-strict-on'
      ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-form'
      ; restore-idem = restore-idem'
      ; restore-fixes = restore-fixes'
      }

open ShiftSeverityGuardWiringFine public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplitShift where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _‚äî_) renaming (zero to lzero)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_; zero)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _‚à∏_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; +_) renaming (_‚â§_ to _‚â§·µ¢_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit as ADSplit
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI

private
  S : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Set
  S {m} {k} = RTC.Carrier (m + k)

  arrow : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí S {m} {k} ‚Üí Nat
  arrow {m} {k} x = MSI.countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

  splitS : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs = _} {‚Ñìa = _} {‚Ñìx = _}
  splitS {m} {k} = record
    { State = S {m} {k}
    ; Shape = S {m} {k}
    ; Arrow = Nat
    ; split = Œª x ‚Üí x , arrow {m} {k} x
    }

  Œ¥ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  Œ¥ {m} {k} = record
    { ŒîShape = Œª x' _ ‚Üí x'
    ; ŒîArrow = Œª a' a ‚Üí a ‚à∏ a'
    }

  forward : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  forward {m} {k} = record
    { Forward = Œª d ‚Üí zero ‚â§ d
    }

  cone : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) ‚Üí ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k}))
  cone {m} {k} œÉ = record
    { Cone = Œª s ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚â§·µ¢ IMQ.QœÉ œÉ s
    }

-- Concrete wiring to the shift step; split/forward/cone are fixed by ADS.
record ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {‚Ñìr : Level}
  {m k : Nat}
  (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
  (R : Set ‚Ñìr)
  (A : MOS.Additive (S {m} {k}))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (S {m} {k}) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (S {m} {k}) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (S {m} {k}))
  (SC : ADSplit.SplitCone (S {m} {k}))
  : Set (suc ‚Ñìr ‚äî suc lzero) where
  field
    coneSplitKit : ADSplit.ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
      (splitS {m} {k})
      R
      (Œ¥ {m} {k})
      (forward {m} {k})
      (cone {m} {k} œÉ)
      (Œª x y ‚Üí y ‚â° TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)
      A B QF AR Pr SC

open ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS

record SplitCone {‚Ñìs} (Shape : Set ‚Ñìs) : Set (suc ‚Ñìs) where
  field
    ConeP : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìs
    ConeQ : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìs

open SplitCone public

-- Bridge: forward steps ‚áí cone on Œîs, and cone on Œîs ‚áí cone on split parts.
record ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx ‚Ñìr}
  (Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx})
  (R : Set ‚Ñìr)
  (Œî : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split))
  (Step : ASD.State Split ‚Üí ASD.State Split ‚Üí Set)
  (A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split))
  (SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split))
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìa ‚äî ‚Ñìx ‚äî ‚Ñìr)) where
  field
    -- Base arrow-separated cone lemma.
    deltaCone : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone Split Œî Fwd Cone Step

    -- Orthogonal split gate for shape deltas.
    splitGate : MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit A B QF AR Pr

    -- If the full Œîs is in the cone, both split components are cone-compatible.
    coneSplit :
      ‚àÄ {x x'} ‚Üí
      ASD.ConeStep Split Œî Cone x x' ‚Üí
      let ds = ASD.ŒîShape Œî (proj‚ÇÅ (ASD.split Split x')) (proj‚ÇÅ (ASD.split Split x))
      in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) √ó
         (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc splitGate ds))

open ArrowSeparatedConeSplit public

-- Derived: forward step implies split cone predicates.
forwardConeSplit :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx ‚Ñìr}
  {Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx}}
  {R : Set ‚Ñìr}
  {Œî : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {Step : ASD.State Split ‚Üí ASD.State Split ‚Üí Set}
  {A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {AR : MOS.AdditiveR R}
  {Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split)}
  ‚Üí (kit : ArrowSeparatedConeSplit Split R Œî Fwd Cone Step A B QF AR Pr SC)
  ‚Üí ‚àÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ASD.ForwardStep Split Œî Fwd x x'
  ‚Üí let ds = ASD.ŒîShape Œî (proj‚ÇÅ (ASD.split Split x')) (proj‚ÇÅ (ASD.split Split x))
        sg = ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.splitGate kit
    in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) √ó
       (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc sg ds))
forwardConeSplit kit st fw =
  ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.coneSplit kit
    (ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone.forward‚áícone (ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.deltaCone kit) st fw)
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeShift where

    ; Shape = S {m} {k}

    ; split = Œª x ‚Üí x , arrow {m} {k} x

  Œ¥ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))

  forward : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))

  cone {m} {k} œÉ = record
    { Cone = Œª s ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚â§·µ¢ IMQ.QœÉ œÉ s
    }

record ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone {m k : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    step‚áíforward : ‚àÄ {x} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    forward‚áícone : ‚àÄ {x} ‚Üí
      ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Üí
      ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} œÉ) x (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)

  kit : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} œÉ) (Œª x y ‚Üí y ‚â° TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x)
  kit = record
    { step‚áíforward = stepForward
    ; forward‚áícone = coneForward
    }
    where
      stepForward :
        ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí y ‚â° TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x ‚Üí
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y
      stepForward {x} {y} eq rewrite eq = step‚áíforward {x}

      coneForward :
        ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí y ‚â° TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x ‚Üí
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y ‚Üí
        ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (Œ¥ {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} œÉ) x y
      coneForward {x} {y} eq fw rewrite eq = forward‚áícone {x} fw

open ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äî_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)

-- Abstract split of state into (shape, arrow)
record ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx : Level} : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìa ‚äî ‚Ñìx)) where
  field
    State : Set ‚Ñìx
    Shape : Set ‚Ñìs
    Arrow : Set ‚Ñìa
    split : State ‚Üí Shape √ó Arrow

open ArrowSplit public

-- Difference operations for shape and arrow components.
record ArrowDelta {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa : Level} (Shape : Set ‚Ñìs) (Arrow : Set ‚Ñìa)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìa)) where
  field
    ŒîShape : Shape ‚Üí Shape ‚Üí Shape
    ŒîArrow : Arrow ‚Üí Arrow ‚Üí Arrow

open ArrowDelta public

-- Forwardness predicate is only about arrow deltas.
record ForwardPred {‚Ñìa : Level} (Arrow : Set ‚Ñìa) : Set (suc ‚Ñìa) where
  field
    Forward : Arrow ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìa

open ForwardPred public

-- Cone screen only depends on shape deltas.
record ConeScreen {‚Ñìs : Level} (Shape : Set ‚Ñìs) : Set (suc ‚Ñìs) where
  field
    Cone : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìs

open ConeScreen public

-- Derived step predicates.
ForwardStep :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìa
ForwardStep S D F x x' =
  Forward F (ŒîArrow D (proj‚ÇÇ (split S x')) (proj‚ÇÇ (split S x)))

ConeStep :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set ‚Ñìs
ConeStep S D C x x' =
  Cone C (ŒîShape D (proj‚ÇÅ (split S x')) (proj‚ÇÅ (split S x)))

-- Keystone lemma: forward step implies cone screen on shape delta.
record ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone
  {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  (Step : State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set)
  : Set (suc (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìa ‚äî ‚Ñìx)) where
  field
    step‚áíforward : ‚àÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ForwardStep S D F x x'
    forward‚áícone : ‚àÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ForwardStep S D F x x' ‚Üí ConeStep S D C x x'

open ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public

-- Convenience: cone-compatibility predicate on steps.
ConeCompatibleStep :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set (‚Ñìs ‚äî ‚Ñìa)
ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x' = ForwardStep S D F x x' ‚Üí ConeStep S D C x x'

coneCompatibleFromKit :
  ‚àÄ {‚Ñìs ‚Ñìa ‚Ñìx}
  {S : ArrowSplit {‚Ñìs} {‚Ñìa} {‚Ñìx}}
  {D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S)}
  {F : ForwardPred (Arrow S)}
  {C : ConeScreen (Shape S)}
  {Step : State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set}
  ‚Üí ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone S D F C Step
  ‚Üí ‚àÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x'
coneCompatibleFromKit kit st fw = forward‚áícone kit st fw

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell predicate: |QœÉ(x)| = 1 (encoded as QœÉ = +1 or QœÉ = -1)

Shell1 : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
Shell1 œÉ x =
  (IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚â° (+ 1)) ‚äé (IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚â° -[1+ 0 ])

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureInstance where

open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy
open import Contraction
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

-- Bundle real (non-toy) closure data.
record RealClosureInstance : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    op  : TOperator S
    sc  : StrictContraction U (TOperator.T op)
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RealIsotropy U (TOperator.T op)
    fs  : RealFiniteSpeed (TOperator.T op)

-- Convert real closure instance into the common ClosureAxioms.
toClosureAxioms : RealClosureInstance ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
toClosureAxioms inst =
  record
    { S   = RealClosureInstance.S inst
    ; U   = RealClosureInstance.U inst
    ; T   = TOperator.T (RealClosureInstance.op inst)
    ; sc  = RealClosureInstance.sc inst
    ; inv = RealClosureInstance.inv inst
    ; iso = RealIsotropy.iso (RealClosureInstance.iso inst)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RealFiniteSpeed.local (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        ; preservesLocality = RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ShellOrbitProfileGenerator where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚à∑_; length)

open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Build a ShellOrbitProfile from a sorted (descending) list of orbit sizes.
-- This keeps the generator concrete while still allowing external data.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

profileFromSorted :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
profileFromSorted {m} sizes =
  record
    { orbitCount = length sizes
    ; top1 = top1Of sizes
    ; top2 = top2Of sizes
    ; top3 = top3Of sizes
    }
  where
    top1Of : List Nat ‚Üí Nat
    top1Of (a ‚à∑ _) = a
    top1Of [] = 0

    top2Of : List Nat ‚Üí Nat
    top2Of (_ ‚à∑ b ‚à∑ _) = b
    top2Of _ = 0

    top3Of : List Nat ‚Üí Nat
    top3Of (_ ‚à∑ _ ‚à∑ c ‚à∑ _) = c
    top3Of _ = 0
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; _++_; replicate)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (take; init; last; _‚à∑ ≥_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, nontrivial renormalization R·µ£ implementing a ‚Äúscale shift‚Äù
------------------------------------------------------------------------

split :
  ‚àÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí
  Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí (Vec A m √ó Vec A k)
split {A} zero    k xs       = ([] , xs)
split {A} (suc m) k (x ‚à∑ xs) with split {A} m k xs
... | (c , t) = (x ‚à∑ c , t)

split-++ :
  ‚àÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (c : Vec A m) (t : Vec A k) ‚Üí
  split m k (c ++ t) ‚â° (c , t)
split-++ zero k [] t = refl
split-++ (suc m) k (x ‚à∑ xs) t =
  cong (Œª p ‚Üí (x ‚à∑ proj‚ÇÅ p , proj‚ÇÇ p)) (split-++ m k xs t)

coarseOf : ‚àÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí Vec A m
coarseOf m k x = proj‚ÇÅ (split m k x)

tailOf : ‚àÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí Vec A k
tailOf m k x = proj‚ÇÇ (split m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail-band operators

shiftTail : ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
shiftTail {zero}    []       = []
shiftTail {suc k‚Ä≤}  (x ‚à∑ xs) = xs ‚à∑ ≥ zer

projTail : ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
projTail {zero}    []       = []
projTail {suc k‚Ä≤}  t        = (init t) ‚à∑ ≥ zer


tailStep : ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
tailStep t = projTail (shiftTail t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift tail-band operators to full state

R·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
R·µ£ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ shiftTail t

P·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
P·µ£ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ projTail t

R·µ£-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  R·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚â° c ++ shiftTail t
R·µ£-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl

P·µ£-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  P·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚â° c ++ projTail t
P·µ£-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl


T·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
T·µ£ {m} {k} x = P·µ£ {m} {k} (R·µ£ {m} {k} x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí A ‚Üí A
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x = iterate n f (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper lemmas for replicate

init-replicate :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí init (replicate (suc k) zer) ‚â° replicate k zer
init-replicate {zero} = refl
init-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (Œª t ‚Üí zer ‚à∑ t) (init-replicate {k})

snoc-replicate :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí (replicate k zer) ‚à∑ ≥ zer ‚â° replicate (suc k) zer
snoc-replicate {zero} = refl
snoc-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (Œª t ‚Üí zer ‚à∑ t) (snoc-replicate {k})

tailStep-forgets-last :
  ‚àÄ {k‚Ä≤ : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k‚Ä≤)) ‚Üí
  tailStep t ‚â° projTail (shiftTail t)
tailStep-forgets-last {k‚Ä≤} t = refl

projTail-replicate :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí projTail (replicate k zer) ‚â° replicate k zer
projTail-replicate {zero}    = refl
projTail-replicate {suc k‚Ä≤}  =
  trans
    (cong (_‚à∑ ≥ zer) (init-replicate {k‚Ä≤}))
    (snoc-replicate {k‚Ä≤})

shiftTail-replicate :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí shiftTail (replicate k zer) ‚â° replicate k zer
shiftTail-replicate {zero}   = refl
shiftTail-replicate {suc k‚Ä≤} =
  snoc-replicate {k‚Ä≤}

tailStep-replicate :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí tailStep (replicate k zer) ‚â° replicate k zer
tailStep-replicate {k} =
  trans (cong projTail (shiftTail-replicate {k}))
        (projTail-replicate {k})

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra Vec lemmas needed for constructive nilpotence
------------------------------------------------------------------------

pair-Œ∑ : ‚àÄ {A B : Set} (p : A √ó B) ‚Üí (proj‚ÇÅ p , proj‚ÇÇ p) ‚â° p
pair-Œ∑ (a , b) = refl

init-‚à∑ ≥ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} {n : Nat} (xs : Vec A n) (a : A) ‚Üí init (xs ‚à∑ ≥ a) ‚â° xs
init-‚à∑ ≥ {n = zero}    []       a = refl
init-‚à∑ ≥ {n = suc n} (x ‚à∑ xs) a rewrite init-‚à∑ ≥ xs a = refl

projTail-idem :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí projTail (projTail t) ‚â° projTail t
projTail-idem {zero} [] = refl
projTail-idem {suc k‚Ä≤} t =
  trans
    (cong (_‚à∑ ≥ zer) (init-‚à∑ ≥ (init t) zer))
    refl

P·µ£-idem :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  P·µ£ {m} {k} (P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° P·µ£ {m} {k} x
P·µ£-idem m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite P·µ£-++ m k c t
        | P·µ£-++ m k c (projTail t)
        | projTail-idem t
  = refl

tailStep‚â°shiftTail : ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí tailStep t ‚â° shiftTail t
tailStep‚â°shiftTail {zero}    [] = refl
tailStep‚â°shiftTail {suc k‚Ä≤} (x ‚à∑ xs)
  rewrite init-‚à∑ ≥ xs zer
  = refl

shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  shiftTail (xs ‚à∑ ≥ zer) ‚â° (shiftTail xs) ‚à∑ ≥ zer
shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer {zero} [] = refl
shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer {suc k} (x ‚à∑ xs) = refl

iterate-shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer :
  ‚àÄ {k : Nat} (n : Nat) (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate n shiftTail (xs ‚à∑ ≥ zer) ‚â° (iterate n shiftTail xs) ‚à∑ ≥ zer
iterate-shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer zero xs = refl
iterate-shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer (suc n) xs
  rewrite shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer xs
        | iterate-shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer n (shiftTail xs)
  = refl

iterate-pointwise :
  ‚àÄ {A : Set} (n : Nat) (f g : A ‚Üí A) (x : A) ‚Üí
  (‚àÄ y ‚Üí f y ‚â° g y) ‚Üí
  iterate n f x ‚â° iterate n g x
iterate-pointwise zero f g x fg = refl
iterate-pointwise (suc n) f g x fg
  rewrite fg x
  = iterate-pointwise n f g (g x) fg

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

tailCollapse-shiftTail :
  ‚àÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate k shiftTail t ‚â° replicate k zer
tailCollapse-shiftTail zero    []       = refl
tailCollapse-shiftTail (suc k) (x ‚à∑ xs) =
  trans
    (iterate-shiftTail-‚à∑ ≥-zer k xs)
    (trans
      (cong (_‚à∑ ≥ zer) (tailCollapse-shiftTail k xs))
      (snoc-replicate {k}))

tailCollapse :
  ‚àÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate k tailStep t ‚â° replicate k zer
tailCollapse k t =
  trans
    (iterate-pointwise k tailStep shiftTail t (Œª y ‚Üí tailStep‚â°shiftTail y))
    (tailCollapse-shiftTail k t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

merge-split :
  ‚àÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (x : Vec A (m + k)) ‚Üí
  (coarseOf m k x ++ tailOf m k x) ‚â° x
merge-split {A} zero    k x = refl
merge-split {A} (suc m) k (x ‚à∑ xs)
  rewrite merge-split {A} m k xs
  = refl

T·µ£-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  T·µ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚â° c ++ tailStep t
T·µ£-++ m k c t
  rewrite R·µ£-++ m k c t
        | P·µ£-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
  = refl

split-T·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  split m k (T·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° (coarseOf m k x , tailStep (tailOf m k x))
split-T·µ£ m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite R·µ£-++ m k c t
        | P·µ£-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
        | split-++ m k c (projTail (shiftTail t))
  = refl

split-iterate-T·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  split m k (iterate n (T·µ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚â°
    ( coarseOf m k x
    , iterate n tailStep (tailOf m k x)
    )
split-iterate-T·µ£ m k zero x
  = sym (pair-Œ∑ (split m k x))
split-iterate-T·µ£ m k (suc n) x
  rewrite split-iterate-T·µ£ m k n (T·µ£ {m} {k} x)
        | split-T·µ£ m k x
  = refl

tailOf-after-Tk :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  tailOf m k (iterate k (T·µ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚â° replicate k zer
tailOf-after-Tk m k x =
  trans
    (cong proj‚ÇÇ (split-iterate-T·µ£ m k k x))
    (tailCollapse k (tailOf m k x))
module DASHI.Physics.RealConeInteriorFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedConeStructure as MCS
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

-- Cone interior/boundary from a signature mask.
coneInteriorFromMask : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí UFTC.ConeInterior {X = Vec Trit m}
coneInteriorFromMask {m} œÉ =
  record
    { InInterior = MCS.Timelike œÉ
    ; Boundary = MCS.Null œÉ
    }
module DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; map)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv; inv-invol; zer)

Carrier : Nat ‚Üí Set
Carrier n = Vec Trit n

invVec : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Carrier n ‚Üí Carrier n
invVec {n} = map inv

invVec-invol : ‚àÄ {n} (x : Carrier n) ‚Üí invVec (invVec x) ‚â° x
invVec-invol [] = refl
invVec-invol (t ‚à∑ ts) rewrite inv-invol t | invVec-invol ts = refl

zeroVec : ‚àÄ {n} ‚Üí Carrier n
zeroVec {n = zero} = []
zeroVec {n = suc n} = zer ‚à∑ zeroVec {n}
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityMapping where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)

-- Clamp severity into 0..9 using min (‚äì).
clamp9 : Nat ‚Üí Nat
clamp9 n = n ‚äì 9

-- Severity mapping: use tail nonzero count as defect magnitude.
code·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Code
code·µ£ {m} {k} x with countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
... | zero    = normal 0
... | suc n   = special (clamp9 (suc n))

-- Policy thresholds (configurable).
safeThreshold·µ£ : Severity
safeThreshold·µ£ = 3

brokenThreshold·µ£ : Severity
brokenThreshold·µ£ = 4

module DASHI.Physics.DefaultClosure where

open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_; _<_; _‚äî_; z‚â§n; s‚â§s)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractive‚â¢; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureStatusFromGlue

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, total instance to close the physics glue
------------------------------------------------------------------------

_‚â¢_ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
x ‚â¢ y = x ‚â° y ‚Üí ‚ä•

Carrier : Set
Carrier = Bool

-- Discrete ultrametric on Bool: 0 if equal, 1 otherwise.
dBool : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Nat
dBool true  true  = zero
dBool false false = zero
dBool true  false = suc zero
dBool false true  = suc zero

id-zeroBool : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí dBool x x ‚â° 0
id-zeroBool true  = refl
id-zeroBool false = refl

symBool : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí dBool x y ‚â° dBool y x
symBool true  true  = refl
symBool false false = refl
symBool true  false = refl
symBool false true  = refl

ultratriangleBool : ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí dBool x z ‚â§ (dBool x y ‚äî dBool y z)
ultratriangleBool true  true  true  = z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool true  true  false = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool true  false true  = z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool true  false false = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool false true  true  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool false true  false = z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool false false true  = s‚â§s z‚â§n
ultratriangleBool false false false = z‚â§n

boolUltrametric : UMetric.Ultrametric Carrier
boolUltrametric =
  record
    { d = dBool
    ; id-zero = id-zeroBool
    ; symmetric = symBool
    ; ultratriangle = ultratriangleBool
    }

-- Constant contraction to false.
T : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
T _ = false

contractiveBool-proof : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí x ‚â¢ y ‚Üí dBool (T x) (T y) < dBool x y
contractiveBool-proof true  false _   = s‚â§s z‚â§n
contractiveBool-proof false true  _   = s‚â§s z‚â§n
contractiveBool-proof true  true  x‚â¢y = ‚ä•-elim (x‚â¢y refl)
contractiveBool-proof false false x‚â¢y = ‚ä•-elim (x‚â¢y refl)

contractiveBool : Contraction.Contractive‚â¢ boolUltrametric T
contractiveBool =
  record
    { contraction‚â¢ = Œª {x} {y} x‚â¢y ‚Üí
        contractiveBool-proof x y x‚â¢y
    }

boolTrueNeqFalse : false ‚â° true ‚Üí ‚ä•
boolTrueNeqFalse ()

uniqueBool : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí T x ‚â° x ‚Üí x ‚â° false
uniqueBool true  hx = ‚ä•-elim (boolTrueNeqFalse hx)
uniqueBool false _  = refl

strictBool : Contraction.StrictContraction boolUltrametric T
strictBool =
  record
    { contractive‚â¢ = contractiveBool
    ; fp = false
    ; fixed = refl
    ; unique = uniqueBool
    }

invBool : Involution Carrier
invBool = record
  { Œπ = Œª x ‚Üí x
  ; invol = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
  }

defaultClosure : Glue.ClosureAxioms
defaultClosure = Glue.mkDefaultClosure boolUltrametric T strictBool invBool

defaultClosureStatus : ClosureStatus
defaultClosureStatus = closureStatusFromGlue defaultClosure

-- Dimension-bound theorem seam (assumption module).
isotropyShellProfile :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat}
  (B : RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí Nat)
  (S : DBA.IndefiniteSignature B)
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
isotropyShellProfile {m} _ _ with m
... | zero = SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = zero} []
... | suc zero = SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = suc zero} []
... | suc (suc zero) = OPE.orbitProfile-m2
... | suc (suc (suc zero)) = OPE.orbitProfile-m3
... | suc (suc (suc (suc zero))) = OPE.orbitProfile-m4
... | suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) = OPE.orbitProfile-m5
... | suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero))))) = OPE.orbitProfile-m6
... | suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))))) = OPE.orbitProfile-m7
... | suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc (suc zero))))))) = OPE.orbitProfile-m8
... | m' = SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = m'} []

zero‚â¢three ()

two‚â¢three : 2 ‚â° 3 ‚Üí ‚ä•
two‚â¢three ()

eight‚â¢twentyfour ()

one68‚â¢twentyfour ()

  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount (SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = m} []) ‚â° 0

empty-contradiction :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount (SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = m} []) ‚â° 3 ‚Üí
  ‚ä•

empty-contradiction-iso :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat}
  (B : RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí Nat)
  (S : DBA.IndefiniteSignature B)
  ‚Üí isotropyShellProfile {m = m} B S ‚â° SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = m} []
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount (isotropyShellProfile {m = m} B S) ‚â° 3
  ‚Üí ‚ä•
empty-contradiction-iso {m} B S eq oc =
  empty-contradiction {m = m}
    (subst (Œª q ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount q ‚â° 3) eq oc)

OrbitProfile-24-6-2‚Üím‚â°4 :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat}
  (B : RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí RTC.Carrier m ‚Üí Nat)
  (S : DBA.IndefiniteSignature B)
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚â° 3
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top1       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚â° 24
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top2       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚â° 6
  ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top3       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚â° 2

module DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; cong‚ÇÇ)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic using (Sign; plus; minus)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count plus/minus in a mask and extract signature

countPlus : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat
countPlus [] = 0
countPlus (plus  ‚à∑ œÉ) = suc (countPlus œÉ)
countPlus (minus ‚à∑ œÉ) = countPlus œÉ

countMinus : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat
countMinus [] = 0
countMinus (plus  ‚à∑ œÉ) = countMinus œÉ
countMinus (minus ‚à∑ œÉ) = suc (countMinus œÉ)

signature : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat √ó Nat
signature œÉ = (countMinus œÉ , countPlus œÉ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete mask constructor: one minus, rest plus

replicatePlus : ‚àÄ (k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Sign k
replicatePlus zero    = []
replicatePlus (suc k) = plus ‚à∑ replicatePlus k

oneMinusRestPlus : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign (suc m)
oneMinusRestPlus {m} = minus ‚à∑ replicatePlus m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Signature of the concrete mask

countPlus-replicatePlus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí countPlus (replicatePlus m) ‚â° m
countPlus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countPlus-replicatePlus {suc m} =
  cong suc (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

countMinus-replicatePlus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí countMinus (replicatePlus m) ‚â° 0
countMinus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countMinus-replicatePlus {suc m} = countMinus-replicatePlus {m}

signature-oneMinus :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí signature (oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚â° (suc 0 , m)
signature-oneMinus {m} =
  cong‚ÇÇ _,_
    (cong suc (countMinus-replicatePlus {m}))
    (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Zero vectors

zeros : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n
zeros {n = zero}  = []
zeros {n = suc n} = zer ‚à∑ zeros {n = n}

embedCore : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCore {m} {k} c = c ++ zeros {n = k}

embedTail : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedTail {m} {k} t = zeros {n = m} ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotœÉ unfolds to a recursive definition

dotœÉ-cons :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (s : IMQ.Sign) (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m)
    (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit m)
    (y : Trit) (ys : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotœÉ (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys)
    ‚â° (IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s * (IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit x * IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit y)) +‚Ñ§ IMQ.dotœÉ œÉ xs ys
dotœÉ-cons s œÉ x xs y ys = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotœÉ against a zero vector is 0

dotœÉ-zero-left :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotœÉ œÉ (zeros {n = m}) y ‚â° 0‚Ñ§
dotœÉ-zero-left [] [] = refl
dotœÉ-zero-left (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  trans
    (dotœÉ-cons s œÉ zer (zeros {n = _}) y ys)
    (trans
    (cong (Œª z ‚Üí z +‚Ñ§ IMQ.dotœÉ œÉ (zeros {n = _}) ys)
            (trans
              (cong (Œª t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s * t) (IntP.*-zeroÀ° (IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit y)))
              (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s))))
      (cong (Œª z ‚Üí 0‚Ñ§ +‚Ñ§ z) (dotœÉ-zero-left œÉ ys)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Core and tail are orthogonal under dotœÉ

dotœÉ-core‚ä•tail :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotœÉ œÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) ‚â° 0‚Ñ§
dotœÉ-core‚ä•tail {zero} {k} œÉ [] t = dotœÉ-zero-left œÉ t
dotœÉ-core‚ä•tail {suc m} {k} (s ‚à∑ œÉ) (x ‚à∑ xs) t =
  trans
    (dotœÉ-cons s œÉ x (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) zer (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
    (trans
    (cong (Œª z ‚Üí z +‚Ñ§ IMQ.dotœÉ œÉ (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
            (trans
              (cong (Œª t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s * t) (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit x)))
              (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s))))
      (cong (Œª z ‚Üí 0‚Ñ§ +‚Ñ§ z) (dotœÉ-core‚ä•tail {m} {k} œÉ xs t)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Therefore B2œÉ is also 0 on core/tail blocks

B2œÉ-core‚ä•tail :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.B2œÉ œÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) ‚â° 0‚Ñ§

  trans (IMQ.B2œÉ‚â°2dotœÉ œÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t))

-- Guarded strictness bundle specialized to the shift carrier, but still abstract
-- in the projection and restore maps (to avoid baking in a specific scheduler).

      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policy·µ£ pol) x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policy·µ£ pol) y ‚Üí

      UMetric.Ultrametric.d U·µ£ (P·µ£ x) (P·µ£ y) < UMetric.Ultrametric.d U·µ£ x y

    restore-normal-form :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      SG.Broken (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policy·µ£ pol) x ‚Üí
      SG.Guard (ShiftSeverityPolicy.policy·µ£ pol) (Restore·µ£ x)

    restore-idem :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore·µ£ (Restore·µ£ x) ‚â° Restore·µ£ x

    restore-fixes :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P·µ£ (Restore·µ£ x) ‚â° Restore·µ£ x

  guarded : SGS.SeverityGuardedStrict
  guarded = record
    { S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)
    ; policy = ShiftSeverityPolicy.policy·µ£ pol
    ; U‚Çõ = U·µ£
    ; P‚Çõ = P·µ£
    ; Restore‚Çõ = Restore·µ£
    ; P-strict-on‚Çõ = P-strict-on
    ; restore-normal-form‚Çõ = restore-normal-form
    ; restore-idem‚Çõ = restore-idem
    ; restore-fixes‚Çõ = restore-fixes
    }

-- Additive structure on Vec ‚Ñ§ m

QÃÇcore-zeroVec : ‚àÄ {m} ‚Üí QP.QÃÇcore (QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}) ‚â° + 0

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Scalar parallelogram lemma on ‚Ñ§

sq : ‚Ñ§ ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
sq x = x * x

swap-sum : ‚àÄ a x b y ‚Üí (a + x) + (b + y) ‚â° (a + b) + (x + y)
swap-sum a x b y =
  Ring.solve 4
    (Œª a x b y ‚Üí
       ((a ‚äï x) ‚äï (b ‚äï y)) , ((a ‚äï b) ‚äï (x ‚äï y)))
    refl a x b y

parallelogram‚Ñ§ :
  ‚àÄ a b ‚Üí
    (sq (a + b) + sq (a - b)) ‚â° (sq a + sq a) + (sq b + sq b)
parallelogram‚Ñ§ a b =
  Ring.solve 2
    (Œª x y ‚Üí
       ( ((x ‚äï y) ‚äó (x ‚äï y)) ‚äï ((x ‚äï (‚äù y)) ‚äó (x ‚äï (‚äù y))) )
       , ( ((x ‚äó x) ‚äï (x ‚äó x)) ‚äï ((y ‚äó y) ‚äï (y ‚äó y)) ))
    refl a b

reassoc :
  ‚àÄ p q r s ‚Üí
    ((p + p) + (q + q)) + ((r + r) + (s + s))
      ‚â°
    ((p + r) + (p + r)) + ((q + s) + (q + s))
reassoc p q r s =
  Ring.solve 4
    (Œª p q r s ‚Üí
       ((p ‚äï p) ‚äï (q ‚äï q)) ‚äï ((r ‚äï r) ‚äï (s ‚äï s))
       , ((p ‚äï r) ‚äï (p ‚äï r)) ‚äï ((q ‚äï s) ‚äï (q ‚äï s)))
    refl p q r s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Parallelogram law for QP.QÃÇcore on Vec ‚Ñ§ m (by induction)

parallelogramQÃÇcore :
  ‚àÄ {m} (x y : Vec ‚Ñ§ m) ‚Üí
    QP.QÃÇcore (x +·µ• y) + QP.QÃÇcore (x +·µ• negVec y)
      ‚â°
    (QP.QÃÇcore x + QP.QÃÇcore x) + (QP.QÃÇcore y + QP.QÃÇcore y)
parallelogramQÃÇcore {zero} [] [] = refl
parallelogramQÃÇcore {suc m} (a ‚à∑ xs) (b ‚à∑ ys) =
  begin
    QP.QÃÇcore ((a ‚à∑ xs) +·µ• (b ‚à∑ ys)) + QP.QÃÇcore ((a ‚à∑ xs) +·µ• negVec (b ‚à∑ ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    ((a + b) * (a + b) + QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• ys))
      + ((a - b) * (a - b) + QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• negVec ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® swap-sum ((a + b) * (a + b)) (QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• ys))
                ((a - b) * (a - b)) (QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• negVec ys)) ‚ü©
    ((a + b) * (a + b) + (a - b) * (a - b))
      + (QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• ys) + QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• negVec ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí t + (QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• ys) + QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• negVec ys)))
        (parallelogram‚Ñ§ a b) ‚ü©
    ((a * a + a * a) + (b * b + b * b))
      + (QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• ys) + QP.QÃÇcore (xs +·µ• negVec ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® cong (Œª t ‚Üí ((a * a + a * a) + (b * b + b * b)) + t)
        (parallelogramQÃÇcore xs ys) ‚ü©
    ((a * a + a * a) + (b * b + b * b))
      + ((QP.QÃÇcore xs + QP.QÃÇcore xs) + (QP.QÃÇcore ys + QP.QÃÇcore ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® reassoc (a * a) (b * b) (QP.QÃÇcore xs) (QP.QÃÇcore ys) ‚ü©
    ((a * a + QP.QÃÇcore xs) + (a * a + QP.QÃÇcore xs))
      + ((b * b + QP.QÃÇcore ys) + (b * b + QP.QÃÇcore ys))
  ‚â°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QP.QÃÇcore (a ‚à∑ xs) + QP.QÃÇcore (a ‚à∑ xs)) + (QP.QÃÇcore (b ‚à∑ ys) + QP.QÃÇcore (b ‚à∑ ys))
  ‚àé

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projection/defect structure (trivial P, D) to satisfy emergence axioms

AdditiveVec‚Ñ§ : ‚àÄ {m} ‚Üí PD.Additive _
AdditiveVec‚Ñ§ {m} =
  record
    { Carrier = Vec ‚Ñ§ m
    ; _+_ = QP._+·µ•_
    ; 0# = QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}
    ; -_ = negVec
    }

PDzero : ‚àÄ {m} ‚Üí PD.ProjectionDefect (AdditiveVec‚Ñ§ {m})
PDzero {m} =
  record
    { P = Œª _ ‚Üí QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}
    ; D = Œª x ‚Üí x
    ; D-def = Œª x ‚Üí
        let
          step1 : x ‚â° QP._+·µ•_ x (negVec (QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}))
          step1 = trans (sym (add·µ•-zero ≥ x)) (cong (Œª t ‚Üí QP._+·µ•_ x t) (sym (negVec-zero {m})))
        in
        step1
    ; P-idem = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
    ; Orth = Œª x _ ‚Üí x ‚â° QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m}
    ; Orth-PD = Œª _ ‚Üí refl
    }

QuadraticEmergenceShiftAxioms :

          QP.QÃÇcore (QP.zeroVec‚Ñ§ {m} +·µ• y)

module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardShiftConcreteFine where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)

-- Concrete severity policy for shift carrier.
policy·µ£ : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SG.SeverityPolicy (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
policy·µ£ {m} {k} = record
  { code = SM.code·µ£ {m} {k}
  ; safeThreshold = SM.safeThreshold·µ£
  ; brokenThreshold = SM.brokenThreshold·µ£
  }

-- Strictness in dNatFine: if two states are distinct but in the same fiber, P·µ£ is strictly contractive.
P-strict-on :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} {x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)} ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) x ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) y ‚Üí
  FC.FiberDistinct (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}) x y ‚Üí
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} y) < FAM.dNatFine x y
P-strict-on {m} {k} _ _ fd =
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers.contractFiber (ROSS.strictP-fiber {m} {k}) fd

restore-normal-form'' :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  SG.Broken (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) x ‚Üí
  SG.Guard (policy·µ£ {m} {k}) (MR.restore·µ£ {m} {k} x)
restore-normal-form'' {m} {k} x _ rewrite MR.tailOf-restore {m} {k} x | MSI.countNZ-replicate-zer {k} =
  z‚â§n

-- Concrete wiring bundle using FineAgreement strictness.
shiftWiringFine : ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí W.ShiftSeverityGuardWiringFine {m} {k}
shiftWiringFine {m} {k} = record
  { policy·µ£' = policy·µ£ {m} {k}
  ; P·µ£' = TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k}
  ; Restore·µ£' = MR.restore·µ£ {m} {k}
  ; d·µ£' = FAM.dNatFine
  ; P-strict-on' = P-strict-on {m} {k}
  ; restore-normal-form' = restore-normal-form'' {m} {k}
  ; restore-idem' = MR.restore-idem {m} {k}
  ; restore-fixes' = MR.restore-fixes {m} {k}
  }
module DASHI.Physics.SeverityGuardedStrictFine where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
