open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseGuardedStrictFine as TG

-- Adapter: build Guard/Broken/Snap from a SeverityPolicy, while leaving
-- Restore/P/d abstract for the concrete instance.
record SeverityGuardedStrictFine : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    S : Set
    policy : SG.SeverityPolicy S

    P‚Çõ : S ‚Üí S
    Restore‚Çõ : S ‚Üí S
    d‚Çõ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Nat

    P-strict-on‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ {x y} ‚Üí
      SG.Guard policy x ‚Üí SG.Guard policy y ‚Üí
      FC.FiberDistinct P‚Çõ x y ‚Üí
      d‚Çõ (P‚Çõ x) (P‚Çõ y) < d‚Çõ x y

    restore-normal-form‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí SG.Broken policy x ‚Üí SG.Guard policy (Restore‚Çõ x)

    restore-idem‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí Restore‚Çõ (Restore‚Çõ x) ‚â° Restore‚Çõ x

    restore-fixes‚Çõ :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí P‚Çõ (Restore‚Çõ x) ‚â° Restore‚Çõ x

  toGuardedStrict : TG.GuardedStrictnessFine
  toGuardedStrict =
    let p = policy in
    record
      { X = S
      ; P = P‚Çõ
      ; d = d‚Çõ
      ; Guard = SG.SeverityPolicy.Guard p
      ; Broken = SG.SeverityPolicy.Broken p
      ; Snap = SG.SeverityPolicy.Snap p
      ; Restore = Restore‚Çõ
      ; P-strict-on = Œª {x} {y} gx gy fd ‚Üí P-strict-on‚Çõ {x = x} {y = y} gx gy fd
      ; restore-normal-form = restore-normal-form‚Çõ
      ; restore-idem = restore-idem‚Çõ
      ; restore-fixes = restore-fixes‚Çõ
      }

open SeverityGuardedStrictFine public

-- A concrete, minimal constraint system with a single constraint.

  record
    { Constraint = ‚ä§
    ; actsOn = Œª S ‚Üí S
    ; apply = Œª {S} _ x ‚Üí x
    }

  record
    { _[_,]_ = Œª _ _ ‚Üí tt
    ; antisym = ‚ä§
    ; jacobi = ‚ä§
    }

  record
    { closes = Œª _ _ ‚Üí (tt , refl)
    }

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticRenormalization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+‚Ñ§_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic split lemmas for coarse/tail under concatenation

coarseOf-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (c ++ t) ‚â° c
coarseOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

tailOf-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (c ++ t) ‚â° t
tailOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Coarse/tail behavior under renormalization R·µ£

coarseOf-R·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-R·µ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-R·µ£ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-R·µ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

R·µ£-decomp :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x ‚â° TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
R·µ£-decomp m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic under renormalization:
-- QœÉ(R·µ£ x) splits into coarse + shifted tail.

QœÉ-split-++ :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat)
    (œÉc : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (œÉt : Vec IMQ.Sign k)
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ (œÉc ++ œÉt) (c ++ t)
    ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ œÉc c +‚Ñ§ IMQ.QœÉ œÉt t
QœÉ-split-++ m k œÉc œÉt c t =
  let
    f = (Œª s xi ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ñ§ s * IMQ.sq‚Ñ§ (IMQ.to‚Ñ§Trit xi))
  in
  trans
    refl
    (trans
      (cong IMQ.sum‚Ñ§ (MSQ.zipWith-++ f œÉc œÉt c t))
      (trans
        (MSQ.sum‚Ñ§-++ (zipWith f œÉc c) (zipWith f œÉt t))
        refl))

QœÉ-split-coarse :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat)
    (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ œÉ (c ++ t)
    ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k œÉ) c
    +‚Ñ§ IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.tailOf m k œÉ) t
QœÉ-split-coarse m k œÉ c t
  =
  trans
    (cong (Œª z ‚Üí IMQ.QœÉ z (c ++ t)) (sym (TCP.merge-split {A = IMQ.Sign} m k œÉ)))
    (QœÉ-split-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k œÉ) (TCP.tailOf m k œÉ) c t)

QœÉ-R :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat)
    (œÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QœÉ œÉ (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x)
    ‚â° IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k œÉ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +‚Ñ§ IMQ.QœÉ (TCP.tailOf   m k œÉ) (TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x))
QœÉ-R m k œÉ x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c t
  = QœÉ-split-coarse m k œÉ c (TCP.shiftTail t)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ñ§)

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic invariants wired onto a RealClosureKitFiber instance.
--
-- This does not change the underlying closure kit; it augments it with:
--   - a mask on the core,
--   - the masked quadratic QœÉ and bilinear B‚ÇÇœÉ pulled back to the full state,
--   - a signature extracted from the mask,
--   - an orbit-profile seam (dimension bound target).

record RealClosureKitFiberMask : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    m k : Nat
    base : RKF.RealClosureKitFiber

    -- Mask on the core (length m).
    mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m

    -- Core-only invariants, lifted to the full state via coarseOf.
    coreQœÉ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí ‚Ñ§
    coreB2œÉ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí ‚Ñ§

    -- Signature extracted from the mask.
    sig : Nat √ó Nat

    -- Orbit-profile seam (dimension-bound target).
    orbitProfile : DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m

open RealClosureKitFiberMask public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constructor: derive all fields from base + mask.

mkMaskKit :
  ‚àÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RKF.RealClosureKitFiber ‚Üí
  Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m ‚Üí
  RealClosureKitFiberMask
mkMaskKit {m} {k} base mask orbitProfile =
  record
    { m = m
    ; k = k
    ; base = base
    ; mask = mask
    ; coreQœÉ = Œª x ‚Üí IMQ.QœÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; coreB2œÉ = Œª x y ‚Üí IMQ.B2œÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
    ; sig = SFM.signature mask
    ; orbitProfile = orbitProfile
    }
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputed where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; cong)
open import Relation.Nullary using (Dec; yes; no)

open import Data.List.Base using (List; []; _‚à∑_; map; filter·µá; length)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (_‚â§?_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_; head; tail)
open import Data.Integer.Base using (‚Ñ§; +_; -1‚Ñ§)
open import Data.Integer using (_‚âü_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic list utilities (kept local to avoid extra imports)

concat : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List (List A) ‚Üí List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs ‚à∑ xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x ‚à∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚à∑ (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : ‚àÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí List B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Trit and Vec

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (Œª ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (Œª eq ‚Üí neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (Œª eq ‚Üí neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Membership / nub

member : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí ((x y : A) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)) ‚Üí A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y ‚à∑ ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí ((x y : A) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x ‚à∑ xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x ‚à∑ nub dec xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg ‚à∑ zer ‚à∑ pos ‚à∑ []

allVecTrit : ‚àÄ (n : Nat) ‚Üí List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] ‚à∑ []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (Œª t ‚Üí map (Œª v ‚Üí t ‚à∑ v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell1 list from a mask

isShell1 : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Bool
isShell1 œÉ x with IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚âü (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QœÉ œÉ x ‚âü -1‚Ñ§
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} œÉ = filter·µá (isShell1 œÉ) (allVecTrit m)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orbit sizes under a finite action list

orbitSizes :
  ‚àÄ {A X : Set} ‚Üí
  (dec : (x y : X) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚â° y)) ‚Üí
  (gs : List A) ‚Üí
  (act : A ‚Üí X ‚Üí X) ‚Üí
  List X ‚Üí
  List Nat
{-# TERMINATING #-}
orbitSizes dec gs act [] = []
orbitSizes dec gs act (x ‚à∑ xs) =
  let
    orb = nub dec (map (Œª g ‚Üí act g x) gs)
    rest = filter·µá (Œª z ‚Üí not (member dec z orb)) xs
  in
  length orb ‚à∑ orbitSizes dec gs act rest
  where
    not : Bool ‚Üí Bool
    not true = false
    not false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Simple descending sort for Nat lists

insertDesc : Nat ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x ‚à∑ []
insertDesc x (y ‚à∑ ys) with x NatP.‚â§? y
... | yes _ = y ‚à∑ insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x ‚à∑ y ‚à∑ ys

sortDesc : List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x ‚à∑ xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Concrete Bool action: invVec toggle

actBool : ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m
actBool true  x = RTC.invVec x
actBool false x = x

bools : List Bool
bools = false ‚à∑ true ‚à∑ []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile for the Bool action on Shell1

orbitProfileBool :
  ‚àÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí
  Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
orbitProfileBool œÉ =
  let
    shell = shell1List œÉ
    sizes = orbitSizes decEqVec bools actBool shell
    sizesSorted = sortDesc sizes
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = _} sizesSorted
module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignature where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚â§_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_)
open import Data.Sum using (_‚äé_)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ P = P ‚Üí ‚ä•

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

-- Count coordinates that snap from nonzero to zero in a single step.
countZeroSnaps : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
countZeroSnaps [] [] = zero
countZeroSnaps (x ‚à∑ xs) (y ‚à∑ ys) =
  snap x y + countZeroSnaps xs ys
  where
    snap : Trit ‚Üí Trit ‚Üí Nat
    snap neg zer = suc zero
    snap pos zer = suc zero
    snap _   _   = zero

-- Predicate: at least k zero-snaps.
SnapAtLeast : ‚àÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Set
SnapAtLeast k x y = k ‚â§ countZeroSnaps x y

-- Abstract diagnostic bundle for a step x -> y.
record SnapSignature {S : Set} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    -- concrete state
    step : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 1: multi-coordinate zeroing (sheet elimination)
    snapZero : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 2: chi2 spike (boundary blow-up)
    chi2Spike : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 3: MDL proxy descent (valid IR movement)
    mdlDescent : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

-- Canonical combined predicate for a snap event.
record IsSnap {S : Set} (Sig : SnapSignature {S}) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    snap : ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.step Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x y ‚Üí
      Set

-- Cone monotonicity except snaps: if not a snap, interior is preserved.
record ConeMonotoneExceptSnaps {S : Set} : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    InInterior : S ‚Üí Set
    Boundary   : S ‚Üí Set
    T          : S ‚Üí S
    Sig        : SnapSignature {S}

    monotoneExceptSnap : ‚àÄ x ‚Üí
      InInterior x ‚Üí
      (¬¨ (SnapSignature.step Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x (T x))) ‚Üí
      InInterior (T x) ‚äé Boundary (T x)

module DASHI.Physics.ContractionQuadraticBridge where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_)

-- Abstract quadratic output forced by contraction.
record QuadraticOutput : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    V : Set
    Scalar : Set
    B : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Scalar
    Q : V ‚Üí Scalar
    Q-def : ‚àÄ v ‚Üí Q v ‚â° B v v
    Lyapunov : Set
    UniqueUpToScale : Set

open QuadraticOutput public

-- Bridge: strict contraction implies a quadratic output.
record Contraction‚áíQuadratic
  {S : Set}
  (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  (T : S ‚Üí S)
  : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    sc : StrictContraction U T
    out : QuadraticOutput

module DASHI.Physics.LiftToFullState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; replicate)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Invariant coarse subspace

embedCoarse : ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCoarse m k c = c ++ replicate k zer

coarseProj : ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit m
coarseProj m k x = TCP.coarseOf m k x

coarse-invariant-R :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.P·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x) ‚â° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.R·µ£ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time collapse + invariant geometry, packaged

coarse-invariant-iter :
  ‚àÄ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate n (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚â° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-iter m k zero x = refl
coarse-invariant-iter m k (suc n) x =
  trans
    (coarse-invariant-iter m k n (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} x))
    (coarse-invariant-T m k x)

finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  ( coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚â° coarseProj m k x )
  √ó
  ( TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚â° replicate k zer )
finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry m k x =
  ( coarse-invariant-iter m k k x
  , TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x
  )

invariantCoarseSubspace :
  ‚àÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  TCP.T·µ£ {m} {k} (embedCoarse m k c) ‚â° embedCoarse m k c
invariantCoarseSubspace m k c
  rewrite TCP.R·µ£-++ m k c (replicate k zer)
        | TCP.P·µ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (replicate k zer))
        | TCP.shiftTail-replicate {k}
        | TCP.projTail-replicate {k}
  = refl

module DASHI.Examples.ConcreteInstances where

-- Minimal concrete witnesses for the parameterised bridge records.
-- These are toy models: finite/constant structures that satisfy the
-- required equalities without using postulates or metas.

module MaassRestoration where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract broken states / restored states.
postulate
  Broken  : Set
  Stable  : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "restoration" map (Tikkun): Broken ‚Üí Stable

record Restoration : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    restore : Broken ‚Üí Stable

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Stability contracts you can actually test:
-- idempotence (restoring twice has no further effect) and coherence
-- with a projection/normal form.

record NormalForm : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    nf : Stable ‚Üí Stable
    nf-idem : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí nf (nf s) ‚â° nf s

record RestorationLaw : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    R  : Restoration
    NF : NormalForm
    restores-to-nf : ‚àÄ b ‚Üí NormalForm.nf NF (Restoration.restore R b) ‚â° Restoration.restore R b

-- Monotonicity property

record Monotone {X : Set}
                (K : State X ‚Üí State X)
                (A : State X ‚Üí Nat)
                : Set where

  field
    monotone :
      ‚àÄ s ‚Üí A (K s) ‚â§ A s
module FixedPoint where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point definition

Fixed : {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set
Fixed K x = K x ‚â° x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Uniqueness of fixed point under contraction

record UniqueFixed
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       (C : Contractive U K)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  open Contractive C

  field
    unique :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí
      Fixed K x ‚Üí
      Fixed K y ‚Üí
      x ‚â° y
module Verification.Prelude where

open import Data.Nat public
  renaming (‚Ñï to Nat)
open import Data.Bool public using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List public using (List; []; _‚à∑_)
open import Data.Product public using (Œ£; _,_; _√ó_; proj‚ÇÅ; proj‚ÇÇ)
open import Data.Empty public using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Data.Unit public using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality public using (_‚â°_; refl; cong; sym; trans)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

fst : {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} ‚Üí Œ£ A B ‚Üí A
fst = proj‚ÇÅ

snd : {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} (p : Œ£ A B) ‚Üí B (proj‚ÇÅ p)
snd = proj‚ÇÇ
module Verification.ZK where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Public  : Set
postulate Private : Set
postulate Output  : Set

-- The spec function (what correctness means)
postulate spec : Public -> Private -> Output

-- An implementation whose correctness you want to prove (could be a circuit)
postulate impl : Public -> Private -> Output

-- A proof object (SNARK) and a verifier predicate
postulate Proof : Set
postulate verify : Public -> Output -> Proof -> Bool

-- Soundness contract (non-ZK): if verifier accepts, output equals spec
-- (This is where you plug the cryptographic theorem/certificate.)
postulate
  zkSoundness :
    (pub : Public) -> (priv : Private) -> (out : Output) -> (pi : Proof) ->
    verify pub out pi ‚â° true ->
    out ‚â° spec pub priv

-- ZK verification artifact: provide pub/out/proof and a verification boolean proof.
record ZKCorrectness : Set1 where
  field
    pub  : Public
    priv : Private
    out  : Output
    pi   : Proof
    accepts : verify pub out pi ‚â° true
    correct : out ‚â° spec pub priv
module Verification.ExecutionReview where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- A tiny abstract control-flow model.
postulate Program : Set
postulate Path    : Set

-- Static analyzer produces a set/list of feasible paths
postulate enumeratePaths : Program ‚Üí List Path

-- A property you claim holds on all paths.
postulate SafeOnPath : Program ‚Üí Path ‚Üí Set

-- ‚ÄúExecution review‚Äù = proof that for every enumerated path, Safe holds.
All : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí Set) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Set
All P []       = ‚ä§
All P (x ‚à∑ xs) = P x √ó All P xs

record ExecutionReview : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    P   : Program
    ok  : All (SafeOnPath P) (enumeratePaths P)
module Verification.SourceHash where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- Abstract bytes; you can refine to Word8 later.
postulate Byte : Set
Bytes = List Byte

-- Cryptographic hash as a function (model-level).
postulate Hash : Set
postulate hash : Bytes ‚Üí Hash

-- A repo snapshot is modeled as its bytes (tarball) + declared hash.
record Snapshot : Set where
  constructor snap
  field
    blob     : Bytes
    declared : Hash

-- Integrity proof obligation: declared equals computed.
record SourceIntegrity : Set where
  field
    S : Snapshot
    ok : Snapshot.declared S ‚â° hash (Snapshot.blob S)
module Verification.BinaryPatching where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Binary : Set
postulate Input  : Set
postulate Output : Set

-- Semantics of a binary as a function (idealization).
postulate run : Binary ‚Üí Input ‚Üí Output

-- Vulnerability predicate (e.g., triggers UAF, OOB, etc.)
postulate Vuln : Binary ‚Üí Set

-- Patch procedure
postulate patch : Binary ‚Üí Binary

postulate SafeInput : Input ‚Üí Set

-- Correctness obligations
record PatchCorrect : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    B : Binary
    -- vulnerability removed
    fixed : ¬¨ Vuln (patch B)
    -- behavior preserved on some agreed safe domain
    preserved : ‚àÄ i ‚Üí SafeInput i ‚Üí run (patch B) i ‚â° run B i

module Ultrametric where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _‚â§_; _<_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï; _‚äî_)
max : ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï
max = _‚äî_


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance function into ‚Ñï (discrete ultrametric)

record Ultrametric (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    d : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Nat

    -- Identity
    id-zero :
      ‚àÄ x ‚Üí d x x ‚â° 0

    -- Symmetry
    symmetric :
      ‚àÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚â° d y x

    -- Strong triangle inequality (ultrametric)
    ultratriangle :
      ‚àÄ x y z ‚Üí
      d x z ‚â§ max (d x y) (d y z)

module CRTPeriod where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Nat.Base   using (NonZero; nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_; [m+kn]%n‚â°m%n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (*-assoc; *-comm; +-assoc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Repo-defined digit function:

d : Nat ‚Üí Nat
d N = ((N % 71) + (N % 59) + (N % 47)) % 10

period : Nat
period = 71 * 59 * 47  -- 196883

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The theorem statement (R1):
-- d(N + k*period) = d(N) for all k.
--
-- Proof is standard modular arithmetic:
-- (N + k*period) mod p = N mod p for p ‚àà {71,59,47}
-- then propagate through sum and mod 10.
--
-- You can discharge this using stdlib DivMod lemmas, or (DASHI-style)
-- by importing a small proof certificate.

instance
  nonZero71 : NonZero 71
  nonZero71 = nonZero
  nonZero59 : NonZero 59
  nonZero59 = nonZero
  nonZero47 : NonZero 47
  nonZero47 = nonZero
  nonZero10 : NonZero 10
  nonZero10 = nonZero

period-thm : ‚àÄ N k ‚Üí d (N + k * period) ‚â° d N
period-thm N k =
  period-thm' step71 step59 step47
  where
    k71 = k * (59 * 47)
    k59 = k * (71 * 47)
    k47 = k * (71 * 59)

    period‚â°59¬∑47¬∑71 : period ‚â° (59 * 47) * 71
    period‚â°59¬∑47¬∑71 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (NatP.*-comm 71 (59 * 47))

    period‚â°71¬∑47¬∑59 : period ‚â° (71 * 47) * 59
    period‚â°71¬∑47¬∑59 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (trans (cong (Œª x ‚Üí 71 * x) (NatP.*-comm 59 47))
          (sym (NatP.*-assoc 71 47 59)))

    period‚â°71¬∑59¬∑47 : period ‚â° (71 * 59) * 47
    period‚â°71¬∑59¬∑47 = NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47

    eq71 : k * period ‚â° k71 * 71
    eq71 = trans (cong (Œª x ‚Üí k * x) period‚â°59¬∑47¬∑71) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (59 * 47) 71))

    eq59 : k * period ‚â° k59 * 59
    eq59 = trans (cong (Œª x ‚Üí k * x) period‚â°71¬∑47¬∑59) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 47) 59))

    eq47 : k * period ‚â° k47 * 47
    eq47 = trans (cong (Œª x ‚Üí k * x) period‚â°71¬∑59¬∑47) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 59) 47))

    step71 : (N + k * period) % 71 ‚â° N % 71
    step71 = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí (N + v) % 71) eq71) ([m+kn]%n‚â°m%n N k71 71)

    step59 : (N + k * period) % 59 ‚â° N % 59
    step59 = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí (N + v) % 59) eq59) ([m+kn]%n‚â°m%n N k59 59)

    step47 : (N + k * period) % 47 ‚â° N % 47
    step47 = trans (cong (Œª v ‚Üí (N + v) % 47) eq47) ([m+kn]%n‚â°m%n N k47 47)

    period-thm' :
      (s71 : (N + k * period) % 71 ‚â° N % 71) ‚Üí
      (s59 : (N + k * period) % 59 ‚â° N % 59) ‚Üí
      (s47 : (N + k * period) % 47 ‚â° N % 47) ‚Üí
      d (N + k * period) ‚â° d N
    period-thm' s71 s59 s47 rewrite s71 | s59 | s47 = refl
module Z6_RegularInverse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin; zero; suc; to‚Ñï)
open import Data.Product.Base using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Z6 elements as Fin 6
Z6 : Set
Z6 = Fin 6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ring operations modulo 6 (postulate or implement via Fin arithmetic).
-- If you want full concreteness, implement add/mul with to‚Ñï and mod 6.
postulate
  _+6_ : Z6 ‚Üí Z6 ‚Üí Z6
  _*6_ : Z6 ‚Üí Z6 ‚Üí Z6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- von Neumann regular inverse witness: a = a*b*a

Regular : Z6 ‚Üí Set
Regular a = Œ£ Z6 (Œª b ‚Üí a ‚â° (a *6 b) *6 a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete witness table (finite, so we can just provide b per a).
-- You can later refine _+6_/_*6_ and this becomes fully checkable.

postulate
  bOf : Z6 ‚Üí Z6
  regular-law : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí a ‚â° (a *6 bOf a) *6 a

regular : ‚àÄ a ‚Üí Regular a
regular a = bOf a , regular-law a
module FascisticSystem where

open import Data.Product using (Œ£; _,_)
open import Data.Sum using (_‚äé_; inj‚ÇÅ; inj‚ÇÇ)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_)

open import Data.Nat as Nat
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)



-- Abstract finite state space

postulate
  S : Set
  finiteS : ‚Ñï          -- cardinality (not constructively used)

-- Entropy function (measure into ‚Ñï for simplicity)

postulate
  H : S ‚Üí ‚Ñï

-- Projection operator (idempotent, non-invertible)

record Projection : Set where
  field
    K        : S ‚Üí S
    idemp    : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí K (K s) ‚â° K s
    contract : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí H (K s) ‚â§ H s

-- System = list of projections applied in fixed order

postulate
  Ktotal : S ‚Üí S

-- Global contraction property

postulate
  monotone : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí H (Ktotal s) ‚â§ H s

-- Strict decrease when not in fixed set

postulate
  strict-decrease :
    ‚àÄ s ‚Üí H (Ktotal s) < H s ‚äé (Ktotal s ‚â° s)

-- Define attractor

Attractor : Set
Attractor = Œ£ S (Œª s ‚Üí Ktotal s ‚â° s)

-- Iteration

iterate : ‚Ñï ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate zero    s = s
iterate (suc n) s = Ktotal (iterate n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ‚ÄúAxiom of completion‚Äù as a termination measure contract:
-- Completion prime provides a stop condition for any recursive refinement loop.

record CompletionLaw (S : Set) : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    measure : S ‚Üí Nat
    step    : S ‚Üí S
    -- If step decreases measure, recursion terminates.
    decreases : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí measure (step s) < measure s
module ThreeAdic_Attractor where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚â°_; refl)
open import Data.Rational using (‚Ñö; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; normalize)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as ‚ÑöP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (trans; sym; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Define x by the equation 3x = x - 1, and solve in ‚Ñö.
-- This is the algebraic ‚Äúdigit-shift‚Äù property you care about.

postulate
  x : ‚Ñö

-- Helpers (stdlib has numerals; we keep explicit)
postulate
  1‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
  2‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
  3‚Ñö : ‚Ñö
  minusHalfQ : ‚Ñö

postulate
  shift : (3‚Ñö * x) ‚â° (x - 1‚Ñö)
  qed : x ‚â° minusHalfQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: if 3x = x - 1 then x = -1/2

solve : shift ‚â° shift ‚Üí x ‚â° minusHalfQ
solve _ =
  -- You can fill this using ‚Ñö ring reasoning:
  -- 3x = x - 1  ‚áí  2x = -1  ‚áí x = -1/2
  -- In Agda, easiest is to use ‚ÑöP.*-cancel ≥ / group properties.
  qed
module MonsterState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Factor mask (15 prime-power factors of |M|).
-- true  = keep
-- false = remove

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b ‚à∑ replicate n b

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Walk state.
-- You can extend this with ‚Äúwindow position‚Äù, ‚Äútarget digits‚Äù, etc.
-- For DASHI: kernel is about how masks evolve; lens decides admissibility.

record State : Set where
  constructor st
  field
    mask   : Mask
    window : Nat   -- abstract ‚Äúdigit window id‚Äù (moving window, index, etc.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A lens is the measurement predicate:
-- admissible s m = ‚Äúremoving to mask m preserves the digit window condition‚Äù.

record Lens : Set‚ÇÅ where
  field
    admissible : State ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Candidate moves:
-- In the real system, this is ‚Äúremove subsets of prime-power factors‚Äù.
-- Here we just take a finite list of candidate masks.

Candidates : Set
Candidates = List Mask
module LogicTlurey where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local equality utilities (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

sym : ‚àÄ {A : Set} {x y : A} ‚Üí x ‚â° y ‚Üí y ‚â° x
sym refl = refl

cong : ‚àÄ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí x ‚â° y ‚Üí f x ‚â° f y
cong f refl = refl

open import Base369

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dialectical stages
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Stage : Set where
  seed      : Stage
  counter   : Stage
  resonance : Stage
  overflow  : Stage

next : Stage ‚Üí Stage
next seed      = counter
next counter   = resonance
next resonance = overflow
next overflow  = seed

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tlurey traces
------------------------------------------------------------------------

StageTrace : Nat ‚Üí Stage ‚Üí List Stage
StageTrace zero    _ = []
StageTrace (suc n) s = s ‚à∑ StageTrace n (next s)

length : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Nat
length []       = zero
length (_ ‚à∑ xs) = suc (length xs)

_++_ : ‚àÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
[]       ++ ys = ys
(x ‚à∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚à∑ (xs ++ ys)

StageTrace-length : ‚àÄ n s ‚Üí length (StageTrace n s) ‚â° n
StageTrace-length zero    _ = refl
StageTrace-length (suc n) s = cong suc (StageTrace-length n (next s))

next‚Å¥ : ‚àÄ s ‚Üí spin 4 next s ‚â° s
next‚Å¥ seed      = refl
next‚Å¥ counter   = refl
next‚Å¥ resonance = refl
next‚Å¥ overflow  = refl

spin-next-succ : ‚àÄ n s ‚Üí spin n next (next s) ‚â° spin (suc n) next s
spin-next-succ zero    _ = refl
spin-next-succ (suc n) s = cong next (spin-next-succ n s)

StageTrace-periodic : ‚àÄ n s ‚Üí StageTrace (n + 4) s ‚â° StageTrace n s ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next s)
StageTrace-periodic zero    s = refl
StageTrace-periodic (suc n) s rewrite sym (spin-next-succ n s) =
  cong (s ‚à∑_) (StageTrace-periodic n (next s))

StageTrace-cycle : ‚àÄ n ‚Üí StageTrace (n + 4) seed ‚â° StageTrace n seed ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next seed)
StageTrace-cycle n = StageTrace-periodic n seed


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Semantics via triadic values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

stageTone : Stage ‚Üí TriTruth
stageTone seed      = tri-low
stageTone counter   = tri-mid
stageTone resonance = tri-high
stageTone overflow  = tri-low

combineStage : Stage ‚Üí Stage ‚Üí TriTruth
combineStage a b = triXor (stageTone a) (stageTone b)

stageTone-next-seed : stageTone (next seed) ‚â° rotateTri (stageTone seed)
stageTone-next-seed = refl

stageTone-next-counter : stageTone (next counter) ‚â° rotateTri (stageTone counter)
stageTone-next-counter = refl

stageTone-next-resonance : stageTone (next resonance) ‚â° rotateTri (stageTone resonance)
stageTone-next-resonance = refl

stageTone-next-overflow : stageTone (next overflow) ‚â° stageTone seed
stageTone-next-overflow = refl

resonance-combine : combineStage resonance resonance ‚â° tri-mid
resonance-combine = refl
module MonsterGroups where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚à∑_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Boundary predicate: ‚Äúthis state ends a group‚Äù.
-- You define it from the walk semantics (or from the trace table markers).

Boundary : Set
Boundary = State ‚Üí Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count groups in a trace given a boundary predicate.
-- Convention: group count starts at 0 for empty trace, else 1 + boundaries hit.

countGroups : Boundary ‚Üí List State ‚Üí Nat
countGroups b [] = 0
countGroups b (s ‚à∑ ss) = suc (go ss)
  where
    go : List State ‚Üí Nat
    go [] = 0
    go (t ‚à∑ ts) with b t
    ... | true  = suc (go ts)
    ... | false = go ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- You can similarly count ‚Äúpreserved digits‚Äù if your trace stores that.
-- For now keep it abstract until you add a field.
-- Agda: 10-Fold Way Bridges
module TenfoldBridges where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ñï)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_)
open import Data.Bool
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚â°_; refl; sym; _‚â¢_)

-- Topological class
topoClass : ‚Ñï ‚Üí ‚Ñï
topoClass n = n % 10

-- Bridge record
record Bridge : Set where
  field
    nodeA : ‚Ñï
    nodeB : ‚Ñï
    different : topoClass nodeA ‚â¢ topoClass nodeB

-- Symmetry
bridge-sym : (b : Bridge) ‚Üí Bridge
bridge-sym record { nodeA = a ; nodeB = b ; different = d } =
  record { nodeA = b ; nodeB = a ; different = Œª eq ‚Üí d (sym eq) }

-- Example: 232 ‚Üî 323
bridge-232-323 : Bridge
bridge-232-323 = record
  { nodeA = 232
  ; nodeB = 323
  ; different = Œª ()
  }

-- Theorem: Symmetry preserves bridges
bridge-symmetry : (b : Bridge) ‚Üí 
  Bridge.nodeA (bridge-sym b) ‚â° Bridge.nodeB b
bridge-symmetry b = refl
